# ГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђ

# ГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђГўвЂўВђ


# --- L1706-1878 (173 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_wizard_launch(event, client_id):
    """POST /ads/wizard/launch Гўв‚¬вЂќ Publica campana multi-canal (FB Ads + IG Ads + WhatsApp CTW).
    
    Reusa el endpoint existente /ads/campaigns/publish pero con los datos del wizard.
    
    Body: {
        "name": "Seminario 9mm - Mayo 2026",
        "image_urls": ["https://s3.../img1.jpg", "https://s3.../img2.jpg", "https://s3.../img3.jpg"],
        "copies": [{"text": "...", "angle": "..."}],
        "cta_text": "Reserva tu cupo",
        "strategy": "sell",
        "channels": ["facebook", "instagram", "whatsapp"],
        "budget_daily": 20000,
        "duration": 7,
        "service_slug": "seminario-tiro-pistola-9mm",
        "country": "CO",
        "cities": [],
        "age_min": 25,
        "age_max": 55,
        "gender": "all",
        "interests": []
    }
    """
    import time as _t
    
    try:
        body = json.loads(event.get("body", "{}") or "{}")
        name = (body.get("name") or f"Campana Wizard {int(_t.time())}").strip()
        image_urls = body.get("image_urls", []) or []
        # Bug #72: arrays paralelos opcionales para multi-formato Meta Advantage+
        image_urls_vertical = body.get("image_urls_vertical", []) or []
        image_urls_horizontal = body.get("image_urls_horizontal", []) or []
        # Bug #73: videos manuales (MP4/MOV subidos via /ads/video/upload-url)
        # Si una variant tiene video, prioriza sobre imagen (Meta acepta solo 1 tipo por ad)
        video_urls = body.get("video_urls", []) or []
        copies = body.get("copies", []) or []
        cta_text = (body.get("cta_text") or "").strip()
        strategy = (body.get("strategy") or "sell").strip()
        channels = body.get("channels", ["facebook", "instagram"]) or []
        budget_daily = max(5000, int(body.get("budget_daily", 15000)))
        duration = int(body.get("duration", 7))
        service_slug = (body.get("service_slug") or "").strip()
        country = (body.get("country") or "CO").strip()
        cities = body.get("cities", []) or []
        age_min = int(body.get("age_min", 18))
        age_max = int(body.get("age_max", 65))
        gender = (body.get("gender") or "all").strip()
        interests = body.get("interests", []) or []
        
        if not image_urls:
            return response(400, {"error": "image_urls requeridas (min 1 imagen final)"})
        if not copies:
            return response(400, {"error": "copies requeridos (min 1 variante de texto)"})
        
        # Construir variants Гўв‚¬вЂќ Bug #69: usa los 4 campos del copy (no hardcode)
        def _extract_copy_fields(copy):
            """Helper: extrae los 4 campos Meta del copy (con fallback retrocompat)."""
            if isinstance(copy, dict):
                return {
                    "headline": (copy.get("headline") or name)[:40],
                    "text": (copy.get("primary_text") or copy.get("text") or "")[:600],
                    "description": (copy.get("description") or cta_text or "")[:30],
                    "cta": copy.get("cta_button") or "MESSAGE_PAGE",
                }
            # Legacy: copy era string
            return {
                "headline": name[:40],
                "text": str(copy)[:600],
                "description": (cta_text or "")[:30],
                "cta": "MESSAGE_PAGE",
            }
        # Helper para resolver los 3 formatos por indice (con fallback al square)
        def _resolve_imgs(idx):
            sq = image_urls[idx] if idx < len(image_urls) else image_urls[0]
            ve = image_urls_vertical[idx] if idx < len(image_urls_vertical) else ""
            ho = image_urls_horizontal[idx] if idx < len(image_urls_horizontal) else ""
            return sq, ve, ho
        variants = []
        for i, copy in enumerate(copies[:len(image_urls)]):
            fields = _extract_copy_fields(copy)
            sq, ve, ho = _resolve_imgs(i)
            vid = video_urls[i] if i < len(video_urls) else ""
            variants.append({
                **fields,
                "image_url": sq,
                "image_vertical": ve,
                "image_horizontal": ho,
                "video_url": vid,          # Bug #73: si presente, ad sera video
            })
        # Si hay mas imagenes que copies, ciclar copies
        for i in range(len(variants), len(image_urls)):
            fields = _extract_copy_fields(copies[i % len(copies)])
            sq, ve, ho = _resolve_imgs(i)
            variants.append({
                **fields,
                "image_url": sq,
                "image_vertical": ve,
                "image_horizontal": ho,
            })
        
        # Determinar objetivo Meta segun estrategia
        objective_map = {
            "sell": "OUTCOME_ENGAGEMENT",
            "promote": "OUTCOME_AWARENESS",
            "lead_gen": "OUTCOME_ENGAGEMENT",
            "branding": "OUTCOME_AWARENESS",
        }
        objective = objective_map.get(strategy, "OUTCOME_ENGAGEMENT")
        
        # Construir el body que /ads/campaigns/publish espera
        publish_body = {
            "name": name,
            "objective": objective,
            "budget_daily": budget_daily,
            "variants": variants,
            "country": country,
            "city": "",
            "radius": "25",
            "duration": str(duration),
            "service_slug": service_slug,
            "age_min": age_min,
            "age_max": age_max,
            "gender": gender,
            "cities": cities,
            "interests": interests,
        }
        
        # Llamar al handler existente de publish (reutilizar codigo, no duplicar)
        # Construimos un event simulado con el body correcto
        publish_event = {
            "body": json.dumps(publish_body),
            "path": "/ads/campaigns/publish",
            "httpMethod": "POST",
            "headers": event.get("headers", {}),
            "queryStringParameters": event.get("queryStringParameters"),
        }
        
        # Importar el handler existente (esta en el mismo archivo)
        # Lo llamamos directamente pasando client_id
        try:
            # El handler de publish espera el body parseado internamente
            result = handle_ads_campaigns_publish(publish_event, client_id)
            
            # Enriquecer response con metadata del wizard
            if isinstance(result, dict) and result.get("statusCode") == 200:
                result_body = json.loads(result.get("body", "{}"))
                result_body["wizard_metadata"] = {
                    "strategy": strategy,
                    "channels": channels,
                    "variants_count": len(variants),
                    "images_count": len(image_urls),
                    "copies_count": len(copies),
                    "source": "wizard_2.0",
                }
                result["body"] = json.dumps(result_body)
            
            # Audit log
            try:
                audit_log(client_id, "user", "WIZARD_CAMPAIGN_LAUNCHED",
                          "ads_wizard",
                          f"name={name[:50]} strategy={strategy} variants={len(variants)} budget={budget_daily}")
            except Exception:
                pass
            
            logger.info(f"Wizard launch: company={client_id} name={name[:40]} "
                       f"variants={len(variants)} strategy={strategy}")
            return result
        except Exception as pub_err:
            logger.error(f"Wizard launch publish error: {pub_err}", exc_info=True)
            return response(500, {"error": f"Error publicando: {str(pub_err)[:200]}"})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/wizard/launch: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)[:200]})


# --- L2014-2284 (271 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_wizard_generate_copies(event, client_id):
    """POST /ads/wizard/generate-copies Гўв‚¬вЂќ Bug #69: 5 variantes COMPLETAS para Meta Ads.
    Cada variante incluye los 4 campos que Meta requiere:
      - headline (max 40 chars)
      - primary_text (400-600 chars con hook + valor + urgencia + CTA + precio)
      - description (max 30 chars)
      - cta_button (enum Meta valido)
    + metadata: pattern, angle, social_proof_used, char_count.
    Body: {
        "copy_angles": [...],           # del plan de generate-strategy
        "product_name": "...",
        "cta_text": "...",              # legacy, usado como hint si no llega cta_button
        "tone": "...",
        "language": "es|en|pt|fr",
        "benefits": [...],
        "use_brand_dna": true,
        "channel": "facebook|instagram", # opcional, varia limites
        "service_slug": ""              # opcional, enriquece prompt con precio/desc
    }
    """
    import urllib3 as _u3_cc
    import unicodedata
    try:
        body = json.loads(event.get("body", "{}") or "{}")
        copy_angles = body.get("copy_angles", []) or []
        product_name = (body.get("product_name") or "").strip()
        cta_text = (body.get("cta_text") or "Reserva ahora").strip()
        tone = (body.get("tone") or "profesional").strip()
        language = (body.get("language") or "es").strip()
        benefits = body.get("benefits", []) or []
        use_brand_dna = body.get("use_brand_dna", True)
        channel = (body.get("channel") or "facebook").strip().lower()
        service_slug = (body.get("service_slug") or "").strip()
        if not copy_angles:
            return response(400, {"error": "copy_angles requeridos (del plan de generate-strategy)"})
        gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
        if not gemini_key:
            return response(400, {"error": "GEMINI_API_KEY no configurada"})
        # === Cargar contexto enriquecido del tenant ===
        try:
            cfg = kb_table.get_item(
                Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}
            ).get("Item", {}) or {}
        except Exception:
            cfg = {}
        brand_name = cfg.get("brand_name", "el negocio")
        vertical = cfg.get("business_vertical", "")
        bp = cfg.get("business_profile", {}) or {}
        currency_label = bp.get("currency_label", cfg.get("currency", ""))
        cta_phrase = str(bp.get("cta_phrase", "")).strip()
        urgency_pool = bp.get("urgency_phrases", []) or []
        global_value_props = bp.get("global_value_props", bp.get("value_props", [])) or []
        location = str(bp.get("location", cfg.get("address", ""))).split("(")[0].strip()
        guarantees = str(bp.get("guarantees", "")).strip()
        # === Brand DNA ===
        social_proof_pool = []
        dna_block = ""
        if use_brand_dna:
            try:
                dna_table = dynamodb.Table("BrandDNA")
                dna_item = dna_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id}).get("Item")
                if dna_item and dna_item.get("dna"):
                    dna = dna_item["dna"]
                    social_proof_pool = dna.get("legal_social_proof", []) or []
                    dna_block = (
                        f"\nVoz de marca: {str(dna.get('voice', ''))[:200]}\n"
                        f"Audiencia: {str(dna.get('target_audience', {}).get('demographics', ''))[:200]}\n"
                        f"Dolores: {json.dumps(dna.get('target_audience', {}).get('pain_points', []), ensure_ascii=False)[:250]}\n"
                        f"Diferenciadores: {json.dumps(dna.get('key_differentiators', []), ensure_ascii=False)[:250]}\n"
                    )
            except Exception:
                pass
        # === Servicio (precio + descripcion) ===
        service_block = ""
        service_price = ""
        if service_slug:
            try:
                cat = kb_table.get_item(
                    Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "services_catalog"}
                ).get("Item", {}) or {}
                for s in (cat.get("services", []) or []):
                    if s.get("slug") == service_slug:
                        pricing = s.get("pricing", {}) or {}
                        reg = pricing.get("regular_price", 0)
                        if reg:
                            reg_int = int(reg)
                            service_price = f"${reg_int:,.0f}".replace(",", ".")
                        service_block = (
                            f"\n=== PRODUCTO ===\n"
                            f"Nombre: {s.get('name', product_name)}\n"
                            f"Descripcion: {str(s.get('description', ''))[:300]}\n"
                            f"Precio: {service_price} {currency_label}\n"
                            f"Caracteristicas: {json.dumps(s.get('characteristics', [])[:5], ensure_ascii=False)[:300]}\n"
                        )
                        if not product_name:
                            product_name = s.get("name", "")
                        if not benefits:
                            benefits = s.get("characteristics", [])[:5] or []
                        break
            except Exception:
                pass
        # === Limites Meta por canal ===
        if channel == "instagram":
            primary_min, primary_max = 400, 580
        else:
            primary_min, primary_max = 400, 600
        headline_max = 40
        description_max = 30
        # === Bloques contextuales ===
        bp_block = ""
        if bp:
            bp_lines = []
            if location:
                bp_lines.append(f"Ubicacion: {location}")
            if global_value_props:
                bp_lines.append(f"Value props: {json.dumps(global_value_props[:5], ensure_ascii=False)}")
            if urgency_pool:
                bp_lines.append(f"Frases urgencia disponibles: {json.dumps(urgency_pool[:5], ensure_ascii=False)}")
            if guarantees:
                bp_lines.append(f"Garantias: {guarantees}")
            if cta_phrase:
                bp_lines.append(f"CTA verbal: {cta_phrase}")
            if bp_lines:
                bp_block = "\n=== PERFIL DE MARCA ===\n" + "\n".join(bp_lines) + "\n"
        sp_block = ""
        if social_proof_pool:
            sp_block = ("\n=== SOCIAL PROOF LEGAL (usa 1 por variante) ===\n"
                        + "\n".join([f"- {sp}" for sp in social_proof_pool[:5]]))
        benefits_text = ", ".join(str(b) for b in benefits[:8]) if benefits else "no especificados"
        angles_text = "\n".join([f"{i+1}. {a}" for i, a in enumerate(copy_angles[:5])])
        lang_map = {"es": "espanol", "en": "ingles", "pt": "portugues", "fr": "frances"}
        lang_name = lang_map.get(language, "espanol")
        prompt = (
            f"Eres copywriter senior de Facebook/Instagram Ads con CTR alto.\n"
            f"Genera 5 variantes COMPLETAS de anuncio para '{product_name or brand_name}'"
            f"{' (' + vertical + ')' if vertical else ''}.\n"
            f"Cada variante con un ANGULO distinto.\n\n"
            f"TONO: {tone}\n"
            f"IDIOMA: {lang_name}\n"
            f"BENEFICIOS: {benefits_text}\n"
            f"CTA verbal sugerido: {cta_phrase or cta_text}\n"
            f"{bp_block}{sp_block}{service_block}{dna_block}\n"
            f"ANGULOS A USAR (1 distinto por variante):\n{angles_text}\n\n"
            f"REGLAS POR VARIANTE:\n"
            f"- headline: max {headline_max} chars, hook fuerte\n"
            f"- primary_text: ENTRE {primary_min} Y {primary_max} chars. "
            f"Estructura: hook (10-15 chars) + dolor/curiosidad + 2-3 value_props + "
            f"social_proof legal + urgencia + CTA explicito + precio si aplica\n"
            f"- description: max {description_max} chars, complementa headline\n"
            f"- cta_button: uno de [MESSAGE_PAGE, LEARN_MORE, SHOP_NOW, SIGN_UP, "
            f"CONTACT_US, GET_QUOTE, APPLY_NOW, BOOK_TRAVEL]\n"
            f"- Sin emojis al inicio (anti-spam Meta)\n"
            f"- Cumplir politicas Meta\n\n"
            f"Responde SOLO JSON valido con este schema:\n"
            "{\n"
            '  "copies": [\n'
            '    {\n'
            '      "headline": "...",\n'
            '      "primary_text": "...",\n'
            '      "description": "...",\n'
            '      "cta_button": "MESSAGE_PAGE",\n'
            '      "pattern": "escasez",\n'
            '      "angle": "...",\n'
            '      "social_proof_used": "...",\n'
            '      "char_count": 547\n'
            '    },\n'
            '    ... 5 variantes\n'
            "  ]\n"
            "}"
        )
        prompt_norm = "".join(
            ch for ch in unicodedata.normalize("NFD", prompt)
            if unicodedata.category(ch) != "Mn"
        )[:14000]
        response_schema = {
            "type": "object",
            "properties": {
                "copies": {
                    "type": "array",
                    "items": {
                        "type": "object",
                        "properties": {
                            "headline": {"type": "string"},
                            "primary_text": {"type": "string"},
                            "description": {"type": "string"},
                            "cta_button": {
                                "type": "string",
                                "enum": ["MESSAGE_PAGE", "LEARN_MORE", "SHOP_NOW",
                                        "SIGN_UP", "CONTACT_US", "GET_QUOTE",
                                        "APPLY_NOW", "BOOK_TRAVEL"]
                            },
                            "pattern": {"type": "string"},
                            "angle": {"type": "string"},
                            "social_proof_used": {"type": "string"},
                            "char_count": {"type": "integer"}
                        },
                        "required": ["headline", "primary_text", "description",
                                     "cta_button", "pattern", "angle"]
                    }
                }
            },
            "required": ["copies"]
        }
        payload = {
            "contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": prompt_norm}]}],
            "generationConfig": {
                "temperature": 0.85,
                "maxOutputTokens": 6000,
                "responseMimeType": "application/json",
                "responseSchema": response_schema,
                "thinkingConfig": {"thinkingBudget": 0}
            }
        }
        _hcc = _u3_cc.PoolManager()
        models = ["gemini-2.5-flash-lite", "gemini-flash-lite-latest"]
        last_err = ""
        for model in models:
            try:
                url = (f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/"
                       f"models/{model}:generateContent?key={gemini_key}")
                res = _hcc.request("POST", url, body=json.dumps(payload),
                                   headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"},
                                   timeout=25.0)
                if res.status != 200:
                    last_err = f"{model} status={res.status}"
                    logger.warning(f"generate-copies v2 {last_err}: {res.data.decode('utf-8')[:200]}")
                    continue
                data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
                text = (data.get("candidates", [{}])[0]
                        .get("content", {}).get("parts", [{}])[0]
                        .get("text", "")).strip()
                if text.startswith("```"):
                    text = text.split("\n", 1)[-1].rsplit("```", 1)[0].strip()
                parsed = json.loads(text)
                copies_raw = parsed.get("copies", [])
                if not copies_raw:
                    last_err = f"{model}: copies vacio"
                    continue
                # Clamp + normalizar
                clean = []
                for v in copies_raw[:5]:
                    pt = str(v.get("primary_text", ""))[:primary_max]
                    v["primary_text"] = pt
                    v["headline"] = str(v.get("headline", ""))[:headline_max]
                    v["description"] = str(v.get("description", ""))[:description_max]
                    v["char_count"] = len(pt)
                    if v.get("cta_button") not in ("MESSAGE_PAGE", "LEARN_MORE", "SHOP_NOW",
                                                    "SIGN_UP", "CONTACT_US", "GET_QUOTE",
                                                    "APPLY_NOW", "BOOK_TRAVEL"):
                        v["cta_button"] = "MESSAGE_PAGE"
                    clean.append(v)
                patterns = [v.get("pattern", "") for v in clean]
                logger.info(f"Wizard copies v2 OK: company={client_id} model={model} "
                            f"count={len(clean)} patterns={patterns}")
                return response(200, {
                    "ok": True,
                    "copies": clean,
                    "pattern_mix": "+".join(patterns),
                    "model": model,
                    "product_name": product_name,
                    "cta_text": cta_text,
                })
            except Exception as e:
                last_err = f"{model}: {str(e)[:200]}"
                logger.warning(f"generate-copies v2 error {last_err}")
                continue
        return response(500, {"error": f"Gemini fallo: {last_err}"})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/wizard/generate-copies: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)[:200]})



# --- L2285-2411 (127 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_wizard_generate_images_preview(event, client_id):
    """POST /ads/wizard/generate-images-preview - Genera 10 imagenes 512px (Bug #70 v3).
    Ahora carga refs REALES del BrandAssets agrupadas por tipo y las pasa como
    inlineData a Gemini. Persiste cada generacion para alimentar Hypothesis Engine.
    Body: {
        "image_prompts": [...],          # del plan de generate-strategy
        "service_slug": "...",           # NUEVO: contexto del servicio
        "brand_asset_urls": [...],       # LEGACY: solo si no hay BrandAssets registrados
        "intent": "ad_image",            # ad_image|product_shot|hero_shot|logo_only
        "language": "es",
        "country": "CO",
        "pattern_target": ""
    }
    """
    from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed
    import time as _t
    try:
        body = json.loads(event.get("body", "{}") or "{}")
        image_prompts = body.get("image_prompts", []) or []
        service_slug = (body.get("service_slug") or "").strip()
        intent = (body.get("intent") or "ad_image").strip().lower()
        language = (body.get("language") or "es").strip().lower()
        country = (body.get("country") or "CO").strip().upper()
        pattern_target = (body.get("pattern_target") or "").strip().lower()
        legacy_urls = body.get("brand_asset_urls", []) or []
        is_append = bool(body.get("append", False))
        if not image_prompts:
            return response(400, {"error": "image_prompts requeridos (del plan de generate-strategy)"})
        image_prompts = image_prompts[:10]
        gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
        if not gemini_key:
            return response(400, {"error": "GEMINI_API_KEY no configurada"})
        # Cuota
        quota_result = consume_wizard_quota(client_id)
        if not quota_result.get("consumed"):
            return response(429, {
                "error": "quota_exceeded",
                "message": quota_result.get("error", "Sin cuota disponible"),
                "is_append": is_append,
            })
        logger.info(f"wizard_quota consumed: company={client_id} "
                    f"source={quota_result.get('source')} append={is_append} "
                    f"prompts={len(image_prompts)}")
        # === Cargar contexto del tenant (Bug #70 v3) ===
        cfg = {}
        try:
            cfg = kb_table.get_item(
                Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}
            ).get("Item", {}) or {}
        except Exception:
            pass
        business_vertical = cfg.get("business_vertical", "")
        # === Cargar BrandAssets agrupados ===
        assets_by_type = get_brand_assets_by_type(client_id)
        # Seleccionar refs relevantes segun intent
        refs_full = select_relevant_refs(assets_by_type, intent=intent, max_refs=3)
        # Fallback: si tenant no tiene BrandAssets, usar URLs legacy del body
        if not refs_full and legacy_urls:
            for url in legacy_urls[:3]:
                ul = url.lower()
                if "/location/" in ul:
                    rtype = "location"
                elif "/team/" in ul:
                    rtype = "team"
                elif "/logo/" in ul:
                    rtype = "logo"
                elif "/product/" in ul:
                    rtype = "product"
                else:
                    rtype = "unknown"
                refs_full.append({"asset_id": "", "s3_url": url, "type": rtype})
        logger.info(f"refs seleccionadas: company={client_id} intent={intent} "
                    f"count={len(refs_full)} types={[r['type'] for r in refs_full]}")
        resolution = os.environ.get("IMAGE_RESOLUTION_PREVIEW", "512")
        thinking = os.environ.get("IMAGE_THINKING_PREVIEW", "minimal")
        # Generar en paralelo
        results = []
        start = _t.time()
        with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
            futures = {
                executor.submit(
                    _generate_single_image,
                    prompt=image_prompts[i],
                    client_id=client_id,
                    gemini_key=gemini_key,
                    resolution=resolution,
                    thinking_level=thinking,
                    index=i,
                    refs_full=refs_full,
                    service_slug=service_slug,
                    business_vertical=business_vertical,
                    language=language,
                    country=country,
                    pattern_target=pattern_target,
                    intent=intent,
                    asset_subtype="preview_512",
                ): i
                for i in range(len(image_prompts))
            }
            for future in as_completed(futures):
                try:
                    result = future.result()
                    results.append(result)
                except Exception as e:
                    idx = futures[future]
                    results.append({"ok": False, "index": idx, "error": str(e)[:200]})
        results.sort(key=lambda x: x.get("index", 0))
        elapsed = round(_t.time() - start, 1)
        total_ok = sum(1 for r in results if r.get("ok"))
        total_failed = len(results) - total_ok
        logger.info(f"Wizard images preview: company={client_id} "
                    f"ok={total_ok} failed={total_failed} elapsed={elapsed}s "
                    f"refs_used={len(refs_full)}")
        return response(200, {
            "ok": True,
            "images": results,
            "total_ok": total_ok,
            "total_failed": total_failed,
            "elapsed_seconds": elapsed,
            "resolution": resolution,
            "refs_used": len(refs_full),
            "refs_types": [r["type"] for r in refs_full],
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/wizard/generate-images-preview: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)[:200]})

def handle_wizard_generate_images_final(event, client_id):
    """POST /ads/wizard/generate-images-final - Re-genera 3 imagenes seleccionadas en 1K (Bug #70 v3).
    Body: {
        "image_prompts": [...],           # 3 prompts seleccionados
        "service_slug": "...",
        "brand_asset_urls": [...],        # LEGACY
        "intent": "ad_image",
        "language": "es",
        "country": "CO",
        "pattern_target": ""
    }
    """
    from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed
    import time as _t
    try:
        body = json.loads(event.get("body", "{}") or "{}")
        image_prompts = body.get("image_prompts", []) or []
        service_slug = (body.get("service_slug") or "").strip()
        intent = (body.get("intent") or "ad_image").strip().lower()
        language = (body.get("language") or "es").strip().lower()

        if not image_prompts:
            return response(400, {"error": "image_prompts requeridos (max 3 seleccionados)"})
        image_prompts = image_prompts[:3]

            return response(400, {"error": "GEMINI_API_KEY no configurada"})

            ).get("Item", {}) or {}
        except Exception:
            pass
        business_vertical = cfg.get("business_vertical", "")
        assets_by_type = get_brand_assets_by_type(client_id)
        refs_full = select_relevant_refs(assets_by_type, intent=intent, max_refs=3)
        if not refs_full and legacy_urls:
            for url in legacy_urls[:3]:

                    rtype = "location"

                    rtype = "team"
                elif "/logo/" in ul:
                    rtype = "logo"
                elif "/product/" in ul:
                    rtype = "product"
                else:
                    rtype = "unknown"
                refs_full.append({"asset_id": "", "s3_url": url, "type": rtype})

                    service_slug=service_slug,
                    business_vertical=business_vertical,
                    language=language,
                    country=country,
                    pattern_target=pattern_target,
                    intent=intent,
                    asset_subtype="final_1k",
                ): i
                for i in range(len(image_prompts))
            }
            for future in as_completed(futures):
                try:
                    results.append(future.result())
                except Exception as e:
                    results.append({"ok": False, "index": futures[future], "error": str(e)[:200]})
        results.sort(key=lambda x: x.get("index", 0))
        elapsed = round(_t.time() - start, 1)

            "quality": "high",
            "refs_used": len(refs_full),

        })
    except Exception as e:

        return response(500, {"error": str(e)[:200]})



# --- L2515-2729 (215 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_wizard_generate_strategy(event, client_id):
    """POST /ads/wizard/generate-strategy Гўв‚¬вЂќ Genera plan estructurado para la campana.
    
    Body: {
        "strategy": "sell|promote|lead_gen|branding",
        "channels": ["facebook", "instagram", "whatsapp"],
        "language": "es|en|pt|fr",
        "product_slug": "seminario-tiro-9mm",
        "benefits": ["Instructores certificados", "15 disparos incluidos"],
        "use_brand_dna": true
    }
    
    Retorna: {
        "plan": {
            "objective": "...",
            "target_summary": "...",
            "image_prompts": ["prompt1", "prompt2", ...],  // 10 prompts para generar imГѓВЎgenes
            "copy_angles": ["angle1", "angle2", ...],      // 5 ГѓВЎngulos para generar textos
            "cta_text": "...",
            "tone": "..."
        }
    }
    """
    import time as _t
    import urllib3 as _u3_ws
    import unicodedata
    
    try:
        body = json.loads(event.get("body", "{}") or "{}")
        strategy = (body.get("strategy") or "sell").strip().lower()
        channels = body.get("channels", ["facebook", "instagram"])
        language = (body.get("language") or "es").strip().lower()
        product_slug = (body.get("product_slug") or "").strip()
        benefits = body.get("benefits", []) or []
        use_brand_dna = body.get("use_brand_dna", True)
        
        # 1. (Wizard quota se descuenta en generate-images-preview, no aqui Гўв‚¬вЂќ strategy es solo texto barato)
        # 2. Cargar Brand DNA si existe y se pidio
        brand_dna_block = ""
        if use_brand_dna:
            try:
                dna_table = dynamodb.Table("BrandDNA")
                dna_item = dna_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id}).get("Item")
                if dna_item and dna_item.get("dna"):
                    dna = dna_item["dna"]
                    brand_dna_block = (
                        f"\n\n=== ADN DE LA MARCA (analizado por IA) ===\n"
                        f"Voz: {dna.get('voice', '')}\n"
                        f"Tono: {dna.get('tone', '')}\n"
                        f"Audiencia: {json.dumps(dna.get('target_audience', {}), ensure_ascii=False)[:500]}\n"
                        f"Propuestas de valor: {json.dumps(dna.get('value_propositions', []), ensure_ascii=False)[:300]}\n"
                        f"Social proof legal: {json.dumps(dna.get('legal_social_proof', []), ensure_ascii=False)[:300]}\n"
                        f"Diferenciadores: {json.dumps(dna.get('key_differentiators', []), ensure_ascii=False)[:300]}\n"
                    )
            except Exception:
                pass
        
        # 3. Cargar info del producto si hay slug
        product_block = ""
        if product_slug:
            try:
                svc_resp = kb_table.get_item(
                    Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": f"service_{product_slug}"}
                )
                svc = svc_resp.get("Item", {})
                if not svc:
                    # Buscar en catalogo
                    cat_resp = kb_table.get_item(
                        Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "services_catalog"}
                    )
                    for s in (cat_resp.get("Item", {}).get("services", []) or []):
                        if s.get("slug") == product_slug:
                            svc = s
                            break
                if svc:
                    product_block = (
                        f"\n\n=== PRODUCTO A PROMOCIONAR ===\n"
                        f"Nombre: {svc.get('name', product_slug)}\n"
                        f"Descripcion: {str(svc.get('description', ''))[:300]}\n"
                        f"Precio: {svc.get('pricing', {}).get('regular_price', 'N/A')} {svc.get('pricing', {}).get('currency', 'COP')}\n"
                        f"Caracteristicas: {json.dumps(svc.get('characteristics', []), ensure_ascii=False)[:300]}\n"
                    )
            except Exception:
                pass
        
        # 4. Cargar config del tenant
        try:
            cfg = kb_table.get_item(
                Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}
            ).get("Item", {})
            brand_name = cfg.get("brand_name", "Mi negocio")
            visual_desc = cfg.get("visual_description", "")
        except Exception:
            brand_name = "Mi negocio"
            visual_desc = ""
        
        benefits_text = "\n".join([f"- {b}" for b in benefits[:10]]) if benefits else "No especificados"
        
        strategy_map = {
            "sell": "VENDER Гўв‚¬вЂќ el objetivo es generar compras/reservas inmediatas",
            "promote": "PROMOCIONAR Гўв‚¬вЂќ dar a conocer el negocio/producto a nuevas audiencias",
            "lead_gen": "GENERAR LEADS Гўв‚¬вЂќ capturar datos de contacto de interesados",
            "branding": "BRANDING Гўв‚¬вЂќ posicionar la marca y generar recordacion",
        }
        strategy_desc = strategy_map.get(strategy, strategy_map["sell"])
        channels_text = ", ".join(channels) if channels else "Facebook, Instagram"
        
        lang_map = {"es": "espanol", "en": "ingles", "pt": "portugues", "fr": "frances"}
        lang_name = lang_map.get(language, "espanol")
        
        # 5. Construir prompt para Gemini
        visual_block = f"\nDescripcion visual del negocio: {visual_desc[:300]}" if visual_desc else ""
        
        prompt = (
            f"Eres un estratega de marketing digital experto en Meta Ads (Facebook + Instagram + WhatsApp).\n"
            f"Genera un plan de campana publicitaria para '{brand_name}'.\n\n"
            f"OBJETIVO: {strategy_desc}\n"
            f"CANALES: {channels_text}\n"
            f"IDIOMA de los textos: {lang_name}\n"
            f"BENEFICIOS del producto/servicio:\n{benefits_text}\n"
            f"{product_block}"
            f"{brand_dna_block}"
            f"{visual_block}\n\n"
            f"Genera un plan en JSON con esta estructura EXACTA:\n"
            "{\n"
            '  "objective": "resumen del objetivo en 1 linea",\n'
            '  "target_summary": "descripcion de la audiencia ideal en 2 lineas",\n'
            '  "image_prompts": [\n'
            '    "prompt detallado para imagen 1 (formula Andromeda: PERSONA + EMOCION + TENSION + CONTEXTO, fotorrealista, primer plano, iluminacion dramatica)",\n'
            '    "prompt 2 (diferente angulo emocional)",\n'
            '    "... hasta 10 prompts distintos"\n'
            '  ],\n'
            '  "copy_angles": [\n'
            '    "angulo persuasivo 1 (ej: escasez + urgencia)",\n'
            '    "angulo 2 (ej: prueba social)",\n'
            '    "angulo 3 (ej: beneficio directo)",\n'
            '    "angulo 4 (ej: dolor + solucion)",\n'
            '    "angulo 5 (ej: curiosidad)"\n'
            '  ],\n'
            '  "cta_text": "texto del boton CTA (ej: Reserva tu cupo, Compra ahora)",\n'
            '  "tone": "tono recomendado para los textos"\n'
            "}\n\n"
            "REGLAS para image_prompts:\n"
            "- Cada prompt debe describir una ESCENA con persona real mostrando EMOCION (adrenalina, sorpresa, satisfaccion, curiosidad)\n"
            "- NO generar imagenes de logos, flyers ni texto plano\n"
            "- Incluir detalles de iluminacion, angulo de camara, ambiente\n"
            "- Variar: primer plano facial, plano medio, accion, antes/despues emocional\n"
            f"- Contexto visual del negocio: {visual_desc[:200] if visual_desc else 'no especificado, usar contexto generico del producto'}\n"
            "- Generar EXACTAMENTE 10 prompts distintos\n"
        )
        
        # Normalizar acentos (Leccion 18)
        prompt_norm = "".join(
            c for c in unicodedata.normalize("NFD", prompt)
            if unicodedata.category(c) != "Mn"
        )[:12000]
        
        payload = {
            "contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": prompt_norm}]}],
            "generationConfig": {
                "temperature": 0.8,
                "maxOutputTokens": 3000,
                "responseMimeType": "application/json",
            },
        }
        
        gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
        if not gemini_key:
            return response(400, {"error": "GEMINI_API_KEY no configurada"})
        
        # Cascada modelos (Leccion 19)
        _hws = _u3_ws.PoolManager()
        models = ["gemini-2.5-flash-lite", "gemini-flash-lite-latest"]
        last_err = ""
        for model in models:
            try:
                url = (f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/"
                       f"models/{model}:generateContent?key={gemini_key}")
                res = _hws.request("POST", url,
                                   body=json.dumps(payload),
                                   headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"},
                                   timeout=30.0)
                if res.status != 200:
                    last_err = f"{model} status={res.status}"
                    continue
                data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
                text = (data.get("candidates", [{}])[0]
                        .get("content", {}).get("parts", [{}])[0]
                        .get("text", "")).strip()
                if text.startswith("```"):
                    text = text.split("\n", 1)[-1].rsplit("```", 1)[0].strip()
                plan = json.loads(text)
                
                # Validar estructura minima
                if not plan.get("image_prompts") or len(plan["image_prompts"]) < 3:
                    last_err = f"{model}: menos de 3 image_prompts"
                    continue
                
                logger.info(f"Wizard strategy OK: company={client_id} model={model} "
                           f"prompts={len(plan.get('image_prompts', []))} "
                           f"angles={len(plan.get('copy_angles', []))}")
                
                return response(200, {
                    "ok": True,
                    "plan": plan,
                    "model": model,
                })
            except Exception as e:
                last_err = f"{model}: {str(e)[:200]}"
                continue
        
        return response(500, {"error": f"Gemini fallo: {last_err}"})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/wizard/generate-strategy: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)[:200]})

# --- L11382-11403 (22 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def _b65_get_attribution_for_campaign(company_id: str, campaign_id: str,
                                       days: int = 7) -> dict:
    """Lee AdsAttribution para una campana especifica. Devuelve metricas crudas."""
    from boto3.dynamodb.conditions import Key, Attr
    import time as _t
    cutoff = int(_t.time()) - days * 86400
    try:
        ads_attr = dynamodb.Table("AdsAttribution")
        resp = ads_attr.query(
            IndexName="campaign-event-index",
            KeyConditionExpression=Key("campaign_id").eq(str(campaign_id)) & Key("created_at").gte(cutoff),
            FilterExpression=Attr("source_first").eq(True),  # solo first-touch (evita doble conteo)
        )
        items = resp.get("Items", [])
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning(f"B6.5 attribution query error: {e}")
        return {"leads": 0, "purchases": 0, "revenue_cents": 0}
    
    leads = sum(1 for i in items if i.get("event_type") == "lead")
    purchases = sum(1 for i in items if i.get("event_type") == "purchase")
    revenue = sum(int(i.get("amount_cents", 0) or 0) for i in items if i.get("event_type") == "purchase")
    return {"leads": leads, "purchases": purchases, "revenue_cents": revenue}


# --- L11404-11434 (31 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def _b65_create_recommendation(company_id: str, campaign_id: str, campaign_name: str,
                                ad_account_id: str, rec_type: str,
                                justification: dict, impact_cents: int,
                                confidence: int, suggested_action: dict) -> str:
    """Crea recomendacion en AdsRecommendations. Devuelve rec_id."""
    import time as _t
    import uuid
    now = int(_t.time())
    rec_id = f"{now}_{campaign_id}_{rec_type}_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:6]}"
    try:
        rec_tbl = dynamodb.Table("AdsRecommendations")
        rec_tbl.put_item(Item={
            "company_id": company_id,
            "rec_id": rec_id,
            "recommendation_type": rec_type,
            "campaign_id": str(campaign_id),
            "campaign_name": campaign_name or campaign_id,
            "ad_account_id": ad_account_id or "",
            "justification": justification,
            "impact_estimate_cents": int(impact_cents),
            "confidence": int(max(0, min(100, confidence))),
            "suggested_action": suggested_action,
            "status": "pending",
            "dismissed_count": 0,
            "created_at": now,
            "expires_at": now + 7 * 86400,  # TTL 7d
        })
        return rec_id
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"B6.5 create_recommendation error: {e}")
        return ""


# --- L11435-11455 (21 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def _b65_already_dismissed_recently(company_id: str, campaign_id: str,
                                      rec_type: str, days: int = 7) -> bool:
    """Si el cliente descarto 3 veces el mismo tipo en la misma campana,
    no volver a sugerir por N dias (regla B6.5.9)."""
    from boto3.dynamodb.conditions import Key, Attr
    import time as _t
    cutoff = int(_t.time()) - days * 86400
    try:
        rec_tbl = dynamodb.Table("AdsRecommendations")
        resp = rec_tbl.query(
            KeyConditionExpression=Key("company_id").eq(company_id),
            FilterExpression=(
                Attr("recommendation_type").eq(rec_type) &
                Attr("campaign_id").eq(str(campaign_id)) &
                Attr("created_at").gte(cutoff) &
                Attr("status").eq("dismissed")
            )
        )
        return len(resp.get("Items", [])) >= 3
    except Exception:
        return False  # no bloquear si query falla


# --- L11456-11623 (168 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def _b65_analyze_campaign(company_id: str, campaign: dict, ad_account_id: str,
                           ad_spend_cents: int) -> list:
    """Analiza una campana y devuelve lista de recomendaciones generadas.
    
    `campaign` debe traer metricas de Meta Insights:
      - id, name, status, daily_budget_cents
      - impressions, clicks, ctr, cpm_cents, cpc_cents, cpl_cents
      - clicks_7d, ctr_7d, ctr_prev_7d (ventana anterior)
      - impressions_24h, ctr_24h, cpl_24h, cpl_prev (24h vs 24h-anterior)
    """
    recs_created = []
    cid = str(campaign.get("id", ""))
    cname = campaign.get("name", cid)
    if not cid:
        return recs_created
    
    # Atribucion real (purchases + revenue del CRM, NO de Meta)
    attr = _b65_get_attribution_for_campaign(company_id, cid, days=7)
    purchases_7d = attr["purchases"]
    revenue_7d = attr["revenue_cents"]
    leads_7d = attr["leads"]
    
    # Calcular ROAS (Return on Ad Spend) real = revenue / spend
    roas = (revenue_7d / ad_spend_cents) if ad_spend_cents > 0 else 0
    
    cpl_now = int(campaign.get("cpl_cents", 0) or 0)
    cpl_prev = int(campaign.get("cpl_prev", 0) or 0)
    ctr_now = float(campaign.get("ctr", 0) or 0)
    ctr_prev = float(campaign.get("ctr_prev_7d", 0) or 0)
    cpm = int(campaign.get("cpm_cents", 0) or 0)
    impressions = int(campaign.get("impressions", 0) or 0)
    clicks = int(campaign.get("clicks", 0) or 0)
    daily_budget = int(campaign.get("daily_budget_cents", 0) or 0)
    
    def _create(rec_type, just, impact_cents=0, confidence=0, action=None):
        if _b65_already_dismissed_recently(company_id, cid, rec_type):
            logger.info(f"B6.5: skipping {rec_type} para {cid} (dismissed 3x recientes)")
            return
        rid = _b65_create_recommendation(
            company_id=company_id, campaign_id=cid, campaign_name=cname,
            ad_account_id=ad_account_id, rec_type=rec_type,
            justification=just, impact_cents=impact_cents, confidence=confidence,
            suggested_action=action or {},
        )
        if rid:
            recs_created.append(rid)
    
    # === REGLA 1: PAUSE Гўв‚¬вЂќ CPL sube +50% en 24h Y CTR cae ===
    if cpl_prev > 0 and cpl_now > 0:
        cpl_jump_pct = ((cpl_now - cpl_prev) / cpl_prev) * 100
        if cpl_jump_pct >= 50 and ctr_now < ctr_prev * 0.85 and impressions >= 1000:
            sample_quality = min(100, impressions // 100)
            _create(
                "pause",
                {
                    "cpl_now_cents": cpl_now, "cpl_prev_cents": cpl_prev,
                    "cpl_jump_pct": round(cpl_jump_pct, 1),
                    "ctr_now": ctr_now, "ctr_prev": ctr_prev,
                    "impressions": impressions,
                    "rule": "CPL +50% en 24h Y CTR cayo >15%",
                },
                impact_cents=daily_budget,  # ahorras 1 dia de budget al pausar
                confidence=min(95, 60 + int(cpl_jump_pct / 5) + sample_quality // 5),
                action={"pause": True, "reason": "ROI deteriorandose"},
            )
            return recs_created  # si pause, no generamos otras
    
    # === REGLA 2: SCALE Гўв‚¬вЂќ CPL bajo + ROAS > 2.5 + conversiones suben ===
    if purchases_7d >= 3 and ad_spend_cents > 0 and roas >= 2.5:
        # Solo si CPL no esta subiendo mucho
        cpl_stable = (cpl_prev == 0) or (cpl_now <= cpl_prev * 1.15)
        if cpl_stable:
            scale_pct = 25 if roas >= 4 else 15  # cap maximo 25%
            new_budget_cents = int(daily_budget * (1 + scale_pct / 100))
            estimated_extra_revenue = int(revenue_7d * (scale_pct / 100) * 0.7)  # 70% efficiency
            _create(
                "scale",
                {
                    "roas": round(roas, 2),
                    "purchases_7d": purchases_7d,
                    "revenue_7d_cents": revenue_7d,
                    "ad_spend_7d_cents": ad_spend_cents,
                    "cpl_now_cents": cpl_now,
                    "rule": f"ROAS {roas:.2f}x con CPL estable y {purchases_7d} ventas reales",
                },
                impact_cents=estimated_extra_revenue,
                confidence=min(90, 50 + int(roas * 10) + (purchases_7d * 2)),
                action={"new_daily_budget_cents": new_budget_cents, "scale_pct": scale_pct},
            )
    
    # === REGLA 3: REDUCE Гўв‚¬вЂќ sigue convirtiendo pero CPL sube gradualmente ===
    elif purchases_7d >= 1 and cpl_prev > 0 and cpl_now > cpl_prev * 1.20 and cpl_now < cpl_prev * 1.50:
        # CPL subio entre 20-50% (no es para pausar pero si bajar budget)
        cpl_creep_pct = ((cpl_now - cpl_prev) / cpl_prev) * 100
        reduce_pct = 20
        new_budget_cents = int(daily_budget * (1 - reduce_pct / 100))
        savings = int(daily_budget * (reduce_pct / 100) * 7)  # ahorro semanal
        _create(
            "reduce",
            {
                "cpl_now_cents": cpl_now, "cpl_prev_cents": cpl_prev,
                "cpl_creep_pct": round(cpl_creep_pct, 1),
                "purchases_7d": purchases_7d,
                "rule": f"CPL marginal sube {cpl_creep_pct:.0f}% pero sigue convirtiendo",
            },
            impact_cents=savings,
            confidence=70,
            action={"new_daily_budget_cents": new_budget_cents, "reduce_pct": reduce_pct},
        )
    
    # === REGLA 4: REFRESH_CREATIVE Гўв‚¬вЂќ CTR cae 30% en 7d (anuncio quemado) ===
    if ctr_prev > 0 and ctr_now > 0 and impressions >= 5000:
        ctr_drop_pct = ((ctr_prev - ctr_now) / ctr_prev) * 100
        if ctr_drop_pct >= 30:
            _create(
                "refresh_creative",
                {
                    "ctr_now": ctr_now, "ctr_prev": ctr_prev,
                    "ctr_drop_pct": round(ctr_drop_pct, 1),
                    "impressions": impressions,
                    "rule": f"CTR cayo {ctr_drop_pct:.0f}% en 7d - audiencia quemada del creativo",
                },
                impact_cents=int(daily_budget * 7 * 0.3),  # 30% del spend semanal recuperable
                confidence=min(85, 50 + int(ctr_drop_pct)),
                action={"refresh_creative": True, "suggestion": "Cambiar imagen + copy del anuncio"},
            )
    
    # === REGLA 5: CHANGE_TARGETING Гўв‚¬вЂќ CPM alto + CTR bajo (audiencia mala) ===
    # CPM alto = competencia alta o audiencia chica. CTR bajo = mensaje no conecta.
    if cpm >= 15000 and ctr_now < 1.0 and impressions >= 3000:  # CPM > $150 y CTR < 1%
        _create(
            "change_targeting",
            {
                "cpm_cents": cpm, "ctr_now": ctr_now,
                "impressions": impressions,
                "rule": "CPM alto + CTR bajo - audiencia saturada o mal segmentada",
            },
            impact_cents=int(daily_budget * 7 * 0.4),
            confidence=70,
            action={
                "change_targeting": True,
                "suggestion": "Probar audiencia lookalike de compradores reales",
            },
        )
    
    # === REGLA 6: RECHARGE_BUDGET Гўв‚¬вЂќ campana top con saldo bajo ===
    # (la calcula el cron a nivel ad_account, no campana - ver _b65_check_account_balance)
    
    # === REGLA 7: AB_TEST Гўв‚¬вЂќ campana ganadora estable, sugerir validar copy ===
    if purchases_7d >= 5 and roas >= 3 and ctr_now >= ctr_prev * 0.95:
        # Solo si nunca hemos sugerido AB test para esta campana en los ultimos 14d
        # (regla anti-spam built-in via dismissed_count)
        _create(
            "ab_test",
            {
                "purchases_7d": purchases_7d, "roas": round(roas, 2),
                "ctr_now": ctr_now, "stable": True,
                "rule": "Campana ganadora estable - es momento de validar copy alternativo",
            },
            impact_cents=int(revenue_7d * 0.15),  # 15% lift estimado del ganador A/B
            confidence=65,
            action={
                "ab_test": True,
                "suggestion": "Crear copy B con angulo diferente (precio vs beneficio vs urgencia)",
            },
        )
    
    return recs_created


# --- L11624-11665 (42 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def _b65_check_account_balance(company_id: str, ad_account_id: str,
                                access_token: str, daily_spend_cents: int) -> str:
    """Regla 6: si el saldo de la cuenta publicitaria alcanza para < 3 dias, recomendar recargar.
    Devuelve rec_id si genero recomendacion, "" si no.
    """
    if not ad_account_id or not access_token or daily_spend_cents <= 0:
        return ""
    try:
        # Meta API: GET /act_xxx?fields=balance,currency,amount_spent
        clean_id = ad_account_id.replace("act_", "")
        url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/act_{clean_id}?fields=balance,currency&access_token={access_token}"
        res = _http.request("GET", url, timeout=8.0)
        if res.status >= 300:
            return ""
        data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
        # balance viene en cents segun docs Meta
        balance_cents = int(data.get("balance", 0) or 0)
        days_left = (balance_cents / daily_spend_cents) if daily_spend_cents > 0 else 999
        if days_left < 3:
            # Crear recomendacion a nivel ad_account (campaign_id = "ACCOUNT_LEVEL")
            return _b65_create_recommendation(
                company_id=company_id,
                campaign_id="ACCOUNT_LEVEL",
                campaign_name=f"Cuenta publicitaria {ad_account_id}",
                ad_account_id=ad_account_id,
                rec_type="recharge_budget",
                justification={
                    "balance_cents": balance_cents,
                    "daily_spend_cents": daily_spend_cents,
                    "days_left": round(days_left, 1),
                    "rule": f"Saldo alcanza solo {days_left:.1f} dias",
                },
                impact_cents=daily_spend_cents * 7,  # 1 semana de campaГѓВ±as en riesgo
                confidence=95,
                suggested_action={
                    "recharge_budget": True,
                    "suggested_amount_cents": daily_spend_cents * 14,  # 2 semanas
                },
            )
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning(f"B6.5 balance check error: {e}")
    return ""


# --- L11912-12040 (129 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_attribution(client_id, qs):
    """GET /ads/attribution - M21: analytics de atribucion por campana.
    
    Query params:
      campaign_id: filtrar por campana especifica (opcional)
      days: ventana de tiempo en dias (default 30, max 365)
      event_type: 'lead' | 'purchase' | 'checkout' | 'schedule' (opcional)
    
    Returns metricas agregadas: leads, purchases, revenue, ROI, top_services.
    Sin scan: usa GSI campaign-event-index si hay campaign_id, si no PK directa.
    """
    import time as _time
    from boto3.dynamodb.conditions import Key, Attr
    
    days = min(int(qs.get("days", 30)), 365)
    campaign_filter = (qs.get("campaign_id") or "").strip()
    event_filter = (qs.get("event_type") or "").strip().lower()
    
    now = int(_time.time())
    cutoff = now - days * 86400
    
    ads_attr_tbl = dynamodb.Table("AdsAttribution")
    items = []
    
    try:
        if campaign_filter:
            # Query directo en GSI
            resp = ads_attr_tbl.query(
                IndexName="campaign-event-index",
                KeyConditionExpression=Key("campaign_id").eq(campaign_filter) & Key("created_at").gte(cutoff),
                FilterExpression=Attr("source_first").eq(True),  # evitar contar 2x last+first
            )
            items = resp.get("Items", [])
        else:
            # Query por PK del tenant
            resp = ads_attr_tbl.query(
                KeyConditionExpression=Key("company_id").eq(client_id),
                FilterExpression=(Attr("created_at").gte(cutoff) & Attr("source_first").eq(True)),
            )
            items = resp.get("Items", [])
            # Paginacion
            while "LastEvaluatedKey" in resp:
                resp = ads_attr_tbl.query(
                    KeyConditionExpression=Key("company_id").eq(client_id),
                    FilterExpression=(Attr("created_at").gte(cutoff) & Attr("source_first").eq(True)),
                    ExclusiveStartKey=resp["LastEvaluatedKey"],
                )
                items.extend(resp.get("Items", []))
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"M21 query error: {e}")
        return response(500, {"error": "no se pudo cargar atribucion"})
    
    if event_filter:
        items = [i for i in items if i.get("event_type") == event_filter]
    
    # Agregaciones
    by_campaign = {}  # campaign_id -> {leads, purchases, checkouts, revenue, services{}}
    total_leads = 0
    total_purchases = 0
    total_checkouts = 0
    total_revenue_cents = 0
    
    for it in items:
        cid = str(it.get("campaign_id", ""))
        etype = it.get("event_type", "")
        amount = int(it.get("amount_cents", 0) or 0)
        slug = it.get("service_slug", "") or ""
        
        if cid not in by_campaign:
            by_campaign[cid] = {
                "campaign_id": cid,
                "leads": 0, "purchases": 0, "checkouts": 0, "schedules": 0,
                "revenue_cents": 0, "services": {},
            }
        c = by_campaign[cid]
        if etype == "lead":
            c["leads"] += 1
            total_leads += 1
        elif etype == "purchase":
            c["purchases"] += 1
            c["revenue_cents"] += amount
            total_purchases += 1
            total_revenue_cents += amount
            if slug:
                c["services"][slug] = c["services"].get(slug, 0) + 1
        elif etype == "checkout":
            c["checkouts"] += 1
            total_checkouts += 1
        elif etype == "schedule":
            c["schedules"] += 1
    
    # Calcular conversion + AOV por campana
    campaigns = []
    for cid, c in by_campaign.items():
        conv_rate = (c["purchases"] / c["leads"] * 100) if c["leads"] else 0
        aov_cents = (c["revenue_cents"] / c["purchases"]) if c["purchases"] else 0
        # Top 3 servicios
        top_svc = sorted(c["services"].items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:3]
        campaigns.append({
            "campaign_id": cid,
            "leads": c["leads"],
            "checkouts": c["checkouts"],
            "purchases": c["purchases"],
            "schedules": c["schedules"],
            "revenue": c["revenue_cents"] / 100,
            "conv_rate_pct": round(conv_rate, 2),
            "aov": round(aov_cents / 100, 2),
            "top_services": [{"slug": s, "count": n} for s, n in top_svc],
        })
    # Ordenar por revenue desc
    campaigns.sort(key=lambda x: x["revenue"], reverse=True)
    
    overall_conv = (total_purchases / total_leads * 100) if total_leads else 0
    
    return response(200, {
        "company_id": client_id,
        "window_days": days,
        "filter_campaign": campaign_filter or None,
        "filter_event_type": event_filter or None,
        "totals": {
            "leads": total_leads,
            "checkouts": total_checkouts,
            "purchases": total_purchases,
            "revenue": total_revenue_cents / 100,
            "conv_rate_pct": round(overall_conv, 2),
        },
        "campaigns": campaigns,
        "campaigns_count": len(campaigns),
    })


# --- L14587-14615 (29 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_narrative(client_id, period="last_7d"):
    import urllib3 as _u3n
    _hn = _u3n.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(200, {"narrative": "Conecta Facebook Ads para ver tu resumen."})
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    brand = config.get("brand_name", "tu negocio")
    currency = config.get("currency", "COP")
    try:
        res = _hn.request("GET", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/insights?fields=spend,impressions,clicks,actions,reach,frequency&date_preset={period}&access_token={token}", timeout=15.0)
        if res.status != 200:
            return response(200, {"narrative": "Sin datos."})
        data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [{}])
        m = data[0] if data else {}
        spend = float(m.get("spend", 0))
        leads = sum(int(a.get("value", 0)) for a in m.get("actions", []) if a.get("action_type") in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d"))
        cpl = round(spend / leads, 0) if leads > 0 else 0
        reach = int(m.get("reach", 0))
        gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
        if gemini_key and spend > 0:
            prompt = f"Resumen ejecutivo breve (3 lineas) de publicidad de {brand} ({currency}). Gasto ${spend:,.0f}, {leads} leads, CPL ${cpl:,.0f}, Alcance {reach:,}. Habla como asesor. Se directo."
            ai_res = _hn.request("POST", f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:generateContent?key={gemini_key}", body=json.dumps({"contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": prompt}]}], "generationConfig": {"temperature": 0.5, "maxOutputTokens": 800}}), headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"}, timeout=20.0)
            if ai_res.status == 200:
                narrative = json.loads(ai_res.data.decode("utf-8"))["candidates"][0]["content"]["parts"][0]["text"].strip()
                return response(200, {"narrative": narrative, "metrics": {"spend": spend, "leads": leads, "cpl": cpl, "reach": reach}})
        return response(200, {"narrative": f"Invertiste ${spend:,.0f}, conseguiste {leads} leads a ${cpl:,.0f} cada uno.", "metrics": {"spend": spend, "leads": leads, "cpl": cpl, "reach": reach}})
    except Exception:
        return response(200, {"narrative": "No se pudo generar el resumen."})


# --- L14616-14634 (19 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_geo_breakdown(client_id, period="last_30d"):
    import urllib3 as _u3gb
    _hgb = _u3gb.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(200, {"regions": []})
    try:
        res = _hgb.request("GET", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/insights?fields=spend,impressions,actions&breakdowns=region&date_preset={period}&limit=20&access_token={token}", timeout=15.0)
        if res.status == 200:
            data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
            regions = []
            for d in data:
                leads = sum(int(a.get("value", 0)) for a in d.get("actions", []) if a.get("action_type") in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d"))
                regions.append({"region": d.get("region", ""), "spend": float(d.get("spend", 0)), "leads": leads})
            regions.sort(key=lambda x: x["leads"], reverse=True)
            return response(200, {"regions": regions[:15]})
    except Exception:
        pass
    return response(200, {"regions": []})

def handle_ads_save_rules(client_id, body):
    rules = {"max_cpl": int(body.get("max_cpl", 0)), "max_spend_daily": int(body.get("max_spend_daily", 0)), "pause_if_no_leads_hours": int(body.get("pause_if_no_leads_hours", 72)), "auto_scale_if_cpl_below": int(body.get("auto_scale_if_cpl_below", 0))}
    kb_table.update_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}, UpdateExpression="SET ads_rules = :r", ExpressionAttributeValues={":r": rules})
    return response(200, {"message": "Reglas guardadas", "rules": rules})


# --- L14642-14656 (15 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_check_landing(client_id, body):
    import urllib3 as _u3cl2
    _hcl2 = _u3cl2.PoolManager()
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    phone = (config.get("phone_display", "") or "").replace("+", "").replace(" ", "")
    checks = [{"check": "Numero WhatsApp", "ok": bool(phone), "detail": phone or "No configurado"}]
    if phone:
        try:
            res = _hcl2.request("GET", f"https://wa.me/{phone}", timeout=10.0, redirect=False)
            checks.append({"check": "Link wa.me", "ok": res.status < 400, "detail": f"HTTP {res.status}"})
        except Exception:
            checks.append({"check": "Link wa.me", "ok": False, "detail": "Error"})
    checks.append({"check": "Bot con prompt", "ok": bool(config.get("prompt")), "detail": "Activo" if config.get("prompt") else "Sin prompt"})
    checks.append({"check": "Pasarela de pago", "ok": bool(config.get("gateway_name")), "detail": config.get("gateway_name", "No configurada")})
    return response(200, {"checks": checks, "all_ok": all(c["ok"] for c in checks)})


# --- L14657-14661 (5 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_report(client_id, period="last_30d"):
    dash = json.loads(handle_ads_dashboard(client_id, period).get("body", "{}"))
    narr = json.loads(handle_ads_narrative(client_id, period).get("body", "{}"))
    geo = json.loads(handle_ads_geo_breakdown(client_id, period).get("body", "{}"))
    return response(200, {**dash, "narrative": narr.get("narrative", ""), "geo_regions": geo.get("regions", []), "report_date": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M"), "period": period})
