# --- L14674-14677 (4 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_set_cpa_target(client_id, body):
    cpa = int(body.get("cpa_target", 0))
    kb_table.update_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}, UpdateExpression="SET ads_cpa_target = :c", ExpressionAttributeValues={":c": cpa})
    return response(200, {"message": "CPA objetivo guardado", "cpa_target": cpa})


# --- L14678-14693 (16 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_errors(client_id):
    import urllib3 as _u3e
    _he = _u3e.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(200, {"errors": []})
    try:
        res = _he.request("GET", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/campaigns?fields=id,name,effective_status&limit=20&access_token={token}", timeout=15.0)
        errors = []
        if res.status == 200:
            for c in json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", []):
                if c.get("effective_status") in ("WITH_ISSUES", "DISAPPROVED"):
                    errors.append({"campaign_id": c.get("id", ""), "name": c.get("name", ""), "status": c.get("effective_status", "")})
        return response(200, {"errors": errors, "count": len(errors)})
    except Exception:
        return response(200, {"errors": []})


# --- L14694-14730 (37 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_search_targeting(client_id, query, target_type="city"):
    """GET /ads/search-targeting?q=medellin&type=city Гўв‚¬вЂќ Busca opciones de targeting en Meta."""
    import urllib3 as _u3st
    _hst = _u3st.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(400, {"error": error})
    if not query or len(query) < 2:
        return response(200, {"results": []})
    type_map = {"city": "adgeolocation", "interest": "adinterest", "behavior": "adbehavior", "region": "adgeolocation"}
    search_type = type_map.get(target_type, "adgeolocation")
    location_types = ""
    if target_type == "city":
        location_types = "&location_types=city"
    elif target_type == "region":
        location_types = "&location_types=region"
    try:
        url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/search?type={search_type}&q={query}{location_types}&limit=15&access_token={token}"
        res = _hst.request("GET", url, timeout=10.0)
        if res.status == 200:
            data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
            results = []
            for item in data.get("data", []):
                r = {"key": item.get("key", ""), "name": item.get("name", "")}
                if target_type in ("city", "region"):
                    r["country_name"] = item.get("country_name", "")
                    r["region"] = item.get("region", "")
                    r["type"] = item.get("type", target_type)
                elif target_type == "interest":
                    r["audience_size"] = item.get("audience_size", 0)
                    r["path"] = item.get("path", [])
                    r["id"] = item.get("id", "")
                results.append(r)
            return response(200, {"results": results, "query": query, "type": target_type})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error search targeting: {e}")
    return response(200, {"results": []})


# --- L14731-15062 (332 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_analyze(client_id, body):
    """POST /ads/analyze v2 Гўв‚¬вЂќ Analisis hibrido mejorado: reglas + ROAS real + comparativa + IA.
    
    Mejoras v2:
    - ROAS real cruzando AdsAttribution + StudentPaymentState
    - Comparativa 7d vs 7d anteriores (Meta API time_range)
    - Diagnostico funnel completo: impresionesГўвЂ вЂ™clicksГўвЂ вЂ™leadsГўвЂ вЂ™ventas
    - Prompt Gemini con datos reales de ventas
    """
    import urllib3 as _u3an
    from datetime import datetime, timedelta
    _han = _u3an.PoolManager()
    campaign_id = body.get("campaign_id", "")
    if not campaign_id:
        return response(400, {"error": "campaign_id es requerido"})
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(400, {"error": error})
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    brand = config.get("brand_name", "Negocio")
    currency = config.get("currency", "COP")
    try:
        # 1. Metricas 7d actuales
        ci_res = _han.request("GET",
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{campaign_id}/insights"
            f"?fields=spend,impressions,clicks,ctr,cpc,actions,reach,frequency,cpm"
            f"&date_preset=last_7d&access_token={token}",
            timeout=15.0)
        metrics = {}
        leads = 0
        if ci_res.status == 200:
            ci_data = json.loads(ci_res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
            if ci_data:
                metrics = ci_data[0]
                for a in metrics.get("actions", []):
                    if a.get("action_type") in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d"):
                        leads += int(a.get("value", 0))
        spend = float(metrics.get("spend", 0))
        impressions = int(metrics.get("impressions", 0))
        clicks = int(metrics.get("clicks", 0))
        ctr = round(float(metrics.get("ctr", 0)), 2)
        frequency = round(float(metrics.get("frequency", 0)), 1)
        reach = int(metrics.get("reach", 0))
        cpm = round(float(metrics.get("cpm", 0)), 2)
        cpl = round(spend / leads, 0) if leads > 0 else 0

        # 2. Metricas 7d ANTERIORES (comparativa)
        today = datetime.utcnow().date()
        prev_end = today - timedelta(days=8)
        prev_start = today - timedelta(days=15)
        prev_res = _han.request("GET",
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{campaign_id}/insights"
            f"?fields=spend,impressions,clicks,ctr,actions,frequency"
            f"&time_range=%7B%22since%22%3A%22{prev_start}%22%2C%22until%22%3A%22{prev_end}%22%7D"
            f"&access_token={token}",
            timeout=12.0)
        prev_spend = 0.0
        prev_leads = 0
        prev_ctr = 0.0
        prev_frequency = 0.0
        if prev_res.status == 200:
            prev_data = json.loads(prev_res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
            if prev_data:
                pm = prev_data[0]
                prev_spend = float(pm.get("spend", 0))
                prev_ctr = round(float(pm.get("ctr", 0)), 2)
                prev_frequency = round(float(pm.get("frequency", 0)), 1)
                for a in pm.get("actions", []):
                    if a.get("action_type") in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d"):
                        prev_leads += int(a.get("value", 0))
        prev_cpl = round(prev_spend / prev_leads, 0) if prev_leads > 0 else 0

        # Tendencias
        lead_trend = "sube" if leads > prev_leads else ("baja" if leads < prev_leads else "igual")
        ctr_trend = "sube" if ctr > prev_ctr * 1.05 else ("baja" if ctr < prev_ctr * 0.95 else "estable")
        cpl_trend = "baja" if prev_cpl > 0 and cpl < prev_cpl * 0.95 else ("sube" if prev_cpl > 0 and cpl > prev_cpl * 1.05 else "estable")

        # 3. ROAS REAL desde AdsAttribution + StudentPaymentState
        roas = 0.0
        real_purchases = 0
        real_revenue = 0
        attribution_note = "Sin datos de atribucion"
        try:
            # FIX: usar funcion correcta _b65_get_attribution_for_campaign
            # devuelve {"leads", "purchases", "revenue_cents"} (NO purchases_7d/revenue_7d)
            attr = _b65_get_attribution_for_campaign(client_id, campaign_id, days=7)
            spend_cents = int(spend * 100)
            if attr and spend_cents > 0:
                real_purchases = int(attr.get("purchases", 0))
                real_revenue_cents = int(attr.get("revenue_cents", 0))
                real_revenue = real_revenue_cents / 100
                roas = round(real_revenue_cents / spend_cents, 2) if spend_cents > 0 else 0
                if real_purchases > 0:
                    attribution_note = f"{real_purchases} ventas reales atribuidas Гўв‚¬вЂќ ROAS {roas:.1f}x"
                else:
                    attribution_note = "Campana conectada al bot pero sin ventas atribuidas aun"
            else:
                attribution_note = "Campana no conectada al bot o sin datos de atribucion"
        except Exception as _ae:
            logger.warning(f"Error attribution analyze: {_ae}", exc_info=True)

        # 4. Metricas por anuncio
        ads_res = _han.request("GET",
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{campaign_id}/ads"
            f"?fields=id,name,effective_status&limit=20&access_token={token}",
            timeout=10.0)
        ads_data = []
        if ads_res.status == 200:
            for ad in json.loads(ads_res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", []):
                ad_m = {}
                ad_leads = 0
                try:
                    amr = _han.request("GET",
                        f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad['id']}/insights"
                        f"?fields=spend,impressions,clicks,ctr,actions,frequency"
                        f"&date_preset=last_7d&access_token={token}",
                        timeout=8.0)
                    if amr.status == 200:
                        amd = json.loads(amr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
                        if amd:
                            ad_m = amd[0]
                            for a in ad_m.get("actions", []):
                                if a.get("action_type") in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d"):
                                    ad_leads += int(a.get("value", 0))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                ads_data.append({
                    "id": ad.get("id", ""),
                    "name": ad.get("name", ""),
                    "status": ad.get("effective_status", ""),
                    "spend": float(ad_m.get("spend", 0)),
                    "impressions": int(ad_m.get("impressions", 0)),
                    "clicks": int(ad_m.get("clicks", 0)),
                    "ctr": round(float(ad_m.get("ctr", 0)), 2),
                    "frequency": round(float(ad_m.get("frequency", 0)), 1),
                    "leads": ad_leads,
                })

        # 5. DIAGNOSTICO DEL FUNNEL (impresiones ГўвЂ вЂ™ clicks ГўвЂ вЂ™ leads ГўвЂ вЂ™ ventas)
        funnel_diagnosis = ""
        conversion_rate_to_lead = round((leads / clicks * 100), 1) if clicks > 0 else 0
        conversion_rate_to_sale = round((real_purchases / leads * 100), 1) if leads > 0 and real_purchases > 0 else 0

        if impressions < 500:
            funnel_diagnosis = "Aun no hay suficientes datos. Espera al menos 48 horas para un analisis confiable."
        elif impressions > 1000 and ctr < 0.8:
            funnel_diagnosis = f"El anuncio no llama la atencion: solo {ctr}% hace click. El problema es el creativo o el texto Гўв‚¬вЂќ no conecta con la audiencia. Renueva imagen y copy."
        elif clicks > 0 and leads == 0 and ctr > 1.0:
            funnel_diagnosis = f"El anuncio atrae clicks ({ctr}% CTR) pero nadie escribe. El problema esta en el CTA o la oferta. Prueba un mensaje mas directo o una promesa mas clara."
        elif leads > 0 and real_purchases == 0 and roas == 0:
            funnel_diagnosis = f"Generas leads (${cpl:,.0f} cada uno) pero no hay ventas atribuidas al bot. Si las ventas ocurren por fuera del bot, usa el boton Reportar a Meta en el CRM."
        elif leads > 0 and real_purchases > 0:
            funnel_diagnosis = (
                f"Funnel completo: {impressions:,} impresiones ГўвЂ вЂ™ {clicks:,} clicks ({ctr}% CTR) ГўвЂ вЂ™ "
                f"{leads} leads (${cpl:,.0f} CPL) ГўвЂ вЂ™ {real_purchases} ventas (ROAS {roas:.1f}x). "
                f"Conversion lead-a-venta: {conversion_rate_to_sale}%."
            )
        elif frequency > 2.5:
            funnel_diagnosis = f"Frecuencia alta ({frequency}x): tu audiencia ya vio el anuncio muchas veces. Los creativos se queman. Renueva imagenes y textos."
        else:
            funnel_diagnosis = f"Campana activa con {leads} leads en 7 dias. CTR {ctr}%, frecuencia {frequency}x."

        # 6. REGLAS DE OPTIMIZACION
        recommendations = []

        # Anuncio peor vs mejor
        if len(ads_data) >= 2:
            sorted_ads = sorted(ads_data, key=lambda x: x["leads"], reverse=True)
            best = sorted_ads[0]
            worst = sorted_ads[-1]
            if best["leads"] > 0 and worst["leads"] == 0 and worst["spend"] > 5:
                recommendations.append({
                    "action": "pausar", "target": worst["name"], "target_id": worst["id"],
                    "reason": f"PAUSAR '{worst['name']}': ${worst['spend']:,.0f} gastados sin un solo lead. '{best['name']}' tiene {best['leads']} leads. Concentra el presupuesto en lo que funciona.",
                    "confidence": "alta"
                })
            if best["leads"] >= 3 and best["spend"] > 0:
                best_cpl = round(best["spend"] / best["leads"], 0)
                recommendations.append({
                    "action": "escalar", "target": best["name"], "target_id": best["id"],
                    "reason": f"ESCALAR '{best['name']}' +20%: mejor anuncio con {best['leads']} leads a ${best_cpl:,.0f} cada uno. ROAS actual {roas:.1f}x Гўв‚¬вЂќ escalar ahora maximiza el retorno.",
                    "confidence": "alta"
                })

        # CPL subiendo vs semana anterior
        if prev_cpl > 0 and cpl > 0 and cpl > prev_cpl * 1.3:
            pct = round((cpl - prev_cpl) / prev_cpl * 100)
            recommendations.append({
                "action": "revisar", "target": "campana", "target_id": campaign_id,
                "reason": f"ATENCION: el costo por lead subio {pct}% vs la semana pasada (${prev_cpl:,.0f} ГўвЂ вЂ™ ${cpl:,.0f}). Revisa si la audiencia se esta saturando o si hay mas competencia en el mercado.",
                "confidence": "media"
            })

        # Frecuencia alta
        if frequency > 2.5:
            recommendations.append({
                "action": "renovar_creativos", "target": "campana", "target_id": campaign_id,
                "reason": f"RENOVAR creativos: frecuencia {frequency}x (era {prev_frequency}x la semana pasada). Tu audiencia ya vio el anuncio demasiadas veces Гўв‚¬вЂќ el CTR caera pronto. Cambia imagenes y copy.",
                "confidence": "alta"
            })

        # Gasto sin resultados
        if spend > 15 and leads == 0 and impressions > 1000:
            recommendations.append({
                "action": "pausar", "target": "campana", "target_id": campaign_id,
                "reason": f"PAUSAR: ${spend:,.0f} gastados y cero leads. Antes de reactivar cambia el creativo, el copy o el publico objetivo.",
                "confidence": "alta"
            })

        # ROAS excelente Гўв‚¬вЂќ sugerir AB test
        if roas >= 3 and real_purchases >= 3:
            recommendations.append({
                "action": "ab_test", "target": "campana", "target_id": campaign_id,
                "reason": f"ROAS {roas:.1f}x con {real_purchases} ventas reales Гўв‚¬вЂќ campana ganadora. Momento ideal para crear una variante B con copy diferente (precio vs beneficio vs urgencia) y multiplicar resultados.",
                "confidence": "media"
            })

        # CPM alto + CTR bajo = audiencia mala
        if cpm > 15 and ctr < 1.0 and impressions >= 3000:
            recommendations.append({
                "action": "cambiar_audiencia", "target": "campana", "target_id": campaign_id,
                "reason": f"CPM alto (${cpm:.0f}) y CTR bajo ({ctr}%): estas pagando caro por una audiencia que no reacciona. Prueba una audiencia lookalike basada en tus compradores reales.",
                "confidence": "media"
            })

        # 7. GEMINI con datos reales de ventas
        ai_insight = ""
        gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
        if gemini_key and spend > 0:
            try:
                ads_summary = ", ".join([
                    f"{a['name']}: ${a['spend']:,.0f} gastados, {a['leads']} leads, CTR {a['ctr']}%, frecuencia {a['frequency']}x"
                    for a in ads_data
                ])
                comparativa = ""
                if prev_spend > 0:
                    comparativa = (
                        f"Semana anterior: ${prev_spend:,.0f} gastados, {prev_leads} leads, "
                        f"CPL ${prev_cpl:,.0f}, CTR {prev_ctr}%. "
                        f"Tendencia leads: {lead_trend}. Tendencia CTR: {ctr_trend}. Tendencia CPL: {cpl_trend}."
                    )
                ventas_reales = ""
                if real_purchases > 0:
                    ventas_reales = f"Ventas reales atribuidas al bot esta semana: {real_purchases} ventas por ${real_revenue:,.0f} {currency} total. ROAS real: {roas:.1f}x."
                else:
                    ventas_reales = "No hay ventas atribuidas directamente a esta campana en el bot esta semana."

                prompt = (
                    f"Eres el asesor de publicidad digital de {brand}. Analiza estos datos con criterio experto.\n\n"
                    f"CAMPANA ESTA SEMANA (7 dias):\n"
                    f"Gasto: ${spend:,.0f} {currency} | Impresiones: {impressions:,} | Clicks: {clicks:,} | CTR: {ctr}% | Frecuencia: {frequency}x\n"
                    f"Leads: {leads} | CPL: ${cpl:,.0f} | CPM: ${cpm:.0f}\n"
                    f"{ventas_reales}\n\n"
                    f"COMPARATIVA VS SEMANA ANTERIOR:\n"
                    f"{comparativa if comparativa else 'Sin datos de semana anterior.'}\n\n"
                    f"ANUNCIOS:\n"
                    f"{ads_summary}\n\n"
                    f"DIAGNOSTICO AUTOMATICO:\n"
                    f"{funnel_diagnosis}\n\n"
                    f"Dame tu analisis en 3 partes:\n"
                    f"1) QUE ESTA FUNCIONANDO BIEN (si hay algo positivo)\n"
                    f"2) EL PROBLEMA PRINCIPAL (identifica el cuello de botella del funnel)\n"
                    f"3) LA ACCION CONCRETA que debe tomar el dueno del negocio HOY\n\n"
                    f"Habla directo, sin rodeos, como si fuera dinero tuyo. "
                    f"NO uses markdown, asteriscos, hashtags ni formato especial. Solo texto plano con saltos de linea."
                )
                # Cascada de modelos (Leccion 19: nunca depender de uno solo)
                # thinkingBudget=0 desactiva pensamiento interno -> libera todos los tokens para texto
                _models_an = ["gemini-2.5-flash", "gemini-2.5-flash-lite", "gemini-flash-lite-latest"]
                _payload_an = {
                    "contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": prompt}]}],
                    "generationConfig": {
                        "temperature": 0.6,
                        "maxOutputTokens": 4096,
                        "thinkingConfig": {"thinkingBudget": 0},
                    },
                }
                for _model_an in _models_an:
                    try:
                        _url_an = (f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/"
                                   f"models/{_model_an}:generateContent?key={gemini_key}")
                        ai_res = _han.request("POST", _url_an,
                                              body=json.dumps(_payload_an),
                                              headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"},
                                              timeout=40.0)
                        if ai_res.status != 200:
                            logger.warning(f"Gemini analyze {_model_an} status={ai_res.status}")
                            continue
                        ai_data = json.loads(ai_res.data.decode("utf-8"))
                        _fin = ai_data.get("candidates", [{}])[0].get("finishReason", "UNKNOWN")
                        logger.info(f"Gemini analyze model={_model_an} finish_reason={_fin}")
                        _txt = (ai_data.get("candidates", [{}])[0]
                                .get("content", {}).get("parts", [{}])[0]
                                .get("text", "")).strip()
                        # Aceptar texto parcial si finishReason=MAX_TOKENS (mejor algo que nada)
                        if _txt:
                            ai_insight = _txt
                            if _fin == "MAX_TOKENS":
                                ai_insight += "\n\n[Analisis recortado por limite del modelo]"
                            break
                        # Si llego texto vacio probar siguiente modelo
                        logger.warning(f"Gemini analyze {_model_an} texto vacio finish={_fin}")
                    except Exception as _ge_inner:
                        logger.warning(f"Gemini analyze {_model_an} error: {_ge_inner}")
                        continue
            except Exception as _ge:
                logger.warning(f"Gemini analyze error: {_ge}")

        return response(200, {
            "campaign_id": campaign_id,
            "metrics": {
                "spend": spend, "impressions": impressions, "reach": reach,
                "clicks": clicks, "ctr": ctr, "leads": leads, "cpl": cpl,
                "frequency": frequency, "cpm": cpm,
                "roas": roas, "real_purchases": real_purchases, "real_revenue": real_revenue,
            },
            "comparison": {
                "prev_spend": prev_spend, "prev_leads": prev_leads,
                "prev_cpl": prev_cpl, "prev_ctr": prev_ctr,
                "lead_trend": lead_trend, "ctr_trend": ctr_trend, "cpl_trend": cpl_trend,
            },
            "attribution": {"note": attribution_note, "purchases": real_purchases, "revenue": real_revenue, "roas": roas},
            "ads": ads_data,
            "recommendations": recommendations,
            "funnel_diagnosis": funnel_diagnosis,
            "ai_insight": ai_insight,
            "best_ad": max(ads_data, key=lambda x: x["leads"])["name"] if ads_data else "",
            "worst_ad": min(ads_data, key=lambda x: x["leads"])["name"] if ads_data and len(ads_data) > 1 else "",
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error analyze v2: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L15063-15143 (81 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_apply_action(client_id, body):
    """POST /ads/apply-action - Ejecuta una recomendacion de la IA.
    Acciones implementadas con Meta Graph API:
      - pausar:    pausa el ad/campana (PAUSED)
      - escalar:   sube presupuesto +20% (cap +30%)
      - reducir:   baja presupuesto -20%
      - activar:   reactiva (ACTIVE)
      - recargar:  no aplica via API (saldo se carga manual desde Meta Billing)
    Acciones que requieren UI o accion manual (devuelven 200 con instruccion):
      - ab_test:           sugerencia para Wizard de variantes (cliente decide)
      - refresh_creative:  cliente debe entrar al editor del ad
      - change_targeting:  cliente debe entrar al editor de audiencia
    """
    import urllib3 as _u3aa
    _haa = _u3aa.PoolManager()
    action = body.get("action", "")
    target_id = body.get("target_id", "")
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(400, {"error": error})
    if not target_id or not action:
        return response(400, {"error": "action y target_id son requeridos", "received_keys": list((body or {}).keys())})
    # Acciones que NO se ejecutan via API (UI guide)
    _ui_only = {
        "ab_test": "Para probar variantes ve al panel 'Г°ЕёЕЅВЇ IA' y usa 'ГўЕ“ВЁ Variantes' sobre el creative ganador.",
        "refresh_creative": "Edita el anuncio desde el dashboard para subir imagen/texto nuevos.",
        "change_targeting": "Edita la audiencia del anuncio desde el wizard.",
        "recharge_budget": "Recarga saldo desde tu cuenta de Meta Ads Manager.",
    }
    if action in _ui_only:
        return response(200, {
            "message": _ui_only[action],
            "target_id": target_id,
            "requires_ui": True,
            "action": action,
        })
    try:
        res = None
        if action == "pausar":
            res = _haa.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{target_id}",
                body=json.dumps({"status": "PAUSED"}),
                headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
            if res.status < 300:
                return response(200, {"message": "Anuncio pausado", "target_id": target_id})
        elif action == "escalar":
            camp_res = _haa.request("GET", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{target_id}?fields=daily_budget&access_token={token}", timeout=8.0)
            if camp_res.status == 200:
                current = int(json.loads(camp_res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("daily_budget", 0))
                new_budget = min(int(current * 1.2), int(current * 1.3))
                res = _haa.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{target_id}",
                    body=json.dumps({"daily_budget": new_budget}),
                    headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
                if res.status < 300:
                    return response(200, {"message": f"Presupuesto escalado a ${new_budget:,}", "target_id": target_id, "new_budget": new_budget})
        elif action == "reducir":
            camp_res = _haa.request("GET", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{target_id}?fields=daily_budget&access_token={token}", timeout=8.0)
            if camp_res.status == 200:
                current = int(json.loads(camp_res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("daily_budget", 0))
                new_budget = max(int(current * 0.8), 1000)  # min $1000 COP/dia
                res = _haa.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{target_id}",
                    body=json.dumps({"daily_budget": new_budget}),
                    headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
                if res.status < 300:
                    return response(200, {"message": f"Presupuesto reducido a ${new_budget:,}", "target_id": target_id, "new_budget": new_budget})
        elif action == "activar":
            res = _haa.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{target_id}",
                body=json.dumps({"status": "ACTIVE"}),
                headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
            if res.status < 300:
                return response(200, {"message": "Activado", "target_id": target_id})
        else:
            return response(400, {"error": f"Accion no reconocida: {action}", "supported": ["pausar","escalar","reducir","activar","ab_test","refresh_creative","change_targeting","recharge_budget"]})
        # Si llegamos aqui, Meta devolvio error
        try:
            err_msg = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("error", {}).get("message", "Error desconocido") if res else "Sin respuesta"
        except Exception:
            err_msg = "Error desconocido"
        return response(400, {"error": f"No se pudo {action}: {err_msg}"})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"apply-action {action} error: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L15144-15164 (21 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_adjust_budget(client_id, body):
    """PUT /ads/budget Гўв‚¬вЂќ Ajustar presupuesto de una campana."""
    import urllib3 as _u3ab
    _hab = _u3ab.PoolManager()
    campaign_id = body.get("campaign_id", "")
    new_budget = int(body.get("budget_daily", 0))
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(400, {"error": error})
    if not campaign_id or not new_budget:
        return response(400, {"error": "campaign_id y budget_daily son requeridos"})
    try:
        res = _hab.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{campaign_id}",
            body=json.dumps({"daily_budget": new_budget}),
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
        if res.status < 300:
            return response(200, {"message": f"Presupuesto ajustado", "campaign_id": campaign_id, "budget_daily": new_budget})
        err = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("error", {}).get("message", "Error")
        return response(400, {"error": err})
    except Exception as e:
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L15165-15222 (58 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_generate_image(client_id, body):
    """POST /ads/generate-image Гўв‚¬вЂќ Genera imagen con IA (Gemini 3.1 Flash Image)."""
    import urllib3 as _u3img
    import base64 as _b64img
    _himg = _u3img.PoolManager()
    prompt_text = body.get("prompt", "").strip()
    service_slug = body.get("service_slug", "")
    if not prompt_text:
        return response(400, {"error": "prompt es requerido"})
    gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
    if not gemini_key:
        return response(400, {"error": "GEMINI_API_KEY no configurada"})
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    brand = config.get("brand_name", "Negocio")
    # Enriquecer prompt con contexto del servicio
    svc_desc = ""
    if service_slug:
        svcs = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "services_catalog"}).get("Item", {}).get("services", [])
        svc = next((s for s in svcs if s.get("slug") == service_slug), None)
        if svc:
            svc_desc = f"{svc.get('name', '')}. {svc.get('description', '')}"
    visual_desc = config.get("visual_description", "")
    visual_ctx = f"CONTEXTO VISUAL DEL NEGOCIO: {visual_desc}. " if visual_desc else ""
    full_prompt = f"Genera una imagen publicitaria profesional para Facebook/Instagram Ads. Negocio: {brand}. {svc_desc}. {visual_ctx}Estilo: {prompt_text}. REGLAS OBLIGATORIAS: La imagen debe ser atractiva y profesional. Sin texto superpuesto. Formato cuadrado 1:1. Colores vibrantes. Alta calidad fotografica. CUMPLIR POLITICAS DE META ADS: No mostrar armas, violencia, sangre, contenido sexual, drogas, alcohol en exceso, ni contenido discriminatorio. Si el negocio involucra armas o temas sensibles, mostrar solo el ambiente profesional, instalaciones, equipamiento de seguridad o personas en actitud positiva de aprendizaje. Nunca mostrar armas apuntando a personas."
    url = f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-3.1-flash-image-preview:generateContent?key={gemini_key}"
    try:
        payload = {
            "contents": [{"parts": [{"text": full_prompt}]}],
            "generationConfig": {"responseModalities": ["TEXT", "IMAGE"]}
        }
        res = _himg.request("POST", url, body=json.dumps(payload),
            headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"}, timeout=110.0)
        if res.status == 200:
            data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
            parts = data.get("candidates", [{}])[0].get("content", {}).get("parts", [])
            for part in parts:
                if part.get("inlineData"):
                    img_b64 = part["inlineData"]["data"]
                    mime = part["inlineData"].get("mimeType", "image/png")
                    ext = "png" if "png" in mime else "jpg"
                    # Subir a S3
                    import uuid as _uuid_img
                    s3_key = f"{client_id}/ads/{_uuid_img.uuid4().hex[:8]}.{ext}"
                    s3_client.put_object(
                        Bucket="clientes-bot-media",
                        Key=s3_key,
                        Body=_b64img.b64decode(img_b64),
                        ContentType=mime
                    )
                    public_url = f"https://clientes-bot-media.s3.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/{s3_key}"
                    return response(200, {"image_url": public_url, "message": "Imagen generada"})
            logger.error(f"Gemini image: no image in response parts")
            return response(400, {"error": "No se pudo generar la imagen. Intenta con otra descripcion."})
        logger.error(f"Gemini image error {res.status}: {res.data.decode('utf-8')[:300]}")
        return response(400, {"error": "Error generando imagen"})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error generate image: {e}")
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L15223-15275 (53 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_create_account(client_id):
    """POST /ads/create-account Гўв‚¬вЂќ Crea Business Portfolio + Ad Account si no tiene."""
    import urllib3 as _u3ca
    _hca = _u3ca.PoolManager()
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    token = config.get("meta_access_token", "")
    business_id = config.get("business_id", "")
    brand = config.get("brand_name", "Mi Negocio")
    currency = config.get("currency", "COP")
    if not token or token == "pending":
        return response(400, {"error": "Conecta Facebook primero"})
    tz_map = {"COP": "America/Bogota", "MXN": "America/Mexico_City", "ARS": "America/Argentina/Buenos_Aires", "CLP": "America/Santiago", "PEN": "America/Lima", "USD": "America/New_York", "EUR": "Europe/Madrid", "BRL": "America/Sao_Paulo"}
    tz_id_map = {"America/Bogota": 141, "America/Mexico_City": 48, "America/Argentina/Buenos_Aires": 106, "America/Santiago": 27, "America/Lima": 59, "America/New_York": 1, "Europe/Madrid": 54, "America/Sao_Paulo": 21}
    tz_name = tz_map.get(currency, "America/Bogota")
    tz_id = tz_id_map.get(tz_name, 141)
    try:
        # Si no tiene business_id, buscar o crear
        if not business_id:
            biz_res = _hca.request("GET", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/me/businesses?access_token={token}", timeout=10.0)
            if biz_res.status == 200:
                businesses = json.loads(biz_res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
                if businesses:
                    business_id = businesses[0].get("id", "")
        if not business_id:
            return response(400, {"error": "No se encontro Business. Crea uno en business.facebook.com"})
        # Crear Ad Account
        payload = {
            "name": f"{brand} - Ads",
            "currency": currency,
            "timezone_id": tz_id,
            "end_advertiser": business_id,
            "media_agency": business_id,
            "partner": "NONE"
        }
        res = _hca.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{business_id}/adaccount",
            body=json.dumps(payload),
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
        if res.status < 300:
            data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
            new_account_id = data.get("id", "")
            # Guardar en config_pro
            kb_table.update_item(
                Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"},
                UpdateExpression="SET ad_account_id = :a, business_id = :b",
                ExpressionAttributeValues={":a": new_account_id, ":b": business_id}
            )
            return response(201, {"message": f"Cuenta publicitaria creada: {brand} - Ads", "ad_account_id": new_account_id})
        err = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("error", {}).get("message", "Error creando cuenta")
        logger.error(f"Error creando ad account: {err}")
        return response(400, {"error": err})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error create ad account: {e}")
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L15276-15309 (34 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_select_account(client_id, body):
    """PUT /ads/select-account Гўв‚¬вЂќ Guardar cuenta publicitaria y pagina seleccionada."""
    ad_account_id = body.get("ad_account_id", "").strip()
    page_id = body.get("page_id", "").strip()
    page_name = body.get("page_name", "").strip()
    instagram_id = body.get("instagram_id", "").strip()
    update_parts = []
    values = {}
    names = {}
    if ad_account_id:
        names["#aai"] = "ad_account_id"
        values[":aai"] = ad_account_id
        update_parts.append("#aai = :aai")
    if page_id:
        names["#pid"] = "page_id"
        values[":pid"] = page_id
        update_parts.append("#pid = :pid")
    if page_name:
        names["#pn"] = "page_name"
        values[":pn"] = page_name
        update_parts.append("#pn = :pn")
    if instagram_id:
        names["#ig"] = "instagram_actor_id"
        values[":ig"] = instagram_id
        update_parts.append("#ig = :ig")
    if not update_parts:
        return response(400, {"error": "Nada que actualizar"})
    kb_table.update_item(
        Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"},
        UpdateExpression="SET " + ", ".join(update_parts),
        ExpressionAttributeNames=names,
        ExpressionAttributeValues=values
    )
    return response(200, {"message": "Cuenta publicitaria actualizada"})


# --- L15310-15412 (103 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_pages(client_id, ad_account_id_filter=""):
    """GET /ads/pages[?ad_account_id=X] Гўв‚¬вЂќ Lista paginas de Facebook.
    
    Sin ad_account_id: TODAS las paginas del usuario (/me/accounts).
    Con ad_account_id: solo las paginas anunciables en esa cuenta (/promote_pages).
    Si falla por permisos, devuelve mensaje claro al usuario.
    """
    import urllib3 as _u3pg
    _hpg = _u3pg.PoolManager()
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    token = config.get("meta_access_token", "")
    current_page = config.get("page_id", "")
    if not token or token == "pending":
        return response(400, {"error": "Conecta Facebook primero", "needs_connect": True})
    try:
        # Si pidieron filtrar por cuenta publicitaria
        if ad_account_id_filter:
            # Asegurar formato act_XXX
            ad_acc = ad_account_id_filter if ad_account_id_filter.startswith("act_") else f"act_{ad_account_id_filter}"
            res = _hpg.request(
                "GET",
                f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_acc}/promote_pages?fields=id,name,picture,access_status&limit=200&access_token={token}",
                timeout=10.0,
            )
            body_str = res.data.decode("utf-8") if res.data else "{}"
            if res.status == 200:
                data = json.loads(body_str)
                pages_raw = data.get("data", []) or []
                if not pages_raw:
                    return response(200, {
                        "pages": [],
                        "current": current_page,
                        "warning": "Esta cuenta publicitaria no tiene paginas anunciables vinculadas. Vincula una en Business Manager > Configuracion del negocio > Cuentas publicitarias > Agregar paginas.",
                        "warning_type": "no_pages_in_account",
                    })
                pages = [
                    {
                        "id": p["id"],
                        "name": p.get("name", ""),
                        "picture": p.get("picture", {}).get("data", {}).get("url", ""),
                        "access_status": p.get("access_status", ""),
                        "selected": p["id"] == current_page,
                    }
                    for p in pages_raw
                ]
                return response(200, {"pages": pages, "current": current_page})
            elif res.status in (400, 403):
                err = json.loads(body_str).get("error", {})
                err_msg = err.get("message", "Sin permisos")
                err_code = err.get("code", 0)
                # 200 = permission denied, 100 = invalid param
                if err_code == 200:
                    return response(200, {
                        "pages": [],
                        "current": current_page,
                        "warning": "No tienes permisos para ver las paginas de esta cuenta publicitaria. Pide a tu administrador que te de acceso o reconecta Facebook.",
                        "warning_type": "permission_denied",
                    })
                logger.warning(f"Meta /promote_pages error {err_code}: {err_msg}")
                return response(200, {
                    "pages": [],
                    "current": current_page,
                    "warning": f"Error consultando paginas: {err_msg}",
                    "warning_type": "meta_error",
                })
        # Modo default: todas las paginas del usuario
        res = _hpg.request(
            "GET",
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/me/accounts?fields=id,name,picture&limit=200&access_token={token}",
            timeout=10.0,
        )
        if res.status == 200:
            data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
            pages_raw = data.get("data", []) or []
            if not pages_raw:
                return response(200, {
                    "pages": [],
                    "current": current_page,
                    "warning": "No tienes paginas de Facebook. Crea una primero en facebook.com/pages/create",
                    "warning_type": "no_pages",
                })
            pages = [
                {
                    "id": p["id"],
                    "name": p.get("name", ""),
                    "picture": p.get("picture", {}).get("data", {}).get("url", ""),
                    "selected": p["id"] == current_page,
                }
                for p in pages_raw
            ]
            return response(200, {"pages": pages, "current": current_page})
        else:
            logger.warning(f"Meta /me/accounts error {res.status}: {res.data.decode('utf-8')[:200]}")
            return response(200, {
                "pages": [],
                "current": current_page,
                "warning": "No se pudieron cargar tus paginas. Reconecta Facebook.",
                "warning_type": "meta_error",
            })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error ads pages: {e}", exc_info=True)
    return response(200, {"pages": [], "current": current_page, "warning": "Error inesperado consultando paginas"})



# --- L15433-15487 (55 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_instagram(client_id, page_id_filter=""):
    """GET /ads/instagram[?page_id=X] Гўв‚¬вЂќ IG multi-page.
    Sin page_id: recorre TODAS las paginas del usuario y devuelve todos los IGs vinculados.
    Con page_id: devuelve solo el IG de esa pagina especifica.
    """
    import urllib3 as _u3ig
    _hig = _u3ig.PoolManager()
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    user_token = config.get("meta_access_token", "")
    current_ig = config.get("instagram_actor_id", "")
    if not user_token or user_token == "pending":
        return response(200, {"instagram_accounts": [], "current": ""})
    # 1. Obtener todas las paginas con su page_token
    pages_data = meta_cached_request(
        _hig,
        f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/me/accounts?fields=id,name,access_token&limit=200",
        user_token,
        f"me_accounts_{client_id}",
        ttl=900,
    )
    all_pages = pages_data.get("data", []) or []
    # Si pidieron una pagina especifica, filtrar
    if page_id_filter:
        all_pages = [p for p in all_pages if p.get("id") == page_id_filter]
    ig_accounts = []
    for p in all_pages:
        pid = p.get("id", "")
        ptoken = p.get("access_token", "")
        pname = p.get("name", "")
        if not pid or not ptoken:
            continue
        try:
            res = _hig.request(
                "GET",
                f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{pid}?fields=instagram_business_account%7Bid%2Cusername%2Cprofile_picture_url%2Cname%7D%2Cconnected_instagram_account%7Bid%2Cusername%2Cprofile_picture_url%7D&access_token={ptoken}",
                timeout=10.0
            )
            if res.status != 200:
                continue
            data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
            iba = data.get("instagram_business_account", {}) or data.get("connected_instagram_account", {}) or {}
            if iba.get("id"):
                ig_accounts.append({
                    "id": iba["id"],
                    "username": iba.get("username", ""),
                    "profile_pic": iba.get("profile_picture_url", ""),
                    "name": iba.get("name", "") or iba.get("username", ""),
                    "page_id": pid,
                    "page_name": pname,
                    "selected": iba["id"] == current_ig,
                })
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Error IG pagina {pid}: {e}")
            continue
    return response(200, {"instagram_accounts": ig_accounts, "current": current_ig})

def handle_ads_accounts(client_id):
    """GET /ads/accounts Гўв‚¬вЂќ Lista cuentas publicitarias activas del usuario."""
    import urllib3 as _u3ac
    _hac = _u3ac.PoolManager()
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    token = config.get("meta_access_token", "")
    if not token or token == "pending":
        return response(400, {"error": "Conecta Facebook primero"})
    try:
        res = _hac.request("GET",
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/me/adaccounts?fields=id,name,account_status,currency,business&access_token={token}",
            timeout=10.0)
        if res.status == 200:
            data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
            accounts = data.get("data", [])
            # Solo activas (account_status=1)
            active = [{"id": a["id"], "name": a.get("name", ""), "currency": a.get("currency", ""), "business_name": a.get("business", {}).get("name", "")} for a in accounts if a.get("account_status") == 1]
            # Marcar cual esta seleccionada actualmente
            current = config.get("ad_account_id", "")
            for a in active:
                a["selected"] = a["id"] == current
            return response(200, {"accounts": active, "current": current})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error ads accounts: {e}")
    return response(200, {"accounts": [], "current": ""})

# --- L15525-15570 (46 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_audience_sync(client_id, body):
    import urllib3 as _u3a
    import hashlib
    _ha = _u3a.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(400, {"error": error})
    audience_name = body.get("name", "").strip() or f"CRM {client_id}"
    segment = body.get("segment", "all")
    leads_resp = leads_table.query(IndexName="company_id-index", KeyConditionExpression=Key("company_id").eq(client_id))
    leads = leads_resp.get("Items", [])
    if segment == "buyers":
        leads = [l for l in leads if l.get("is_buyer") or l.get("lead_stage") == "cerrado_ganado"]
    elif segment == "interested":
        leads = [l for l in leads if l.get("lead_stage") in ("interesado", "negociacion")]
    elif segment == "new":
        leads = [l for l in leads if l.get("lead_stage") == "nuevo"]
    if not leads:
        return response(400, {"error": "No hay leads en este segmento"})
    hashed = []
    for lead in leads:
        digits = "".join(c for c in str(lead.get("phoneNumber", "")) if c.isdigit())
        if digits:
            if not digits.startswith("57"):
                digits = "57" + digits
            hashed.append(hashlib.sha256(digits.encode()).hexdigest())
    try:
        cr = _ha.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/customaudiences",
            body=json.dumps({"name": audience_name, "subtype": "CUSTOM", "description": f"CRM {segment}", "customer_file_source": "USER_PROVIDED_ONLY"}),
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
        if cr.status >= 300:
            return response(400, {"error": json.loads(cr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("error", {}).get("message", "Error")})
        audience_id = json.loads(cr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("id", "")
        _ha.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{audience_id}/users",
            body=json.dumps({"payload": {"schema": ["PHONE"], "data": [[h] for h in hashed[:10000]], "is_raw": False}}),
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
        try:
            cfg = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
            auds = cfg.get("ads_audiences", [])
            auds.append({"id": audience_id, "name": audience_name, "segment": segment, "count": len(leads), "created_at": int(time.time())})
            kb_table.update_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}, UpdateExpression="SET ads_audiences = :a", ExpressionAttributeValues={":a": auds[-20:]})
        except Exception:
            pass
        return response(201, {"message": f"Audiencia creada con {len(leads)} contactos", "audience_id": audience_id})
    except Exception as e:
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})

def handle_ads_campaign_generate(client_id, body):
    """POST /ads/campaigns/generate Гўв‚¬вЂќ IA genera 4 variantes de creativos con contexto completo."""
    import urllib3 as _u3g
    _hg = _u3g.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(400, {"error": error})
    service_slug = body.get("service_slug", "")
    budget_daily = int(body.get("budget_daily", 10000))
    audience_id = body.get("audience_id", "")
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    brand = config.get("brand_name", "Negocio")
    currency = config.get("currency", "COP")
    # Construir contexto rico del servicio
    svc_context = ""
    svc_image = ""
    svc_name = brand
    if service_slug:
        svcs = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "services_catalog"}).get("Item", {}).get("services", [])
        svc = next((s for s in svcs if s.get("slug") == service_slug), None)
        if svc:
            svc_name = svc.get("name", "")
            svc_image = svc.get("image_url", "")
            p = svc.get("pricing", {}).get("regular_price", 0)
            promo = svc.get("pricing", {}).get("promotional_price", 0)
            chars = svc.get("characteristics", [])
            keywords = svc.get("keywords", [])
            desc = svc.get("description", "")
            svc_context = f"SERVICIO A PROMOCIONAR: "
            svc_context += f"Nombre: {svc_name}. "
            svc_context += f"Descripcion: {desc}. "
            svc_context += f"Precio: ${p:,} {currency}. "
            location = config.get("scheduling", {}).get("location_name", "") or config.get("brand_name", "")
            svc_context += f"Negocio: {brand}. "
            if promo:
                svc_context += f"Precio promocional: ${promo:,} {currency} (DESTACAR!). "
            if chars:
                svc_context += f"Caracteristicas: {', '.join(str(c) for c in chars[:5])}. "
            if keywords:
                svc_context += f"Palabras clave: {', '.join(str(k) for k in keywords[:5])}. "
    else:
        svc_context = f"PROMOCION GENERAL del negocio {brand}."
    gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
    if not gemini_key:
        return response(200, {"variants": [{"headline": svc_name[:40], "text": f"Conoce {svc_name} en {brand}", "description": "Reserva ahora", "cta": "WHATSAPP_MESSAGE"}], "service_image": svc_image})
    try:
        language = config.get("language", "espanol")
        lang_map = {"espanol": "espanol", "ingles": "English", "portugues": "portugues", "frances": "francais"}
        lang = lang_map.get(language, language)
        system = f"""Eres un experto en Facebook Ads e Instagram Ads.
Genera EXACTAMENTE 4 variantes de anuncio diferentes para {brand}.
Cada variante debe ser UNICA y enfocada en el servicio especifico.
Escribe en {lang}, tono persuasivo pero natural.
NUNCA uses texto generico como "Conoce nuestros servicios".
Siempre menciona el nombre del servicio y su beneficio principal.
Moneda: {currency}."""
        prompt = f"""{svc_context}
Genera EXACTAMENTE 4 variantes de anuncio. Cada una con enfoque diferente:
1. HOOK DIRECTO: Pregunta que enganche + beneficio + precio + ubicacion
2. PRUEBA SOCIAL: Experiencia de cliente + que incluye + como reservar
3. URGENCIA: Cupos limitados + precio especial + que incluye + requisitos
4. INFORMATIVO COMPLETO: Todo lo que necesita saber (precio, ubicacion, que incluye, requisitos, como llegar)
REGLAS PARA EL TEXTO:
- El texto principal (text) debe tener entre 300 y 800 caracteres (NO 125, Facebook permite hasta 2200)
- Incluir SIEMPRE: precio, ubicacion o ciudad, que incluye el servicio, como reservar (escribir por WhatsApp)
- Usar emojis estrategicos (2-4 por anuncio)
- Incluir un call-to-action claro al final del texto
- El headline es corto (max 40 chars) pero impactante
- La description es el subtitulo (max 30 chars)
Responde SOLO JSON valido:
{{"variants": [
  {{"headline": "Titulo corto impactante (max 40 chars)", "text": "Texto LARGO y completo del anuncio (300-800 chars). Incluir precio, ubicacion, que incluye, requisitos, como reservar. Con emojis.", "description": "Subtitulo corto (max 30 chars)", "cta": "WHATSAPP_MESSAGE"}},
  {{"headline": "...", "text": "...", "description": "...", "cta": "WHATSAPP_MESSAGE"}},
  {{"headline": "...", "text": "...", "description": "...", "cta": "WHATSAPP_MESSAGE"}},
  {{"headline": "...", "text": "...", "description": "...", "cta": "WHATSAPP_MESSAGE"}}
]}}"""
        payload = {
            "system_instruction": {"parts": [{"text": system}]},
            "contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": prompt}]}],
            "generationConfig": {"temperature": 0.8, "maxOutputTokens": 4000, "responseMimeType": "application/json"}
        }
        # Retry con fallback a modelo 2.0
        res = None
        for _attempt in range(3):
            _url_gen = f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:generateContent?key={gemini_key}"
            res = _hg.request("POST", _url_gen, body=json.dumps(payload), headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"}, timeout=30.0)
            if res.status == 200:
                break
            if res.status in (503, 429):
                import time as _t_r
                _t_r.sleep(3 * (_attempt + 1))
                continue
            break
        if res.status == 200:
            data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
            text = data["candidates"][0]["content"]["parts"][0]["text"]
            # Limpiar JSON de Gemini
            import re as _re_ads
            logger.info(f"Gemini raw ads FULL: {repr(text[:1000])}")
            clean = text.strip()
            if clean.startswith("```"):
                clean = clean.split("\n", 1)[-1]
                clean = clean.rsplit("```", 1)[0]
            # Reparar JSON truncado o malformado
            try:
                result = json.loads(clean)
            except json.JSONDecodeError:
                # Intentar reparar: quitar trailing commas, cerrar strings
                repaired = _re_ads.sub(r',\s*([}\]])', r'\1', clean)
                try:
                    result = json.loads(repaired)
                except json.JSONDecodeError:
                    logger.error(f"Gemini JSON irreparable: {clean[:300]}")
                    result = None
            if result:
                variants = result.get("variants", [])
                if variants:
                    return response(200, {"variants": variants, "budget_daily": budget_daily, "audience_id": audience_id, "service_image": svc_image, "service_name": svc_name})
        logger.error(f"Gemini ads generate status={res.status}: {res.data.decode('utf-8')[:300]}")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error generando creativos: {e}")
    return response(200, {"variants": [{"headline": svc_name[:40], "text": f"Descubre {svc_name} en {brand}. Escribenos!", "description": "Reserva ahora", "cta": "WHATSAPP_MESSAGE"}], "service_image": svc_image})
