def handle_ads_campaign_publish(client_id, body):
    import urllib3 as _u3p
    _hp = _u3p.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(400, {"error": error})
    # page_id es opcional Гўв‚¬вЂќ si no hay, se usa link directo a WhatsApp
    name = body.get("name", f"Campana {int(time.time())}")
    objective = body.get("objective", "OUTCOME_ENGAGEMENT")
    budget = int(body.get("budget_daily", 10000))
    audience_id = body.get("audience_id", "")
    variants = body.get("variants", [])
    if not variants:
        return response(400, {"error": "No hay variantes"})
    cfg = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    phone_wa = (cfg.get("phone_display", "") or "").replace("+", "").replace(" ", "")
    # Obtener imagen del servicio del catalogo
    service_slug = body.get("service_slug", "")
    svc_image = ""
    if service_slug:
        svcs = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "services_catalog"}).get("Item", {}).get("services", [])
        svc = next((s for s in svcs if s.get("slug") == service_slug), None)
        if svc:
            svc_image = svc.get("image_url", "")
    if not svc_image:
        svc_image = cfg.get("brand_logo_url", "")
    try:
        cr = _hp.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/campaigns",
            body=json.dumps({"name": name, "objective": objective, "status": "PAUSED", "special_ad_categories": [], "is_adset_budget_sharing_enabled": False}),
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
        if cr.status >= 300:
            return response(400, {"error": json.loads(cr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("error", {}).get("message", "Error")})
        campaign_id = json.loads(cr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("id", "")
        # Targeting dinamico desde wizard
        country = body.get("country", "CO")
        city = body.get("city", "")
        radius = body.get("radius", "0")
        if audience_id:
            tgt = {"custom_audiences": [{"id": audience_id}]}
        else:
            tgt = {"geo_locations": {"countries": [country]}, "age_min": 18, "age_max": 65}
            # Si hay ciudad, buscar su key en Meta API
            if city and radius != "0":
                try:
                    _city_res = _hp.request("GET",
                        f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/search?type=adgeolocation&location_types=city&q={city}&access_token={token}",
                        timeout=8.0)
                    if _city_res.status == 200:
                        _city_data = json.loads(_city_res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
                        if _city_data:
                            _city_key = _city_data[0].get("key", "")
                            if _city_key:
                                tgt["geo_locations"] = {"cities": [{"key": _city_key, "radius": int(radius), "distance_unit": "kilometer"}]}
                except Exception as _ce:
                    logger.warning(f"Error buscando ciudad en Meta: {_ce}")
        asr = _hp.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/adsets",
            body=json.dumps({"name": f"{name} - AdSet", "campaign_id": campaign_id, "daily_budget": budget, "billing_event": "IMPRESSIONS", "optimization_goal": "LINK_CLICKS", "bid_strategy": "LOWEST_COST_WITHOUT_CAP", "status": "PAUSED", "targeting": tgt}),
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
        if asr.status >= 300:
            err_full = json.loads(asr.data.decode("utf-8"))
            logger.error(f"Meta adset error: {err_full}")
            return response(400, {"error": err_full.get("error", {}).get("message", "Error adset"), "meta_error": err_full})
        adset_id = json.loads(asr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("id", "")
        ad_ids = []
        # Advantage+ multi-format creative (Bloque 4 v4)
        # Si la variante trae image_vertical/image_horizontal, subimos los 3 formatos a Meta
        # y usamos asset_feed_spec para que Meta optimice por placement.
        for idx, v in enumerate(variants[:4]):
            link = f"https://wa.me/{phone_wa}" if phone_wa else "https://wa.me/"
            img_square = v.get("image_url", "") or svc_image
            img_vertical = v.get("image_vertical", "")
            img_horizontal = v.get("image_horizontal", "")
            has_3_formats = bool(img_square and img_vertical and img_horizontal)
            creative_payload = {"name": f"{name} - Creative {idx+1}"}
            if has_3_formats:
                # Subir los 3 formatos a Meta y obtener image_hashes
                hash_square = _upload_image_to_meta_hash(_hp, ad_account, token, img_square)
                hash_vertical = _upload_image_to_meta_hash(_hp, ad_account, token, img_vertical)
                hash_horizontal = _upload_image_to_meta_hash(_hp, ad_account, token, img_horizontal)
                if hash_square and hash_vertical and hash_horizontal:
                    # Advantage+ creative con asset_feed_spec
                    creative_payload["object_story_spec"] = {"page_id": page_id or ""}
                    creative_payload["asset_feed_spec"] = {
                        "images": [
                            {"hash": hash_square},
                            {"hash": hash_vertical},
                            {"hash": hash_horizontal},
                        ],
                        "bodies": [{"text": v.get("text", "")}],
                        "titles": [{"text": v.get("headline", "")}],
                        "descriptions": [{"text": v.get("description", "")}],
                        "link_urls": [{"website_url": link}],
                        "call_to_action_types": [v.get("cta", "LEARN_MORE")],
                        "ad_formats": ["SINGLE_IMAGE"],
                    }
                    # Habilitar Advantage+ creative enhancements (mejoras automaticas de imagen/texto)
                    creative_payload["degrees_of_freedom_spec"] = {
                        "creative_features_spec": {
                            "standard_enhancements": {"enroll_status": "OPT_IN"},
                            "image_enhancements": {"enroll_status": "OPT_IN"},
                            "text_optimizations": {"enroll_status": "OPT_IN"},
                        }
                    }
                    logger.info(f"Creative {idx+1} con 3 formatos + Advantage+")
                else:
                    has_3_formats = False
                    logger.warning(f"Fallback a 1 imagen: alguno de los 3 hashes fallГѓВі")
            # Bug #73: soporte VIDEO en lugar de imagen
            video_url_v = v.get("video_url", "")
            if video_url_v:
                # Subir video a Meta y obtener video_id
                video_id, vid_err = _upload_video_to_meta(ad_account, token, video_url_v)
                if video_id:
                    creative_payload["object_story_spec"] = {
                        "page_id": page_id or "",
                        "video_data": {
                            "video_id": video_id,
                            "message": v.get("text", ""),
                            "title": v.get("headline", "")[:40],
                            "link_description": v.get("description", "")[:30],
                            "call_to_action": {
                                "type": v.get("cta", "LEARN_MORE"),
                                "value": {"link": link},
                            },
                            "image_url": v.get("image_url", "") or svc_image,  # thumbnail fallback
                        }
                    }
                    # Activar enhancements para video tambien
                    creative_payload["degrees_of_freedom_spec"] = {
                        "creative_features_spec": {
                            "standard_enhancements": {"enroll_status": "OPT_IN"},
                        }
                    }
                    logger.info(f"Creative {idx+1} con VIDEO video_id={video_id}")
                    # Saltar el fallback de imagen Гўв‚¬вЂќ ya tenemos video
                    has_3_formats = True  # bypass para evitar bloque imagen abajo
                else:
                    logger.warning(f"Video upload fail: {vid_err}, fallback a imagen")
            if not has_3_formats and not video_url_v:
                # Fallback: 1 sola imagen via picture link (compat hacia atras)
                creative_payload["object_story_spec"] = {
                    "page_id": page_id or "",
                    "link_data": {
                        "message": v.get("text", ""),
                        "link": link,
                        "picture": img_square,
                        "name": v.get("headline", ""),
                        "description": v.get("description", ""),
                        "call_to_action": {"type": v.get("cta", "LEARN_MORE")},
                    }
                }
                # Activar standard enhancements aun en modo simple
                creative_payload["degrees_of_freedom_spec"] = {
                    "creative_features_spec": {
                        "standard_enhancements": {"enroll_status": "OPT_IN"},
                    }
                }
            ccr = _hp.request(
                "POST",
                f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/adcreatives",
                body=json.dumps(creative_payload),
                headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"},
            )
            if ccr.status >= 300:
                logger.error(f"Meta creative error: {ccr.data.decode('utf-8')[:500]}")
            if ccr.status < 300:
                creative_id = json.loads(ccr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("id", "")
                adr = _hp.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/ads",
                    body=json.dumps({"name": f"{name} - Ad {idx+1}", "adset_id": adset_id, "creative": {"creative_id": creative_id}, "status": "PAUSED"}),
                    headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
                if adr.status < 300:
                    ad_ids.append(json.loads(adr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("id", ""))
        try:
            cfg2 = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
            camps = cfg2.get("ads_campaigns", [])
            camps.append({"campaign_id": campaign_id, "adset_id": adset_id, "ad_ids": ad_ids, "name": name, "status": "PAUSED", "budget_daily": budget, "created_at": int(time.time())})
            kb_table.update_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}, UpdateExpression="SET ads_campaigns = :c", ExpressionAttributeValues={":c": camps[-50:]})
        except Exception:
            pass
        return response(201, {"message": f"Campana creada (PAUSADA)", "campaign_id": campaign_id, "ads": len(ad_ids)})
    except Exception as e:
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L15915-15972 (58 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_creative_ranking(client_id):
    """GET /ads/creative-ranking Гўв‚¬вЂќ Devuelve ranking de creatives por campana.
    Lee de AdsRecommendations donde recommendation_type=creative_ranking.
    Multi-tenant: filtra por company_id del tenant.
    """
    try:
        rec_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsRecommendations")
        # Query por company_id + filtrar solo creative_ranking
        resp = rec_table.scan(
            FilterExpression="company_id = :cid AND recommendation_type = :rt",
            ExpressionAttributeValues={
                ":cid": client_id,
                ":rt": "creative_ranking",
            },
            ProjectionExpression="rec_id, campaign_id, campaign_name, ranking, "
                                "best_ctr_x100, worst_ctr_x100, best_creative_text, "
                                "total_ads, created_at",
        )
        items = resp.get("Items", [])
        
        # Agrupar por campaign_id (quedarse con el mas reciente)
        by_campaign = {}
        for item in items:
            cid = item.get("campaign_id", "")
            created = int(item.get("created_at", 0))
            if cid not in by_campaign or created > int(by_campaign[cid].get("created_at", 0)):
                by_campaign[cid] = item
        
        # Formatear response
        rankings = []
        for cid, item in by_campaign.items():
            ranking_data = item.get("ranking", [])
            # Reconvertir ctr_x100 a float para el frontend
            for r in ranking_data:
                r["ctr"] = round(int(r.get("ctr_x100", 0)) / 100, 2)
            rankings.append({
                "campaign_id": cid,
                "campaign_name": item.get("campaign_name", ""),
                "total_ads": int(item.get("total_ads", 0)),
                "best_ctr": round(int(item.get("best_ctr_x100", 0)) / 100, 2),
                "worst_ctr": round(int(item.get("worst_ctr_x100", 0)) / 100, 2),
                "best_creative_text": item.get("best_creative_text", ""),
                "ranking": ranking_data,
                "analyzed_at": int(item.get("created_at", 0)),
            })
        
        # Ordenar por best_ctr desc
        rankings.sort(key=lambda x: x.get("best_ctr", 0), reverse=True)
        
        return response(200, {
            "rankings": rankings,
            "total_campaigns": len(rankings),
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/creative-ranking: {e}")
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})
# Cache en memoria de variantes generadas: {ad_id: {"data": [...], "ts": int}}
_hook_variants_cache: dict = {}


# --- L15973-16095 (123 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def _ingest_creative_winners(company_id: str, lookback_days: int = 30) -> dict:
    """Motor 1 Гўв‚¬вЂќ Content Ingestion.
    
    Analiza creative_ranking de los ultimos N dias del tenant, identifica
    ganadores (CTR >= top20% del tenant en esa ventana) y los persiste
    enriquecidos en AdsCreativeLibrary.
    
    Retorna: {scanned, winners, ingested, threshold_ctr}
    """
    import time as _t
    from boto3.dynamodb.conditions import Attr
    
    now = int(_t.time())
    cutoff = now - lookback_days * 86400
    summary = {"scanned": 0, "winners": 0, "ingested": 0, "threshold_ctr": 0.0,
                "errors": []}
    
    try:
        rec_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsRecommendations")
        lib_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsCreativeLibrary")
        
        # 1. Scan creative_ranking del tenant en la ventana
        resp = rec_table.scan(
            FilterExpression="company_id = :cid AND recommendation_type = :rt "
                             "AND created_at >= :ts",
            ExpressionAttributeValues={
                ":cid": company_id,
                ":rt": "creative_ranking",
                ":ts": cutoff,
            },
            ProjectionExpression="campaign_id, campaign_name, #r, created_at",
            ExpressionAttributeNames={"#r": "ranking"},
        )
        items = resp.get("Items", [])
        
        # 2. Aplanar todos los ads de todos los rankings
        all_ads = []
        for item in items:
            campaign_id = item.get("campaign_id", "")
            campaign_name = item.get("campaign_name", "")
            ts = int(item.get("created_at", 0))
            for ad in (item.get("ranking", []) or []):
                ad_copy = dict(ad)
                ad_copy["_campaign_id"] = campaign_id
                ad_copy["_campaign_name"] = campaign_name
                ad_copy["_ts"] = ts
                all_ads.append(ad_copy)
        
        summary["scanned"] = len(all_ads)
        if not all_ads:
            return summary
        
        # 3. Calcular threshold (top 20% del CTR del tenant)
        ctrs = sorted([int(a.get("ctr_x100", 0)) for a in all_ads], reverse=True)
        top20_idx = max(0, int(len(ctrs) * 0.2) - 1)
        threshold_x100 = ctrs[top20_idx] if ctrs else 0
        summary["threshold_ctr"] = round(threshold_x100 / 100, 2)
        
        # Filtrar ganadores
        winners = [a for a in all_ads if int(a.get("ctr_x100", 0)) >= threshold_x100
                   and int(a.get("ctr_x100", 0)) > 0]
        summary["winners"] = len(winners)
        
        if not winners:
            return summary
        
        # 4. Detectar patron emocional con heuristica simple
        #    (Gemini analiza on-demand desde /ads/library/winners Гўв‚¬вЂќ aqui solo guardamos)
        def _quick_pattern(text: str) -> str:
            text_low = (text or "").lower()
            if any(w in text_low for w in ["ultim", "cupos", "agotad", "queda", "solo hoy"]):
                return "escasez"
            if any(w in text_low for w in ["descub", "no te pierd", "secret", "increib"]):
                return "curiosidad"
            if any(w in text_low for w in ["+50", "+100", "+1000", "clientes", "personas confiar"]):
                return "prueba_social"
            if any(w in text_low for w in ["dolor", "cansad", "frustra", "harto", "no soport"]):
                return "dolor"
            if any(w in text_low for w in ["gratis", "regalo", "obten", "consigue", "lleva"]):
                return "beneficio"
            return "neutro"
        
        # 5. Persistir winners en AdsCreativeLibrary (idempotente: creative_id como SK)
        for w in winners:
            try:
                ad_id = w.get("ad_id", "")
                if not ad_id:
                    continue
                creative_text = str(w.get("creative_text", ""))[:500]
                ctr_x100 = int(w.get("ctr_x100", 0))
                pattern = _quick_pattern(creative_text)
                
                creative_id = f"{ad_id}_{w.get('_ts', now)}"
                lib_table.put_item(Item={
                    "company_id": company_id,
                    "creative_id": creative_id,
                    "ad_id": ad_id,
                    "ad_name": w.get("ad_name", ""),
                    "campaign_id": w.get("_campaign_id", ""),
                    "campaign_name": w.get("_campaign_name", ""),
                    "creative_text": creative_text,
                    "creative_image": w.get("creative_image", ""),
                    "pattern": pattern,
                    "ctr_x100": ctr_x100,  # SK del GSI pattern-ctr-index
                    "impressions": int(w.get("impressions", 0)),
                    "clicks": int(w.get("clicks", 0)),
                    "leads": int(w.get("leads", 0)),
                    "spend": int(w.get("spend", 0)),
                    "cpl": int(w.get("cpl", 0)),
                    "ingested_at": now,
                    "ranking_ts": int(w.get("_ts", now)),
                })
                summary["ingested"] += 1
            except Exception as e:
                summary["errors"].append(str(e)[:150])
                continue
        
        logger.info(f"Motor 1 ingestion: company={company_id} {summary}")
        return summary
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"_ingest_creative_winners error: {e}", exc_info=True)
        summary["errors"].append(str(e)[:200])
        return summary


# --- L16096-16222 (127 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_library(event, client_id):
    """GET /ads/library Гўв‚¬вЂќ Lista creativos del tenant unificados.
    Query params:
    - type: image|video|copy|winners (default: image)
        * image, video, copy ГўвЂ вЂ™ lee AdsCreativeGenerations
        * winners ГўвЂ вЂ™ lee AdsCreativeLibrary (ganadores enriquecidos del Motor 1-5)
    - pattern: filtrar por patron (solo aplica a winners)
    - period: ventana en dias (default 30, max 365)
    - limit: max items (default 50, max 200)
    - cursor: paginacion (base64 LastEvaluatedKey)
    """
    try:
        from boto3.dynamodb.conditions import Key
        import time as _t
        import base64 as _b64_lib
        qs = event.get("queryStringParameters") or {}
        lib_type = (qs.get("type") or "image").strip().lower()
        pattern_filter = (qs.get("pattern") or "").strip().lower()
        period = max(1, min(365, int(qs.get("period") or 30)))
        limit = max(1, min(200, int(qs.get("limit") or 50)))
        cursor = qs.get("cursor") or ""
        cutoff = int(_t.time()) - period * 86400
        # === WINNERS (logica antigua, sin tocar) ===
        if lib_type == "winners":
            lib_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsCreativeLibrary")
            key_cond = Key("company_id").eq(client_id)
            filter_parts = ["ingested_at >= :ts"]
            attr_values = {":ts": cutoff}
            if pattern_filter:
                filter_parts.append("#p = :pat")
                attr_values[":pat"] = pattern_filter
            query_kwargs = {
                "KeyConditionExpression": key_cond,
                "FilterExpression": " AND ".join(filter_parts),
                "ExpressionAttributeValues": attr_values,
                "Limit": limit * 2,
            }
            if pattern_filter:
                query_kwargs["ExpressionAttributeNames"] = {"#p": "pattern"}
            resp = lib_table.query(**query_kwargs)
            items = resp.get("Items", [])
            items.sort(key=lambda x: int(x.get("ctr_x100", 0)), reverse=True)
            items = items[:limit]
            formatted = []
            for it in items:
                formatted.append({
                    "creative_id": it.get("creative_id", ""),
                    "ad_id": it.get("ad_id", ""),
                    "ad_name": it.get("ad_name", ""),
                    "pattern": it.get("pattern", ""),
                    "ctr": float(it.get("ctr_x100", 0)) / 100.0,
                    "thumbnail_url": it.get("thumbnail_url", ""),
                    "body_text": it.get("body_text", "")[:200],
                    "ingested_at": int(it.get("ingested_at", 0)),
                })
            return response(200, {
                "ok": True,
                "type": "winners",
                "items": formatted,
                "total": len(formatted),
                "cap": _get_library_cap(client_id),
                "current_count": _count_library_items(client_id),
            })
        # === IMAGE / VIDEO / COPY (AdsCreativeGenerations) ===
        if lib_type not in ("image", "video", "copy"):
            return response(400, {"error": f"type invalido. Usa: image|video|copy|winners"})
        gen_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsCreativeGenerations")
        query_kwargs = {
            "KeyConditionExpression": Key("company_id").eq(client_id),
            "FilterExpression": "asset_type = :at AND generated_at >= :ts",
            "ExpressionAttributeValues": {":at": lib_type, ":ts": cutoff},
            "Limit": limit * 2,
            "ScanIndexForward": False,  # mas reciente primero
        }
        if cursor:
            try:
                last_key = json.loads(_b64_lib.b64decode(cursor).decode())
                query_kwargs["ExclusiveStartKey"] = last_key
            except Exception:
                pass
        resp = gen_table.query(**query_kwargs)
        items = resp.get("Items", [])
        items = items[:limit]
        formatted = []
        for it in items:
            formatted.append({
                "generation_id": it.get("generation_id", ""),
                "asset_type": it.get("asset_type", ""),
                "asset_subtype": it.get("asset_subtype", ""),
                "s3_url": it.get("s3_url", ""),
                "service_slug": it.get("service_slug", ""),
                "business_vertical": it.get("business_vertical", ""),
                "pattern_target": it.get("pattern_target", ""),
                "language": it.get("language", "es"),
                "country": it.get("country", ""),
                "model": it.get("model", ""),
                "generated_at": int(it.get("generated_at", 0)),
                "campaign_id": it.get("campaign_id", "_pending_") if it.get("campaign_id", "_pending_") != "_pending_" else "",
                "verdict": it.get("verdict", "pending"),
                "outcome_ctr": float(it.get("outcome_ctr", 0)),
                "prompt_preview": (it.get("prompt_used") or "")[:200],
            })
        # Cursor para paginacion
        next_cursor = ""
        if resp.get("LastEvaluatedKey"):
            try:
                next_cursor = _b64_lib.b64encode(
                    json.dumps(resp["LastEvaluatedKey"], default=str).encode()
                ).decode()
            except Exception:
                pass
        cap = _get_library_cap(client_id)
        current = _count_library_items(client_id)
        return response(200, {
            "ok": True,
            "type": lib_type,
            "items": formatted,
            "total": len(formatted),
            "cap": cap,
            "current_count": current,
            "library_full": (cap > 0 and current >= cap),
            "next_cursor": next_cursor,
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"handle_ads_library error: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)[:200]})



# --- L16292-16475 (184 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def _analyze_winner_patterns(company_id: str, period_days: int = 30,
                             use_gemini: bool = True) -> dict:
    """Motor 2 Гўв‚¬вЂќ Winner Analysis.
    
    Lee AdsCreativeLibrary del tenant, dedup por ad_id (queda el mas reciente),
    re-clasifica patrones con Gemini, agrupa, devuelve top patrones + 
    sugerencias cross-tenant del vertical.
    
    Retorna: {top_patterns, winners_dedup, cross_tenant_suggestions, vertical}
    """
    import time as _t
    from boto3.dynamodb.conditions import Key
    
    now = int(_t.time())
    cutoff = now - period_days * 86400
    
    try:
        lib_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsCreativeLibrary")
        resp = lib_table.query(
            KeyConditionExpression=Key("company_id").eq(company_id),
            FilterExpression="ingested_at >= :ts",
            ExpressionAttributeValues={":ts": cutoff},
        )
        items = resp.get("Items", [])
        
        if not items:
            return {
                "top_patterns": [],
                "winners_dedup": [],
                "cross_tenant_suggestions": [],
                "vertical": None,
                "period_days": period_days,
            }
        
        # Dedup por ad_id (queda el ranking_ts mas reciente)
        by_ad = {}
        for it in items:
            ad_id = it.get("ad_id", "")
            if not ad_id:
                continue
            ts = int(it.get("ranking_ts", 0))
            if ad_id not in by_ad or ts > int(by_ad[ad_id].get("ranking_ts", 0)):
                by_ad[ad_id] = it
        winners = list(by_ad.values())
        
        # Re-clasificar pattern con Gemini si el texto existe
        if use_gemini:
            for w in winners:
                ctext = str(w.get("creative_text", ""))
                if ctext and len(ctext) >= 5:
                    new_pattern = _classify_pattern_gemini(ctext)
                    w["pattern"] = new_pattern
                    # Actualizar en DDB de paso (idempotente)
                    try:
                        lib_table.update_item(
                            Key={"company_id": company_id,
                                 "creative_id": w["creative_id"]},
                            UpdateExpression="SET #p = :p",
                            ExpressionAttributeNames={"#p": "pattern"},
                            ExpressionAttributeValues={":p": new_pattern},
                        )
                    except Exception:
                        pass
        
        # Agrupar por pattern: contar + CTR promedio + leads totales
        by_pattern = {}
        for w in winners:
            p = w.get("pattern", "neutro")
            if p not in by_pattern:
                by_pattern[p] = {
                    "pattern": p, "count": 0, "ctr_sum_x100": 0,
                    "total_leads": 0, "total_spend": 0,
                    "best_creative": None, "best_ctr_x100": 0,
                }
            ctr_x100 = int(w.get("ctr_x100", 0))
            by_pattern[p]["count"] += 1
            by_pattern[p]["ctr_sum_x100"] += ctr_x100
            by_pattern[p]["total_leads"] += int(w.get("leads", 0))
            by_pattern[p]["total_spend"] += int(w.get("spend", 0))
            if ctr_x100 > by_pattern[p]["best_ctr_x100"]:
                by_pattern[p]["best_ctr_x100"] = ctr_x100
                by_pattern[p]["best_creative"] = {
                    "ad_id": w.get("ad_id", ""),
                    "ad_name": w.get("ad_name", ""),
                    "creative_text": str(w.get("creative_text", ""))[:200],
                    "creative_image": w.get("creative_image", ""),
                    "ctr": round(ctr_x100 / 100, 2),
                    "leads": int(w.get("leads", 0)),
                }
        
        # Calcular avg + ordenar por count*avg (impacto)
        top = []
        for p, d in by_pattern.items():
            avg_ctr = round(d["ctr_sum_x100"] / d["count"] / 100, 2) if d["count"] else 0
            cpl_avg = int(d["total_spend"] / d["total_leads"]) if d["total_leads"] else 0
            top.append({
                "pattern": p,
                "count": d["count"],
                "avg_ctr": avg_ctr,
                "best_ctr": round(d["best_ctr_x100"] / 100, 2),
                "total_leads": d["total_leads"],
                "avg_cpl": cpl_avg,
                "best_creative": d["best_creative"],
                "impact_score": round(avg_ctr * d["count"], 2),
            })
        top.sort(key=lambda x: x["impact_score"], reverse=True)
        
        # Sugerencias cross-tenant Гўв‚¬вЂќ leer config_pro del tenant
        cross_suggestions = []
        vertical = None
        try:
            cfg = get_config_pro(company_id)
            vertical = cfg.get("business_vertical", "").strip().lower() or None
            optin = bool(cfg.get("ads_cross_tenant_optin", False))
            
            if vertical:
                # Leer pool del vertical (independiente del optin, todos pueden LEER)
                pool_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsCrossTenantPool")
                pool_resp = pool_table.query(
                    KeyConditionExpression=Key("vertical").eq(vertical),
                    Limit=50,
                )
                pool_items = pool_resp.get("Items", [])
                
                # Agrupar por pattern: count + avg ctr_delta
                pool_by_pattern = {}
                for pi in pool_items:
                    p = pi.get("pattern", "")
                    if not p:
                        continue
                    if p not in pool_by_pattern:
                        pool_by_pattern[p] = {"pattern": p, "count": 0,
                                              "delta_sum_x100": 0}
                    pool_by_pattern[p]["count"] += 1
                    pool_by_pattern[p]["delta_sum_x100"] += int(
                        pi.get("ctr_delta_x100", 0))
                
                # Formatear sugerencias ordenadas por count
                for p, d in pool_by_pattern.items():
                    avg_delta = round(
                        d["delta_sum_x100"] / d["count"] / 100, 2) if d["count"] else 0
                    cross_suggestions.append({
                        "pattern": p,
                        "wins_count": d["count"],
                        "avg_ctr_uplift_pct": avg_delta,
                    })
                cross_suggestions.sort(key=lambda x: x["wins_count"], reverse=True)
                cross_suggestions = cross_suggestions[:5]
        except Exception as ce:
            logger.warning(f"Cross-tenant suggestions error: {ce}")
        
        # Formatear winners para response
        winners_formatted = []
        for w in winners:
            winners_formatted.append({
                "creative_id": w.get("creative_id", ""),
                "ad_id": w.get("ad_id", ""),
                "ad_name": w.get("ad_name", ""),
                "campaign_name": w.get("campaign_name", ""),
                "creative_text": str(w.get("creative_text", ""))[:300],
                "creative_image": w.get("creative_image", ""),
                "pattern": w.get("pattern", "neutro"),
                "ctr": round(int(w.get("ctr_x100", 0)) / 100, 2),
                "leads": int(w.get("leads", 0)),
                "spend": int(w.get("spend", 0)),
                "cpl": int(w.get("cpl", 0)),
            })
        winners_formatted.sort(key=lambda x: x["ctr"], reverse=True)
        
        return {
            "top_patterns": top[:5],
            "winners_dedup": winners_formatted,
            "cross_tenant_suggestions": cross_suggestions,
            "vertical": vertical,
            "period_days": period_days,
            "total_winners_unique_ads": len(winners),
        }
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"_analyze_winner_patterns error: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return {
            "top_patterns": [], "winners_dedup": [],
            "cross_tenant_suggestions": [], "vertical": None,
            "period_days": period_days, "error": str(e)[:200],
        }


# --- L16552-16687 (136 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def _learn_from_variant(company_id: str, variant: dict,
                        access_token: str) -> dict:
    """Helper Motor 5 Гўв‚¬вЂќ evalua UNA variante a 7d y aprende.
    
    1. Fetch metricas variante + original
    2. Calcula delta CTR
    3. Si gano (>=+20%) ГўвЂ вЂ™ ingiere en AdsCreativeLibrary + cross-tenant pool
    4. Actualiza variant en AdsHookVariants con metrics_7d + verdict
    
    Retorna dict con resultado.
    """
    import time as _t
    
    now = int(_t.time())
    variant_id = variant.get("variant_id", "")
    new_ad_id = variant.get("new_ad_id", "")
    original_ad_id = variant.get("original_ad_id", "")
    pattern = variant.get("pattern", "neutro")
    hook = variant.get("hook", "")
    
    result = {"variant_id": variant_id, "verdict": "no_data",
              "ctr_delta_pct": 0, "ingested": False, "cross_tenant_pushed": False}
    
    # 1. Fetch metricas de ambos ads
    variant_metrics = _fetch_ad_metrics_7d(new_ad_id, access_token)
    original_metrics = _fetch_ad_metrics_7d(original_ad_id, access_token)
    
    if not variant_metrics or variant_metrics.get("impressions", 0) < 100:
        # No hay data suficiente Гўв‚¬вЂќ actualizar variant con verdict='insufficient'
        result["verdict"] = "insufficient_data"
        try:
            hv_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsHookVariants")
            hv_table.update_item(
                Key={"company_id": company_id, "variant_id": variant_id},
                UpdateExpression="SET metrics_7d = :m, original_metrics_7d = :om, "
                                 "verdict = :v, learned_at = :ts, #s = :st",
                ExpressionAttributeNames={"#s": "status"},
                ExpressionAttributeValues={
                    ":m": variant_metrics or {},
                    ":om": original_metrics or {},
                    ":v": "insufficient_data",
                    ":ts": now,
                    ":st": "EVALUATED",
                },
            )
        except Exception:
            pass
        return result
    
    # 2. Calcular delta
    v_ctr = float(variant_metrics.get("ctr", 0))
    o_ctr = float(original_metrics.get("ctr", 0)) if original_metrics else 0
    
    if o_ctr > 0:
        delta_pct = round(((v_ctr - o_ctr) / o_ctr) * 100, 1)
    else:
        delta_pct = 0 if v_ctr == 0 else 100  # original sin data, variante con data
    
    result["ctr_delta_pct"] = delta_pct
    
    # 3. Determinar veredicto
    if delta_pct >= 20:
        verdict = "winner"
    elif delta_pct >= 5:
        verdict = "marginal_winner"
    elif delta_pct >= -5:
        verdict = "tie"
    elif delta_pct >= -20:
        verdict = "marginal_loser"
    else:
        verdict = "loser"
    result["verdict"] = verdict
    
    # 4. Si gano (incluyendo marginal_winner), ingerir + cross-tenant
    if verdict in ("winner", "marginal_winner") and v_ctr > 0:
        try:
            lib_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsCreativeLibrary")
            ctr_x100 = int(v_ctr * 100)
            lib_table.put_item(Item={
                "company_id": company_id,
                "creative_id": f"variant_{new_ad_id}_{now}",
                "ad_id": new_ad_id,
                "ad_name": f"Variante {pattern} (auto-learned)",
                "campaign_id": variant.get("campaign_id", ""),
                "campaign_name": "Variant Winner",
                "creative_text": hook,
                "creative_image": "",
                "pattern": pattern,
                "ctr_x100": ctr_x100,
                "impressions": variant_metrics.get("impressions", 0),
                "clicks": variant_metrics.get("clicks", 0),
                "leads": variant_metrics.get("leads", 0),
                "spend": variant_metrics.get("spend", 0),
                "cpl": variant_metrics.get("cpl", 0),
                "ingested_at": now,
                "ranking_ts": now,
                "source": "variant_winner",
                "ctr_delta_pct": delta_pct,
            })
            result["ingested"] = True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Motor 5 ingest library error: {e}")
        
        # Cross-tenant pool (solo si opt-in)
        if verdict == "winner":  # solo winners fuertes
            pushed = _push_cross_tenant_pool(
                company_id, pattern,
                ctr_delta_x100=int(delta_pct * 100),
                hook_length=len(hook),
            )
            result["cross_tenant_pushed"] = pushed
    
    # 5. Actualizar variant con metrics + verdict
    try:
        hv_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsHookVariants")
        hv_table.update_item(
            Key={"company_id": company_id, "variant_id": variant_id},
            UpdateExpression="SET metrics_7d = :m, original_metrics_7d = :om, "
                             "verdict = :v, ctr_delta_pct = :d, "
                             "learned_at = :ts, #s = :st",
            ExpressionAttributeNames={"#s": "status"},
            ExpressionAttributeValues={
                ":m": variant_metrics,
                ":om": original_metrics or {},
                ":v": verdict,
                ":d": int(delta_pct * 100),  # int para DDB
                ":ts": now,
                ":st": "EVALUATED",
            },
        )
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning(f"Motor 5 update variant error: {e}")
    
    logger.info(f"Motor 5 LEARN: company={company_id} variant={variant_id} "
                f"verdict={verdict} delta={delta_pct}% v_ctr={v_ctr} o_ctr={o_ctr}")
    return result


# --- L16688-16774 (87 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_cron_variant_learn():
    """POST /ads/cron-variant-learn Гўв‚¬вЂќ cron diario.
    
    Busca variantes con learn_at <= now Y status=PENDING_REVIEW. Por cada una:
    1. Fetch metricas 7d
    2. Calcula delta CTR
    3. Si gano: ingiere en AdsCreativeLibrary + cross-tenant pool (si opt-in)
    4. Actualiza variant con verdict + metrics
    """
    import time as _t
    from boto3.dynamodb.conditions import Attr
    
    now = int(_t.time())
    summary = {
        "scanned": 0, "evaluated": 0, "winners": 0,
        "marginal_winners": 0, "losers": 0, "ties": 0,
        "insufficient": 0, "ingested": 0, "cross_tenant_pushed": 0,
        "errors": [],
    }
    
    try:
        hv_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsHookVariants")
        # Scan variantes que ya cumplieron 7d + aun pending
        resp = hv_table.scan(
            FilterExpression="learn_at <= :now AND #s = :pending",
            ExpressionAttributeNames={"#s": "status"},
            ExpressionAttributeValues={
                ":now": now,
                ":pending": "PENDING_REVIEW",
            },
        )
        variants = resp.get("Items", [])
        summary["scanned"] = len(variants)
        
        # Agrupar por company_id para no leer token N veces
        by_company = {}
        for v in variants:
            cid = v.get("company_id", "")
            if not cid:
                continue
            by_company.setdefault(cid, []).append(v)
        
        for cid, cid_variants in by_company.items():
            try:
                _resp = kb_table.get_item(
                    Key={"company_id": cid, "kb_key": "config_pro"}
                )
                cfg = _resp.get("Item", {}) or {}
                token = cfg.get("meta_access_token", "")
                if not token or token == "pending":
                    summary["errors"].append({"tenant": cid,
                                              "error": "no_token"})
                    continue
                
                for v in cid_variants:
                    try:
                        result = _learn_from_variant(cid, v, token)
                        summary["evaluated"] += 1
                        verdict = result.get("verdict", "")
                        if verdict == "winner":
                            summary["winners"] += 1
                        elif verdict == "marginal_winner":
                            summary["marginal_winners"] += 1
                        elif verdict in ("loser", "marginal_loser"):
                            summary["losers"] += 1
                        elif verdict == "tie":
                            summary["ties"] += 1
                        elif verdict == "insufficient_data":
                            summary["insufficient"] += 1
                        if result.get("ingested"):
                            summary["ingested"] += 1
                        if result.get("cross_tenant_pushed"):
                            summary["cross_tenant_pushed"] += 1
                    except Exception as e:
                        summary["errors"].append({
                            "variant": v.get("variant_id", "")[:30],
                            "error": str(e)[:150],
                        })
            except Exception as e:
                summary["errors"].append({"tenant": cid, "error": str(e)[:150]})
        
        logger.info(f"Motor 5 cron: {summary}")
        return response(200, summary)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Motor 5 cron fatal: {e}", exc_info=True)
        summary["errors"].append({"step": "fatal", "error": str(e)[:200]})
        return response(500, summary)


# --- L16775-16838 (64 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_variant_metrics(event, client_id):
    """GET /ads/variants/{variant_id}/metrics Гўв‚¬вЂќ comparativa variante vs original.
    
    Path: /ads/variants/<variant_id>/metrics
    """
    try:
        path = event.get("path", "") or event.get("rawPath", "")
        # Extraer variant_id del path
        parts = [p for p in path.split("/") if p]
        # Path esperado: ads/variants/<variant_id>/metrics
        variant_id = ""
        for i, part in enumerate(parts):
            if part == "variants" and i + 1 < len(parts):
                variant_id = parts[i + 1]
                break
        if not variant_id:
            return response(400, {"error": "variant_id requerido en el path"})
        
        hv_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsHookVariants")
        item = hv_table.get_item(
            Key={"company_id": client_id, "variant_id": variant_id}
        ).get("Item")
        
        if not item:
            return response(404, {"error": "Variante no encontrada"})
        
        # Si todavГѓВ­a no se evaluГѓВі, intentar fetch on-demand si pasaron >= 24h
        import time as _t
        now = int(_t.time())
        if not item.get("metrics_7d") and (now - int(item.get("created_at", 0))) >= 86400:
            try:
                _resp = kb_table.get_item(
                    Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}
                )
                cfg = _resp.get("Item", {}) or {}
                token = cfg.get("meta_access_token", "")
                if token and token != "pending":
                    _learn_from_variant(client_id, item, token)
                    # Re-leer item actualizado
                    item = hv_table.get_item(
                        Key={"company_id": client_id, "variant_id": variant_id}
                    ).get("Item") or item
            except Exception:
                pass
        
        # Formatear response
        return response(200, {
            "variant_id": variant_id,
            "new_ad_id": item.get("new_ad_id", ""),
            "original_ad_id": item.get("original_ad_id", ""),
            "hook": item.get("hook", ""),
            "pattern": item.get("pattern", ""),
            "status": item.get("status", "PENDING_REVIEW"),
            "verdict": item.get("verdict", "pending"),
            "ctr_delta_pct": round(int(item.get("ctr_delta_pct", 0)) / 100, 1)
                             if item.get("ctr_delta_pct") else 0,
            "metrics_variant_7d": item.get("metrics_7d") or {},
            "metrics_original_7d": item.get("original_metrics_7d") or {},
            "created_at": int(item.get("created_at", 0)),
            "learned_at": int(item.get("learned_at", 0)) if item.get("learned_at") else None,
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/variants/metrics: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L16839-17076 (238 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_duplicate_ad(event, client_id):
    """POST /ads/duplicate-ad Гўв‚¬вЂќ Motor 4: Creative Production.
    
    Duplica un ad ganador con un primary_text nuevo (variante de hook).
    El ad nuevo se crea en PAUSED para que el cliente revise antes de activar.
    
    Body: {
        "original_ad_id": "<ad_id de Meta>",
        "new_primary_text": "<hook nuevo>",
        "pattern": "escasez|curiosidad|...",  // opcional, para tracking
        "name_suffix": "v1 escasez"           // opcional, sufijo del ad_name
    }
    Response: {success, new_ad_id, new_creative_id, variant_id, status: "PAUSED"}
    """
    import time as _t
    import urllib.parse
    
    try:
        body = json.loads(event.get("body", "{}") or "{}")
        original_ad_id = (body.get("original_ad_id") or "").strip()
        new_primary_text = (body.get("new_primary_text") or "").strip()
        pattern = (body.get("pattern") or "").strip().lower() or "neutro"
        name_suffix = (body.get("name_suffix") or "").strip()
        
        if not original_ad_id or not new_primary_text:
            return response(400, {"error": "original_ad_id y new_primary_text son requeridos"})
        
        # Lanzar hooks validation
        if len(new_primary_text) > 500:
            return response(400, {"error": "new_primary_text excede 500 chars"})
        
        # 1. Cargar token + ad_account_id del tenant
        try:
            _kb_resp = kb_table.get_item(
                Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}
            )
            cfg = _kb_resp.get("Item", {}) or {}
        except Exception as _kbe:
            logger.error(f"Motor 4 kb_table.get_item error: {_kbe}")
            return response(500, {"error": "No se pudo leer config_pro del tenant"})
        access_token = cfg.get("meta_access_token", "")
        ad_account_id = cfg.get("ad_account_id", "")
        if not access_token or access_token == "pending":
            return response(400, {"error": "meta_access_token no configurado en este tenant"})
        if not ad_account_id:
            return response(400, {"error": "ad_account_id no configurado en este tenant"})
        # Normalizar ad_account_id (a veces viene con prefijo act_)
        if not ad_account_id.startswith("act_"):
            ad_account_id_clean = f"act_{ad_account_id}"
        else:
            ad_account_id_clean = ad_account_id
        
        _h_dup = _u3.PoolManager() if "_u3" in dir() else None
        # Crear PoolManager local si no existe el global
        import urllib3 as _u3_dup
        _h_dup = _u3_dup.PoolManager()
        
        # 2. GET el ad original (fields completos)
        ad_url = (
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v22.0/{original_ad_id}"
            f"?fields=name,adset_id,campaign_id,status,creative{{id,object_story_spec,"
            f"asset_feed_spec,effective_object_story_id,thumbnail_url,name}}"
            f"&access_token={access_token}"
        )
        ad_res = _h_dup.request("GET", ad_url, timeout=10.0)
        if ad_res.status != 200:
            err_body = ad_res.data.decode("utf-8")[:300]
            logger.error(f"Motor 4: GET ad falla {ad_res.status}: {err_body}")
            return response(400, {"error": "No se pudo leer el ad original",
                                  "detail": err_body, "meta_status": ad_res.status})
        ad_data = json.loads(ad_res.data.decode("utf-8"))
        adset_id = ad_data.get("adset_id", "")
        creative_orig = ad_data.get("creative", {}) or {}
        oss_orig = creative_orig.get("object_story_spec", {}) or {}
        
        if not adset_id:
            return response(400, {"error": "El ad original no tiene adset_id (es un draft?)"})
        
        afs_orig = creative_orig.get("asset_feed_spec") or {}
        has_afs = bool(afs_orig)
        has_oss_full = bool(oss_orig.get("link_data") or oss_orig.get("video_data")
                            or oss_orig.get("photo_data"))
        
        if not has_afs and not has_oss_full:
            return response(400, {"error": "El ad original no tiene estructura soportada "
                                           "(asset_feed_spec ni object_story_spec con link/video/photo_data)"})
        
        # 3. Construir creative NUEVO segun la estructura del original
        creative_name = f"Variante {pattern[:12]} - {int(_t.time())}"
        creative_payload = {
            "name": creative_name,
            "access_token": access_token,
        }
        
        if has_afs:
            # CASO Advantage+ Creative Гўв‚¬вЂќ agregamos UN body nuevo (la variante)
            # SOLO con el hook generado. Resto del asset_feed_spec se preserva intacto.
            # Limpiamos campos auto-generados por Meta que no se aceptan en POST
            afs_new = json.loads(json.dumps(afs_orig))
            
            # Quitar adlabels de TODOS los assets (Meta las regenera)
            for k in ("images", "videos", "bodies", "titles",
                      "descriptions", "link_urls"):
                for item in afs_new.get(k, []) or []:
                    item.pop("adlabels", None)
            
            # Limpiar image_crops deprecados (191x100 ГўвЂ вЂ™ Meta lo rechaza desde 2025+)
            # Mantenemos solo crops modernos. Si no hay modernos, eliminamos image_crops.
            _DEPRECATED_CROPS = {"191x100", "16x9", "9x16"}  # legacy keys
            for img in afs_new.get("images", []) or []:
                crops = img.get("image_crops") or {}
                if crops:
                    # Quitar deprecados
                    modern = {k: v for k, v in crops.items()
                              if k not in _DEPRECATED_CROPS}
                    if modern:
                        img["image_crops"] = modern
                    else:
                        img.pop("image_crops", None)
            
            # Quitar customization rules (Meta las regenera con nuevos adlabels)
            afs_new.pop("asset_customization_rules", None)
            
            # Reemplazar bodies: dejar SOLO la variante nueva
            # (Meta randomiza entre bodies; si dejamos los viejos, la variante
            # solo aparece en ~1/N requests. Quedarse con UNA fuerza el test).
            afs_new["bodies"] = [{"text": new_primary_text}]
            
            creative_payload["asset_feed_spec"] = json.dumps(afs_new)
            # object_story_spec minimo (solo page + ig) Гўв‚¬вЂќ Meta lo requiere
            oss_min = {
                "page_id": oss_orig.get("page_id", ""),
            }
            if oss_orig.get("instagram_user_id"):
                oss_min["instagram_user_id"] = oss_orig["instagram_user_id"]
            if oss_orig.get("instagram_actor_id"):
                oss_min["instagram_actor_id"] = oss_orig["instagram_actor_id"]
            if not oss_min.get("page_id"):
                return response(400, {"error": "El ad original no tiene page_id en object_story_spec"})
            creative_payload["object_story_spec"] = json.dumps(oss_min)
        else:
            # CASO clasico Гўв‚¬вЂќ reemplazar message en link/video/photo_data
            oss_new = json.loads(json.dumps(oss_orig))
            for key in ("link_data", "video_data", "photo_data"):
                if key in oss_new:
                    oss_new[key]["message"] = new_primary_text
                    break
            creative_payload["object_story_spec"] = json.dumps(oss_new)
        
        cr_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v22.0/{ad_account_id_clean}/adcreatives"
        cr_res = _h_dup.request(
            "POST", cr_url,
            fields=creative_payload,  # multipart/form-data
            timeout=15.0,
        )
        if cr_res.status not in (200, 201):
            err = cr_res.data.decode("utf-8")[:400]
            logger.error(f"Motor 4: POST adcreative falla {cr_res.status}: {err}")
            return response(400, {"error": "No se pudo crear el creative nuevo",
                                  "detail": err, "meta_status": cr_res.status})
        cr_data = json.loads(cr_res.data.decode("utf-8"))
        new_creative_id = cr_data.get("id", "")
        if not new_creative_id:
            return response(500, {"error": "Meta no retorno creative_id",
                                  "detail": cr_res.data.decode("utf-8")[:200]})
        
        # 5. POST ad nuevo en la MISMA adset, status PAUSED
        original_name = ad_data.get("name", "Ad")
        new_ad_name = f"{original_name[:60]} Гўв‚¬вЂќ {name_suffix or pattern}"[:120]
        ad_payload = {
            "name": new_ad_name,
            "adset_id": adset_id,
            "creative": json.dumps({"creative_id": new_creative_id}),
            "status": "PAUSED",  # FilosofГѓВ­a: cliente revisa antes de activar
            "access_token": access_token,
        }
        new_ad_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v22.0/{ad_account_id_clean}/ads"
        new_ad_res = _h_dup.request(
            "POST", new_ad_url,
            fields=ad_payload,
            timeout=15.0,
        )
        if new_ad_res.status not in (200, 201):
            err = new_ad_res.data.decode("utf-8")[:400]
            logger.error(f"Motor 4: POST ad falla {new_ad_res.status}: {err}")
            return response(400, {"error": "Creative creado pero ad falla",
                                  "detail": err,
                                  "new_creative_id": new_creative_id,
                                  "meta_status": new_ad_res.status})
        new_ad_data = json.loads(new_ad_res.data.decode("utf-8"))
        new_ad_id = new_ad_data.get("id", "")
        
        # 6. Persistir en AdsHookVariants (tracking para Motor 5)
        now = int(_t.time())
        variant_id = f"var_{new_ad_id}_{now}"
        try:
            hv_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsHookVariants")
            hv_table.put_item(Item={
                "company_id": client_id,
                "variant_id": variant_id,
                "original_ad_id": original_ad_id,
                "new_ad_id": new_ad_id,
                "new_creative_id": new_creative_id,
                "adset_id": adset_id,
                "campaign_id": ad_data.get("campaign_id", ""),
                "hook": new_primary_text[:500],
                "pattern": pattern,
                "name_suffix": name_suffix,
                "status": "PENDING_REVIEW",  # cliente debe activar manualmente en Meta
                "created_at": now,
                "learn_at": now + 7 * 86400,  # Motor 5 evalГѓВєa a los 7 dГѓВ­as
                "expires_at": now + 90 * 86400,  # TTL 90 dГѓВ­as
                "metrics_7d": None,  # se completa con Motor 5
            })
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Motor 4: ad creado pero tracking fallo: {e}")
        
        # 7. Audit log
        try:
            audit_log(client_id, "user", "AD_VARIANT_CREATED",
                      "ads_duplicate", f"original={original_ad_id} new={new_ad_id} pattern={pattern}")
        except Exception:
            pass
        
        logger.info(f"Motor 4 OK: company={client_id} original={original_ad_id} "
                    f"new={new_ad_id} creative={new_creative_id} pattern={pattern}")
        return response(200, {
            "success": True,
            "new_ad_id": new_ad_id,
            "new_creative_id": new_creative_id,
            "variant_id": variant_id,
            "adset_id": adset_id,
            "status": "PAUSED",
            "message": "Variante creada en Meta. Reviewala y activala manualmente desde Ads Manager (o reactivala desde este dashboard).",
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/duplicate-ad: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L17077-17128 (52 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_library_delete(event, client_id):
    """DELETE /ads/library Гўв‚¬вЂќ Bulk delete de creativos seleccionados.
    Body: {"generation_ids": ["gen_xxx", "gen_yyy", ...]}  (max 100 por request)
    Tambien borra el archivo S3 asociado (best-effort, no bloquea).
    Retorna: {ok, deleted, failed}
    """
    try:
        body = json.loads(event.get("body", "{}") or "{}")
        gen_ids = body.get("generation_ids", []) or []
        if not gen_ids:
            return response(400, {"error": "generation_ids requerido (lista)"})
        if not isinstance(gen_ids, list):
            return response(400, {"error": "generation_ids debe ser lista"})
        gen_ids = [str(g) for g in gen_ids[:100]]  # cap seguridad
        gen_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsCreativeGenerations")
        bucket = os.environ.get("S3_MEDIA_BUCKET", "clientes-bot-media")
        deleted = 0
        failed = []
        for gen_id in gen_ids:
            try:
                # Leer item primero para sacar s3_url y borrar el archivo
                got = gen_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "generation_id": gen_id})
                item = got.get("Item")
                if not item:
                    failed.append({"id": gen_id, "reason": "not_found"})
                    continue
                # Borrar S3 file (best-effort)
                s3_url = item.get("s3_url", "") or ""
                if s3_url and bucket in s3_url:
                    try:
                        from urllib.parse import urlparse
                        s3_key = urlparse(s3_url).path.lstrip("/")
                        if s3_key:
                            s3_client.delete_object(Bucket=bucket, Key=s3_key)
                    except Exception as _se:
                        logger.warning(f"delete S3 fail {gen_id}: {_se}")
                # Borrar de DDB
                gen_table.delete_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "generation_id": gen_id})
                deleted += 1
            except Exception as e:
                failed.append({"id": gen_id, "reason": str(e)[:100]})
        logger.info(f"library_delete: client={client_id} deleted={deleted} failed={len(failed)}")
        return response(200, {
            "ok": True,
            "deleted": deleted,
            "failed": failed,
            "current_count": _count_library_items(client_id),
            "cap": _get_library_cap(client_id),
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"handle_ads_library_delete error: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)[:200]})
