def handle_ads_library_winners(event, client_id):
    """GET /ads/library/winners Гўв‚¬вЂќ Top patrones del tenant + sugerencias cross-tenant.
    
    Query params:
    - period: ventana en dias (default 30, max 365)
    - skip_gemini: si "1" no re-clasifica con Gemini (mas rapido, usa pattern guardado)
    """
    try:
        qs = event.get("queryStringParameters") or {}
        period = max(1, min(365, int(qs.get("period") or 30)))
        use_gemini = (qs.get("skip_gemini") or "0") != "1"
        
        result = _analyze_winner_patterns(client_id, period_days=period,
                                          use_gemini=use_gemini)
        return response(200, result)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/library/winners: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L17147-17179 (33 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_cron_ingest_winners():
    """Cron diario Гўв‚¬вЂќ invoca _ingest_creative_winners para todos los tenants
    con phone_number_id activo en KnowledgeBase.
    """
    try:
        kb_table = dynamodb.Table("KnowledgeBase")
        # Scan tenants activos (kb_key=config_pro + phone_number_id no vacio)
        resp = kb_table.scan(
            FilterExpression="kb_key = :kb AND attribute_exists(phone_number_id) "
                             "AND phone_number_id <> :empty",
            ExpressionAttributeValues={":kb": "config_pro", ":empty": ""},
            ProjectionExpression="company_id",
        )
        tenants = [t["company_id"] for t in resp.get("Items", []) if t.get("company_id")]
        
        summary = {"tenants_checked": 0, "tenants_ingested": 0,
                   "total_winners": 0, "errors": []}
        
        for cid in tenants:
            summary["tenants_checked"] += 1
            try:
                result = _ingest_creative_winners(cid, lookback_days=30)
                if result.get("ingested", 0) > 0:
                    summary["tenants_ingested"] += 1
                    summary["total_winners"] += result["ingested"]
            except Exception as e:
                summary["errors"].append({"tenant": cid, "error": str(e)[:150]})
        
        logger.info(f"Motor 1 cron: {summary}")
        return response(200, summary)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Motor 1 cron fatal: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L17180-17404 (225 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_generate_ad_variants(event, client_id):
    """POST /ads/generate-ad-variants - Bug #69: Variantes COMPLETAS de anuncio.
    Devuelve headline + primary_text 400-600 + description + cta_button
    para reemplazar el creative completo via handle_ads_duplicate_ad.
    Body: {ad_id, creative_text, service_slug, channel}
    Response: {variants:[...], pattern_mix, model, ad_id, cached}
    """
    import urllib3 as _u3_av
    import unicodedata
    try:
        body = json.loads(event.get("body", "{}") or "{}")
        ad_id = (body.get("ad_id") or "").strip()
        creative_text = (body.get("creative_text") or "").strip()[:1500]
        service_slug = (body.get("service_slug") or "").strip()
        channel = (body.get("channel") or "facebook").strip().lower()
        gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
        if not gemini_key:
            return response(400, {"error": "GEMINI_API_KEY no configurada"})
        # 1. Cargar config_pro
        try:
            _kb = kb_table.get_item(
                Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}
            ).get("Item", {}) or {}
        except Exception:
            _kb = {}
        bp = _kb.get("business_profile", {}) or {}
        brand_name = _kb.get("brand_name", "el negocio")
        vertical = _kb.get("business_vertical", "")
        default_price = str(bp.get("default_price", "")).strip()
        currency_label = bp.get("currency_label", "COP")
        cta_phrase = str(bp.get("cta_phrase", "Escribenos por WhatsApp")).strip()
        urgency_pool = bp.get("urgency_phrases", []) or []
        value_props = bp.get("value_props", []) or []
        location = str(bp.get("location", "")).strip()
        guarantees = str(bp.get("guarantees", "")).strip()
        # 2. Brand DNA (social proof legal + voz)
        dna_block = ""
        social_proof_pool = []
        try:
            dna_table = dynamodb.Table("BrandDNA")
            dna_item = dna_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id}).get("Item")
            if dna_item and dna_item.get("dna"):
                dna = dna_item["dna"]
                social_proof_pool = dna.get("legal_social_proof", []) or []
                dna_block = (
                    f"\nVoz de marca: {str(dna.get('voice', ''))[:200]}\n"
                    f"Audiencia: {str(dna.get('target_audience', {}).get('demographics', ''))[:200]}\n"
                    f"Dolores: {json.dumps(dna.get('target_audience', {}).get('pain_points', []), ensure_ascii=False)[:250]}\n"
                    f"Diferenciadores: {json.dumps(dna.get('key_differentiators', []), ensure_ascii=False)[:250]}\n"
                )
        except Exception:
            pass
        # 3. Servicio (fallback de precio si business_profile no lo trae)
        service_block = ""
        if service_slug:
            try:
                cat = kb_table.get_item(
                    Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "services_catalog"}
                ).get("Item", {}) or {}
                for s in (cat.get("services", []) or []):
                    if s.get("slug") == service_slug:
                        pricing = s.get("pricing", {}) or {}
                        reg_price = pricing.get("regular_price", 0)
                        if not default_price and reg_price:
                            default_price = f"{int(reg_price):,} {currency_label}".replace(",", ".")
                        service_block = (
                            f"\n=== PRODUCTO ===\n"
                            f"Nombre: {s.get('name', '')}\n"
                            f"Descripcion: {str(s.get('description', ''))[:250]}\n"
                            f"Precio: {reg_price} {currency_label}\n"
                            f"Caracteristicas: {json.dumps(s.get('characteristics', [])[:5], ensure_ascii=False)[:300]}\n"
                        )
                        break
            except Exception:
                pass
        # Limites Meta por canal
        if channel == "instagram":
            primary_min, primary_max = 400, 580
            headline_max = 40
        else:
            primary_min, primary_max = 400, 600
            headline_max = 40
        description_max = 30
        # Bloques contextuales (solo si hay datos)
        bp_block = ""
        if bp:
            bp_block = "\n=== PERFIL DE MARCA ===\n"
            if location:
                bp_block += f"Ubicacion: {location}\n"
            if default_price:
                bp_block += f"Precio referencia: {default_price}\n"
            if value_props:
                bp_block += f"Value props: {json.dumps(value_props[:5], ensure_ascii=False)}\n"
            if urgency_pool:
                bp_block += f"Frases urgencia disponibles: {json.dumps(urgency_pool[:5], ensure_ascii=False)}\n"
            if guarantees:
                bp_block += f"Garantias: {guarantees}\n"
            bp_block += f"CTA reusable: {cta_phrase}\n"
        sp_block = ""
        if social_proof_pool:
            sp_block = (
                "\n=== SOCIAL PROOF LEGAL (usa 1 por variante) ===\n"
                + "\n".join([f"- {sp}" for sp in social_proof_pool[:5]])
            )
        ref_block = ""
        if creative_text:
            ref_block = f"\n=== ANUNCIO GANADOR (tono de referencia, NO copiar) ===\n{creative_text[:800]}\n"
        prompt = (
            f"Eres copywriter senior de Facebook/Instagram Ads. CTR alto, hooks fuertes.\n"
            f"Genera 3 variantes COMPLETAS de anuncio para {brand_name}"
            f"{' (' + vertical + ')' if vertical else ''}.\n"
            f"Cada variante con patron emocional DISTINTO: escasez, prueba_social, beneficio_directo.\n\n"
            f"{bp_block}{sp_block}{service_block}{dna_block}{ref_block}\n"
            f"REGLAS POR VARIANTE:\n"
            f"- headline: max {headline_max} chars, hook fuerte\n"
            f"- primary_text: ENTRE {primary_min} Y {primary_max} chars. "
            f"Estructura: hook (10-15 chars) + dolor/curiosidad + 2-3 value_props "
            f"+ social_proof + urgencia + CTA explicito + precio si aplica\n"
            f"- description: max {description_max} chars, complementa headline\n"
            f"- cta_button: uno de [MESSAGE_PAGE, LEARN_MORE, SHOP_NOW, SIGN_UP, "
            f"CONTACT_US, GET_QUOTE, APPLY_NOW, BOOK_TRAVEL]\n"
            f"- Patron emocional DIFERENTE en cada variante\n"
            f"- Sin emojis al inicio (anti-spam Meta)\n"
            f"- Cumplir politicas Meta: no violencia explicita, no claims medicos exagerados\n\n"
            f"Responde SOLO JSON valido."
        )
        prompt_norm = "".join(
            c for c in unicodedata.normalize("NFD", prompt)
            if unicodedata.category(c) != "Mn"
        )[:12000]
        response_schema = {
            "type": "object",
            "properties": {
                "variants": {
                    "type": "array",
                    "items": {
                        "type": "object",
                        "properties": {
                            "headline": {"type": "string"},
                            "primary_text": {"type": "string"},
                            "description": {"type": "string"},
                            "cta_button": {
                                "type": "string",
                                "enum": ["MESSAGE_PAGE", "LEARN_MORE", "SHOP_NOW",
                                        "SIGN_UP", "CONTACT_US", "GET_QUOTE",
                                        "APPLY_NOW", "BOOK_TRAVEL"]
                            },
                            "pattern": {"type": "string"},
                            "angle": {"type": "string"},
                            "social_proof_used": {"type": "string"},
                            "char_count": {"type": "integer"}
                        },
                        "required": ["headline", "primary_text", "description",
                                     "cta_button", "pattern", "angle"]
                    }
                },
                "pattern_mix": {"type": "string"}
            },
            "required": ["variants"]
        }
        payload = {
            "contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": prompt_norm}]}],
            "generationConfig": {
                "temperature": 0.85,
                "maxOutputTokens": 4096,
                "responseMimeType": "application/json",
                "responseSchema": response_schema,
                "thinkingConfig": {"thinkingBudget": 0}
            }
        }
        _h_av = _u3_av.PoolManager()
        models = ["gemini-2.5-flash-lite", "gemini-flash-lite-latest"]
        last_err = ""
        for model in models:
            try:
                url = (
                    f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/"
                    f"models/{model}:generateContent?key={gemini_key}"
                )
                res = _h_av.request("POST", url, body=json.dumps(payload),
                                    headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"},
                                    timeout=25.0)
                if res.status != 200:
                    last_err = f"{model} status={res.status} body={res.data.decode('utf-8')[:200]}"
                    logger.warning(f"generate-ad-variants {last_err}")
                    continue
                data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
                text = (data.get("candidates", [{}])[0]
                        .get("content", {}).get("parts", [{}])[0]
                        .get("text", "")).strip()
                if text.startswith("```"):
                    text = text.split("\n", 1)[-1].rsplit("```", 1)[0].strip()
                parsed = json.loads(text)
                variants = parsed.get("variants", []) or []
                if not variants:
                    last_err = f"{model}: variants vacio"
                    continue
                # Validacion + char_count auto
                clean = []
                for v in variants[:3]:
                    pt = str(v.get("primary_text", ""))[:600]
                    v["primary_text"] = pt
                    v["headline"] = str(v.get("headline", ""))[:40]
                    v["description"] = str(v.get("description", ""))[:30]
                    v["char_count"] = len(pt)
                    clean.append(v)
                patterns = [v.get("pattern", "") for v in clean]
                logger.info(f"ad-variants OK: company={client_id} model={model} "
                            f"count={len(clean)} patterns={patterns}")
                return response(200, {
                    "ok": True,
                    "variants": clean,
                    "pattern_mix": "+".join(patterns),
                    "model": model,
                    "ad_id": ad_id,
                    "cached": False
                })
            except Exception as e:
                last_err = f"{model}: {str(e)[:200]}"
                logger.warning(f"generate-ad-variants error {last_err}")
                continue
        return response(500, {"error": f"Gemini fallo: {last_err}"})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/generate-ad-variants: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)[:200]})


# --- L17405-17621 (217 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_generate_hook_variants(event, client_id):
    """POST /ads/generate-hook-variants Гўв‚¬вЂќ Genera 3 variantes de hook basadas
    en un creative ganador. Usa Gemini Flash Lite (barato + sin bug acentos).
    
    Body: {"ad_id": "...", "creative_text": "...", "campaign_name": "..."}
    Response: {"variants": [{"hook": "...", "pattern": "..."}], "cached": bool}
    """
    import time as _t
    try:
        body = json.loads(event.get("body", "{}") or "{}")
        ad_id = (body.get("ad_id") or "").strip()
        creative_text = (body.get("creative_text") or "").strip()
        campaign_name = (body.get("campaign_name") or "").strip()
        
        if not ad_id or not creative_text:
            return response(400, {"error": "ad_id y creative_text son requeridos"})
        
        # Motor 3 extendido: multi_pattern=true genera 3 hooks de 3 patrones DISTINTOS
        multi_pattern = bool(body.get("multi_pattern", False))
        
        # Cache 5 min por (ad_id, multi_pattern)
        now = int(_t.time())
        cache_key = f"{ad_id}#multi" if multi_pattern else ad_id
        cached = _hook_variants_cache.get(cache_key)
        if cached and (now - cached["ts"]) < 300:
            return response(200, {
                "variants": cached["data"],
                "cached": True,
                "ad_id": ad_id,
                "multi_pattern": multi_pattern,
            })
        
        gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
        if not gemini_key:
            return response(400, {"error": "GEMINI_API_KEY no configurada"})
        
        # Quitar acentos del input (Bug #29 Гўв‚¬вЂќ Gemini vomita \n con UTF-8)
        import unicodedata
        creative_norm = "".join(
            c for c in unicodedata.normalize("NFD", creative_text)
            if unicodedata.category(c) != "Mn"
        )
        
        # Motor 3 extendido: si multi_pattern, sugerir los top patrones del tenant
        suggested_patterns_block = ""
        if multi_pattern:
            try:
                # Reusa Motor 2 sin Gemini (rapido, lee de DDB)
                wa = _analyze_winner_patterns(client_id, period_days=60,
                                              use_gemini=False)
                top = wa.get("top_patterns", [])[:3]
                cross = wa.get("cross_tenant_suggestions", [])[:3]
                
                suggested = []
                for tp in top:
                    if tp.get("pattern") and tp["pattern"] != "neutro":
                        suggested.append(tp["pattern"])
                # Si no hay datos del tenant, usar cross-tenant del vertical
                if not suggested and cross:
                    suggested = [c["pattern"] for c in cross if c.get("pattern")]
                # Default si no hay nada: 3 patrones clasicos
                if not suggested:
                    suggested = ["escasez", "curiosidad", "prueba_social"]
                # Asegurar 3 distintos
                while len(suggested) < 3:
                    for p in ["escasez", "curiosidad", "beneficio", "prueba_social", "dolor"]:
                        if p not in suggested:
                            suggested.append(p)
                            break
                suggested = suggested[:3]
                
                suggested_patterns_block = (
                    f"\n\nEn esta industria los patrones que mas convierten son: "
                    f"{', '.join(suggested)}. "
                    f"Genera UNA variante de cada patron (3 variantes en total, "
                    f"cada una con un patron DISTINTO)."
                )
            except Exception:
                suggested_patterns_block = (
                    "\n\nGenera 3 variantes con 3 patrones DISTINTOS: "
                    "escasez, curiosidad, prueba_social."
                )
        
        if multi_pattern:
            prompt = (
                "Eres un copywriter experto en Facebook Ads con CTR alto. "
                "Tu trabajo es generar 3 variantes de hook (gancho inicial) "
                "basadas en un anuncio GANADOR, cada una con un patron emocional "
                "DISTINTO para diversificar el testing.\n\n"
                f"Anuncio ganador (CTR alto comprobado):\n"
                f"---\n{creative_norm[:600]}\n---"
                f"{suggested_patterns_block}\n\n"
                "Cada variante debe tener:\n"
                "- Maximo 125 caracteres (limite primary text Meta)\n"
                "- Mismo idioma del original (espanol)\n"
                "- Sin emojis al inicio (anti-spam Meta)\n"
                "- Hook fuerte en las primeras 8 palabras\n"
                "- Patron emocional DISTINTO entre las 3 variantes\n\n"
                "Responde SOLO en JSON valido con esta estructura exacta:\n"
                "{\n"
                '  "pattern": "multi",\n'
                '  "variants": [\n'
                '    {"hook": "texto v1", "angle": "...", "pattern": "escasez"},\n'
                '    {"hook": "texto v2", "angle": "...", "pattern": "curiosidad"},\n'
                '    {"hook": "texto v3", "angle": "...", "pattern": "prueba_social"}\n'
                "  ]\n"
                "}"
            )
        else:
            prompt = (
                "Eres un copywriter experto en Facebook Ads con CTR alto. "
                "Tu trabajo es generar 3 variantes de hook (gancho inicial) "
                "basadas en un anuncio GANADOR.\n\n"
                f"Anuncio ganador (CTR alto comprobado):\n"
                f"---\n{creative_norm[:600]}\n---\n\n"
                "Analiza el patron emocional/psicologico del ganador "
                "(urgencia, curiosidad, beneficio, dolor, prueba social, etc) "
                "y genera 3 variantes que MANTENGAN ese mismo patron pero con "
                "angulos distintos. Cada variante debe tener:\n"
                "- Maximo 125 caracteres (limite primary text Meta)\n"
                "- Mismo idioma del original (espanol)\n"
                "- Sin emojis al inicio (anti-spam Meta)\n"
                "- Hook fuerte en las primeras 8 palabras\n\n"
                "Responde SOLO en JSON valido con esta estructura exacta:\n"
                "{\n"
                '  "pattern": "urgencia|curiosidad|beneficio|dolor|prueba_social|escasez",\n'
                '  "variants": [\n'
                '    {"hook": "texto variante 1", "angle": "que cambia vs original"},\n'
                '    {"hook": "texto variante 2", "angle": "..."},\n'
                '    {"hook": "texto variante 3", "angle": "..."}\n'
                "  ]\n"
                "}"
            )
        
        payload = {
            "contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": prompt}]}],
            "generationConfig": {
                "temperature": 0.85,
                "maxOutputTokens": 600,
                "responseMimeType": "application/json",
            },
        }
        
        # Cascada: gemini-2.5-flash-lite ГўвЂ вЂ™ gemini-flash-lite-latest
        import urllib3 as _u3_hgv
        _hgv = _u3_hgv.PoolManager()
        models = ["gemini-2.5-flash-lite", "gemini-flash-lite-latest"]
        last_err = ""
        for model in models:
            try:
                url = (
                    f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/"
                    f"models/{model}:generateContent?key={gemini_key}"
                )
                res = _hgv.request(
                    "POST", url,
                    body=json.dumps(payload),
                    headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"},
                    timeout=15.0,
                )
                if res.status != 200:
                    last_err = f"{model} status={res.status}"
                    continue
                data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
                text = (
                    data.get("candidates", [{}])[0]
                    .get("content", {})
                    .get("parts", [{}])[0]
                    .get("text", "")
                ).strip()
                # Quitar markdown si vino envuelto
                if text.startswith("```"):
                    text = text.split("\n", 1)[-1].rsplit("```", 1)[0].strip()
                parsed = json.loads(text)
                variants = parsed.get("variants", [])
                pattern = parsed.get("pattern", "")
                
                # Sanitizar Гўв‚¬вЂќ en multi_pattern cada variante trae su propio pattern
                clean_variants = []
                for v in variants[:3]:
                    hook = str(v.get("hook", "")).strip()[:200]
                    angle = str(v.get("angle", "")).strip()[:100]
                    v_pattern = str(v.get("pattern", "")).strip().lower() if multi_pattern else pattern
                    if hook:
                        clean_variants.append({
                            "hook": hook,
                            "angle": angle,
                            "pattern": v_pattern or pattern,
                        })
                
                if not clean_variants:
                    last_err = f"{model} variants vacias"
                    continue
                
                # Cache
                _hook_variants_cache[cache_key] = {"data": clean_variants, "ts": now}
                logger.info(
                    f"Hook variants OK: ad_id={ad_id} model={model} "
                    f"pattern={pattern} count={len(clean_variants)}"
                )
                return response(200, {
                    "variants": clean_variants,
                    "cached": False,
                    "ad_id": ad_id,
                    "model": model,
                    "pattern": pattern,
                    "multi_pattern": multi_pattern,
                })
            except Exception as e:
                last_err = f"{model}: {str(e)[:100]}"
                continue
        
        logger.error(f"Hook variants fallback: {last_err}")
        return response(500, {"error": "No se pudo generar variantes", "detail": last_err})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/generate-hook-variants: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L17622-17798 (177 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_cron_recommend():
    """POST /ads/cron-recommend - B6.5.D: cron diario que SOLO genera recomendaciones.
    
    NO aplica cambios. Por cada tenant con ads configurados:
      1. Trae campanas activas + insights 24h y 7d (Meta API)
      2. Para cada campana: corre _b65_analyze_campaign con datos reales + AdsAttribution
      3. Tambien corre _b65_check_account_balance a nivel cuenta publicitaria
      4. Genera recomendaciones en la tabla AdsRecommendations (status=pending)
    
    El cliente las revisa en /dashboard/ads/recommendations y decide aplicarlas o no.
    Reemplaza al cron viejo (handle_ads_cron_optimize) que aplicaba cambios automaticos.
    """
    import urllib3 as _u3
    _h = _u3.PoolManager()
    summary = {
        "tenants_checked": 0,
        "tenants_with_recs": 0,
        "total_recommendations": 0,
        "by_type": {},
        "errors": [],
    }
    try:
        # 1) Listar tenants con ads configurados (mismo patron que cron viejo)
        resp = kb_table.scan(
            FilterExpression="kb_key = :kb AND attribute_exists(ad_account_id) AND attribute_exists(meta_access_token)",
            ExpressionAttributeValues={":kb": "config_pro"},
            ProjectionExpression="company_id, ad_account_id, meta_access_token, brand_name"
        )
        tenants = resp.get("Items", [])
        summary["tenants_checked"] = len(tenants)
        logger.info(f"B6.5 cron: {len(tenants)} tenants con ads configurados")
        
        for t in tenants:
            cid = t.get("company_id", "")
            ad_account = t.get("ad_account_id", "")
            token = t.get("meta_access_token", "")
            if not cid or not ad_account or not token or token == "pending":
                continue
            
            tenant_recs = []
            try:
                # 2) Traer campanas ACTIVE de la cuenta
                url_camps = (
                    f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/campaigns"
                    f"?fields=id,name,status,effective_status,daily_budget"
                    f"&filtering=[{{'field':'effective_status','operator':'IN','value':['ACTIVE']}}]"
                    f"&limit=25&access_token={token}"
                )
                cres = _h.request("GET", url_camps, timeout=12.0)
                if cres.status != 200:
                    summary["errors"].append({"tenant": cid, "step": "list_campaigns", "code": cres.status})
                    continue
                campaigns = json.loads(cres.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
                
                # 3) Total spend del ad_account 7d (para regla 6 y ROAS calculations)
                spend_url = (
                    f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/insights"
                    f"?fields=spend&date_preset=last_7d&access_token={token}"
                )
                sres = _h.request("GET", spend_url, timeout=10.0)
                ad_spend_7d_cents = 0
                daily_spend_cents = 0
                if sres.status == 200:
                    sd = json.loads(sres.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
                    if sd:
                        # Meta devuelve spend en unidades base (USD/MXN: dolares; COP: pesos)
                        # Convertir a "cents-like" para consistencia interna (mult x 100)
                        ad_spend_7d_cents = int(float(sd[0].get("spend", 0)) * 100)
                        daily_spend_cents = ad_spend_7d_cents // 7
                
                # 4) Por cada campana: insights 7d + 24h + ventana anterior
                for camp_idx, camp in enumerate(campaigns):
                    camp_id = camp.get("id", "")
                    if not camp_id:
                        continue
                    # Rate limit: 1s entre campaГѓВ±as para no saturar Meta API
                    if camp_idx > 0:
                        time.sleep(1)
                    daily_budget = int(camp.get("daily_budget", 0) or 0)
                    
                    # Metricas 7d
                    m7 = _b65_fetch_campaign_metrics(_h, camp_id, token, "last_7d")
                    # Metricas 7d anteriores (para detectar tendencia CTR)
                    m7_prev = _b65_fetch_campaign_metrics(_h, camp_id, token, "last_14d")
                    # Metricas 24h
                    m24 = _b65_fetch_campaign_metrics(_h, camp_id, token, "yesterday")
                    m24_prev = _b65_fetch_campaign_metrics(_h, camp_id, token, "last_3d")
                    
                    # Calcular CTR_prev_7d como las 7d anteriores (14d total - 7d recientes)
                    impr_14 = m7_prev.get("impressions", 0)
                    impr_7 = m7.get("impressions", 0)
                    clicks_14 = m7_prev.get("clicks", 0)
                    clicks_7 = m7.get("clicks", 0)
                    impr_prev = max(0, impr_14 - impr_7)
                    clicks_prev = max(0, clicks_14 - clicks_7)
                    ctr_prev_7d = (clicks_prev / impr_prev * 100) if impr_prev else 0
                    
                    # CPL prev 24h: 3d - yesterday (aproximacion)
                    leads_24 = m24.get("leads", 0)
                    leads_prev = max(0, m24_prev.get("leads", 0) - leads_24)
                    spend_24_cents = m24.get("spend_cents", 0)
                    spend_prev_cents = max(0, m24_prev.get("spend_cents", 0) - spend_24_cents)
                    cpl_now = (spend_24_cents // leads_24) if leads_24 else 0
                    cpl_prev = (spend_prev_cents // leads_prev) if leads_prev else 0
                    
                    campaign_metrics = {
                        "id": camp_id,
                        "name": camp.get("name", camp_id),
                        "daily_budget_cents": daily_budget,
                        "impressions": impr_7,
                        "clicks": clicks_7,
                        "ctr": m7.get("ctr", 0),
                        "ctr_prev_7d": ctr_prev_7d,
                        "ctr_24h": m24.get("ctr", 0),
                        "cpm_cents": m7.get("cpm_cents", 0),
                        "cpc_cents": m7.get("cpc_cents", 0),
                        "cpl_cents": cpl_now,
                        "cpl_prev": cpl_prev,
                    }
                    
                    # 5) Analizar
                    rec_ids = _b65_analyze_campaign(
                        company_id=cid,
                        campaign=campaign_metrics,
                        ad_account_id=ad_account,
                        ad_spend_cents=ad_spend_7d_cents,
                    )
                    tenant_recs.extend(rec_ids)
                    
                    # B6.5 v2: analisis a nivel creative (ranking de ads por CTR)
                    # Solo para campanas con suficientes impressions (evitar ruido)
                    if impr_7 >= 500:
                        try:
                            _b65_fetch_ad_creative_ranking(
                                _h, camp_id, token, cid, camp.get("name", camp_id)
                            )
                        except Exception as _cr_err:
                            logger.warning(f"B6.5 v2 creative ranking skip: {_cr_err}")
                
                # 6) Regla 6: balance check (a nivel ad_account, no campana)
                rid_balance = _b65_check_account_balance(
                    company_id=cid,
                    ad_account_id=ad_account,
                    access_token=token,
                    daily_spend_cents=daily_spend_cents,
                )
                if rid_balance:
                    tenant_recs.append(rid_balance)
                
                if tenant_recs:
                    summary["tenants_with_recs"] += 1
                    summary["total_recommendations"] += len(tenant_recs)
                    logger.info(f"B6.5 cron tenant {cid}: {len(tenant_recs)} recomendaciones generadas")
                
                # TODO B6.5.6: si hay rec con impact_estimate_cents > $50k COP -> push FCM al owner
                # Lo conectamos cuando agreguemos send_push_to_owner helper
            
            except Exception as te:
                logger.error(f"B6.5 cron error para tenant {cid}: {te}")
                summary["errors"].append({"tenant": cid, "step": "analyze", "error": str(te)[:150]})
        
        # Contar by_type para el response del cron
        if summary["total_recommendations"] > 0:
            try:
                rec_tbl = dynamodb.Table("AdsRecommendations")
                # Las recien creadas tienen created_at en los ultimos 5 min
                cutoff = int(time.time()) - 300
                # No tenemos GSI por created_at solo - skip stats detalladas, las leemos via /ads/recommendations
            except Exception:
                pass
        
        logger.info(f"B6.5 cron resumen: {summary}")
        return response(200, summary)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"B6.5 cron fatal: {e}", exc_info=True)
        summary["errors"].append({"step": "fatal", "error": str(e)[:200]})
        return response(200, summary)


# --- L17799-17835 (37 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def _b65_fetch_campaign_metrics(http_pool, campaign_id: str, token: str,
                                  date_preset: str) -> dict:
    """Helper: trae metricas Meta Insights de una campana para un date_preset.
    Returns dict con impressions, clicks, ctr, cpm_cents, cpc_cents, leads, spend_cents.
    """
    try:
        url = (
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{campaign_id}/insights"
            f"?fields=impressions,clicks,ctr,cpm,cpc,spend,actions"
            f"&date_preset={date_preset}&access_token={token}"
        )
        res = http_pool.request("GET", url, timeout=10.0)
        if res.status != 200:
            return {}
        data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
        if not data:
            return {}
        d = data[0]
        # Buscar leads en actions[]
        leads = 0
        for act in (d.get("actions") or []):
            at = act.get("action_type", "")
            if at in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d",
                      "onsite_conversion.lead_grouped"):
                leads += int(float(act.get("value", 0) or 0))
        return {
            "impressions": int(d.get("impressions", 0) or 0),
            "clicks": int(d.get("clicks", 0) or 0),
            "ctr": float(d.get("ctr", 0) or 0),
            "cpm_cents": int(float(d.get("cpm", 0) or 0) * 100),
            "cpc_cents": int(float(d.get("cpc", 0) or 0) * 100),
            "spend_cents": int(float(d.get("spend", 0) or 0) * 100),
            "leads": leads,
        }
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning(f"B6.5 fetch metrics error {campaign_id} {date_preset}: {e}")
        return {}
