def handle_ads_cron_optimize():
    """Legacy Гўв‚¬вЂќ reemplazado por handle_ads_cron_recommend."""
    pass


# --- L17839-18052 (214 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def _b65_fetch_ad_creative_ranking(http_pool, campaign_id: str, token: str,
                                    company_id: str, campaign_name: str) -> list:
    """B6.5 v2: trae ads individuales de una campana + metricas 7d de cada uno.
    Retorna lista ordenada por CTR desc (ranking de creatives).
    Guarda el ranking en AdsRecommendations como tipo 'creative_ranking'.
    
    Multi-tenant: usa meta_cached_request para no golpear Meta API.
    """
    try:
        # 1. Traer ads de la campana
        ads_url = (
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{campaign_id}/ads"
            f"?fields=id,name,status,creative{{id,body,title,image_url,thumbnail_url}}"
            f"&limit=50&access_token={token}"
        )
        ads_res = http_pool.request("GET", ads_url, timeout=10.0)
        if ads_res.status != 200:
            return []
        ads = json.loads(ads_res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
        if not ads:
            return []
        
        # 2. Metricas 7d de cada ad
        ranked = []
        for ad in ads[:20]:  # Max 20 ads por campana (rate limit safety)
            ad_id = ad.get("id", "")
            if not ad_id:
                continue
            try:
                m_url = (
                    f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_id}/insights"
                    f"?fields=impressions,clicks,ctr,cpm,cpc,spend,actions"
                    f"&date_preset=last_7d&access_token={token}"
                )
                m_res = http_pool.request("GET", m_url, timeout=8.0)
                if m_res.status != 200:
                    continue
                m_data = json.loads(m_res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
                if not m_data:
                    continue
                d = m_data[0]
                
                # Extraer leads de actions[]
                leads = 0
                for act in (d.get("actions") or []):
                    at = act.get("action_type", "")
                    if at in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d",
                              "onsite_conversion.lead_grouped"):
                        leads += int(float(act.get("value", 0) or 0))
                
                impressions = int(d.get("impressions", 0) or 0)
                clicks = int(d.get("clicks", 0) or 0)
                ctr = float(d.get("ctr", 0) or 0)
                spend = float(d.get("spend", 0) or 0)
                cpl = (spend / leads) if leads > 0 else 0
                
                # Extraer creative data
                creative = ad.get("creative", {}) or {}
                
                ranked.append({
                    "ad_id": ad_id,
                    "ad_name": ad.get("name", ""),
                    "ad_status": ad.get("status", ""),
                    "creative_id": creative.get("id", ""),
                    "creative_text": creative.get("body", "") or creative.get("title", ""),
                    "creative_image": creative.get("image_url", "") or creative.get("thumbnail_url", ""),
                    "impressions": impressions,
                    "clicks": clicks,
                    "ctr": round(ctr, 2),
                    "spend": round(spend, 0),
                    "leads": leads,
                    "cpl": round(cpl, 0),
                })
            except Exception:
                continue
        
        # 3. Ordenar por CTR desc (el creative con mejor CTR primero)
        ranked.sort(key=lambda x: x.get("ctr", 0), reverse=True)
        
        # ============================================================
        # B6.5 v2 Гўв‚¬вЂќ Regla #8: KILL_CREATIVE
        # Detecta creatives perdedores: CTR<1% + >=500 impr + CPL>2x promedio.
        # Solo RECOMIENDA (no auto-pausa). Cliente decide desde tab "Г°ЕёЕЅВЇ IA".
        # ============================================================
        try:
            _cpls = [r.get("cpl", 0) for r in ranked if r.get("cpl", 0) > 0]
            _avg_cpl = (sum(_cpls) / len(_cpls)) if _cpls else 0
            _kc_created = 0
            for _ad in ranked:
                _impr = int(_ad.get("impressions", 0))
                _ctr = float(_ad.get("ctr", 0))
                _cpl = float(_ad.get("cpl", 0))
                _spend = int(_ad.get("spend", 0))
                _ad_id = _ad.get("ad_id", "")
                if not _ad_id:
                    continue
                # Criterios duros (todos deben cumplirse)
                if _impr < 500:
                    continue
                if _ctr >= 1.0:
                    continue
                if _avg_cpl <= 0 or _cpl <= (2 * _avg_cpl):
                    continue
                # Anti-spam: compound key campaign#ad para filtrar por anuncio,
                # no por campana entera (sino dismiss 1 ad bloquea todos).
                _compound_cid = f"{campaign_id}#{_ad_id}"
                if _b65_already_dismissed_recently(company_id, _compound_cid, "kill_creative"):
                    continue
                _b65_create_recommendation(
                    company_id=company_id,
                    campaign_id=_compound_cid,
                    campaign_name=f"{campaign_name} > {_ad.get('ad_name', _ad_id)[:40]}",
                    ad_account_id="",
                    rec_type="kill_creative",
                    justification={
                        "impressions": _impr,
                        "ctr_pct": round(_ctr, 2),
                        "cpl_cop": _cpl,
                        "avg_cpl_campaign": round(_avg_cpl, 0),
                        "threshold_ctr_pct": 1.0,
                        "threshold_cpl_multiplier": 2.0,
                        "spend_wasted_cop": _spend,
                    },
                    impact_cents=_spend * 100,  # spend ya en COP enteros, convert a cents
                    confidence=85,
                    suggested_action={
                        "type": "pause_ad",
                        "ad_id": _ad_id,
                        "ad_name": _ad.get("ad_name", ""),
                        "creative_text": str(_ad.get("creative_text", ""))[:200],
                        "reason": "low_ctr_high_cpl",
                    },
                )
                _kc_created += 1
                logger.info(
                    f"B6.5 v2 KILL_CREATIVE: ad={_ad_id} CTR={_ctr}% "
                    f"CPL={_cpl} avg={_avg_cpl:.0f} spend={_spend}"
                )
            if _kc_created:
                logger.info(f"B6.5 v2: {_kc_created} kill_creative recs creadas para {campaign_name}")
        except Exception as _kc_err:
            logger.warning(f"B6.5 v2 kill_creative skip: {_kc_err}")
        
        # 4. Guardar ranking en AdsRecommendations (para que el frontend lo lea)
        if ranked and company_id:
            try:
                rec_table = dynamodb.Table("AdsRecommendations")
                rec_id = f"creative_ranking_{campaign_id}_{int(time.time())}"
                # Convertir floats a tipos DDB-safe (Decimal no necesario si usamos int/str)
                _safe_ranking = []
                for _r in ranked[:10]:
                    _safe_ranking.append({
                        "ad_id": _r.get("ad_id", ""),
                        "ad_name": _r.get("ad_name", ""),
                        "ad_status": _r.get("ad_status", ""),
                        "creative_id": _r.get("creative_id", ""),
                        "creative_text": str(_r.get("creative_text", ""))[:200],
                        "creative_image": _r.get("creative_image", ""),
                        "impressions": int(_r.get("impressions", 0)),
                        "clicks": int(_r.get("clicks", 0)),
                        "ctr_x100": int(_r.get("ctr", 0) * 100),  # 2.45% ГўвЂ вЂ™ 245 (evita float)
                        "spend": int(_r.get("spend", 0)),
                        "leads": int(_r.get("leads", 0)),
                        "cpl": int(_r.get("cpl", 0)),
                    })
                rec_table.put_item(Item={
                    "company_id": company_id,
                    "rec_id": rec_id,
                    "recommendation_type": "creative_ranking",
                    "campaign_id": campaign_id,
                    "campaign_name": campaign_name,
                    "ranking": _safe_ranking,
                    "best_ctr_x100": int(ranked[0].get("ctr", 0) * 100) if ranked else 0,
                    "best_creative_text": str(ranked[0].get("creative_text", ""))[:200] if ranked else "",
                    "worst_ctr_x100": int(ranked[-1].get("ctr", 0) * 100) if ranked else 0,
                    "total_ads": len(ranked),
                    "status": "info",
                    "created_at": int(time.time()),
                    "expires_at": int(time.time()) + 7 * 86400,
                })
                logger.info(f"B6.5 v2: creative ranking guardado para {campaign_name} ({len(ranked)} ads, best CTR={ranked[0].get('ctr', 0)}%)")
            except Exception as _re:
                logger.warning(f"B6.5 v2: error guardando ranking: {_re}")
        
        return ranked
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning(f"B6.5 v2 creative ranking error {campaign_id}: {e}")
        return []
    """POST /ads/cron-optimize Гўв‚¬вЂќ Cron diario: optimiza campanas de TODOS los clientes."""
    try:
        # Buscar todos los clientes con ads configurados
        resp = kb_table.scan(
            FilterExpression="kb_key = :kb AND attribute_exists(ad_account_id)",
            ExpressionAttributeValues={":kb": "config_pro"},
            ProjectionExpression="company_id"
        )
        clients = [item["company_id"] for item in resp.get("Items", [])]
        results = []
        for cid in clients:
            try:
                result = handle_ads_auto_optimize(cid)
                body_data = json.loads(result.get("body", "{}"))
                actions = body_data.get("actions", [])
                alerts = body_data.get("alerts", [])
                if actions or alerts:
                    results.append({"company_id": cid, "actions": len(actions), "alerts": len(alerts)})
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Cron optimize error for {cid}: {e}")
        logger.info(f"Ads cron: {len(clients)} clientes, {len(results)} con acciones")
        return response(200, {"clients_checked": len(clients), "clients_with_actions": len(results), "details": results})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error cron optimize: {e}")
        return response(200, {"error": str(e)})



# --- L18053-18160 (108 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_auto_optimize(client_id):
    """POST /ads/auto-optimize Гўв‚¬вЂќ Optimizacion automatica (cron diario o manual).
    Proteccion de presupuesto + redistribucion + alertas."""
    import urllib3 as _u3ao
    _hao = _u3ao.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(200, {"actions": [], "message": "Sin config de ads"})
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    currency = config.get("currency", "COP")
    actions_taken = []
    alerts = []
    try:
        # Obtener campanas activas
        res = _hao.request("GET",
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/campaigns?fields=id,name,status,effective_status,daily_budget&filtering=[{{'field':'effective_status','operator':'IN','value':['ACTIVE']}}]&limit=20&access_token={token}",
            timeout=15.0)
        if res.status != 200:
            return response(200, {"actions": [], "message": "Error leyendo campanas"})
        camps = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
        for camp in camps:
            cid = camp.get("id", "")
            cname = camp.get("name", "")
            budget = int(camp.get("daily_budget", 0))
            # Metricas ultimas 24h
            try:
                mr = _hao.request("GET",
                    f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{cid}/insights?fields=spend,impressions,clicks,ctr,actions,frequency&date_preset=today&access_token={token}",
                    timeout=10.0)
                m = {}
                c_leads = 0
                if mr.status == 200:
                    md = json.loads(mr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
                    if md:
                        m = md[0]
                        for a in m.get("actions", []):
                            if a.get("action_type") in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d"):
                                c_leads += int(a.get("value", 0))
                c_spend = float(m.get("spend", 0))
                c_freq = float(m.get("frequency", 0))
                c_ctr = float(m.get("ctr", 0))
                c_impressions = int(m.get("impressions", 0))
            except Exception:
                continue
            # PROTECCION: spend > budget * 1.2 -> pausar
            if budget > 0 and c_spend > budget * 1.2:
                try:
                    _hao.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{cid}",
                        body=json.dumps({"status": "PAUSED"}),
                        headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
                    actions_taken.append({"action": "pausar", "campaign": cname, "reason": f"Gasto ${c_spend:,.0f} excede presupuesto ${budget:,.0f}"})
                except Exception:
                    pass
            # SATURACION: frequency > 2.5 y CTR cayendo
            if c_freq > 2.5:
                alerts.append({"campaign": cname, "type": "saturacion", "message": f"Frequency {c_freq}. Renueva creativos."})
            # SIN RESULTADOS: gasto > $15 USD equiv sin leads
            usd_rates = {"COP": 4200, "MXN": 17, "ARS": 900, "USD": 1}
            rate = usd_rates.get(currency, 1)
            spend_usd = c_spend / rate if rate > 0 else c_spend
            if spend_usd > 15 and c_leads == 0 and c_impressions > 1000:
                alerts.append({"campaign": cname, "type": "sin_resultados", "message": f"${c_spend:,.0f} gastados hoy sin leads."})
        # REDISTRIBUCION: mover presupuesto de peor a mejor
        # Solo si hay 2+ campanas activas con datos
        camps_with_data = [c for c in camps if int(c.get("daily_budget", 0)) > 0]
        if len(camps_with_data) >= 2:
            camp_scores = []
            for camp in camps_with_data:
                cid = camp.get("id", "")
                try:
                    mr = _hao.request("GET",
                        f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{cid}/insights?fields=spend,actions&date_preset=last_3d&access_token={token}",
                        timeout=8.0)
                    c_leads = 0
                    c_spend = 0
                    if mr.status == 200:
                        md = json.loads(mr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
                        if md:
                            c_spend = float(md[0].get("spend", 0))
                            for a in md[0].get("actions", []):
                                if a.get("action_type") in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d"):
                                    c_leads += int(a.get("value", 0))
                    cpl = c_spend / c_leads if c_leads > 0 else 999999
                    camp_scores.append({"id": cid, "name": camp.get("name", ""), "budget": int(camp.get("daily_budget", 0)), "leads": c_leads, "cpl": cpl})
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if len(camp_scores) >= 2:
                camp_scores.sort(key=lambda x: x["cpl"])
                best = camp_scores[0]
                worst = camp_scores[-1]
                if best["leads"] > 0 and worst["cpl"] > best["cpl"] * 2:
                    # Mover 15% del peor al mejor (max 30%)
                    move = min(int(worst["budget"] * 0.15), int(best["budget"] * 0.30))
                    if move > 1000:
                        try:
                            _hao.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{best['id']}",
                                body=json.dumps({"daily_budget": best["budget"] + move}),
                                headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
                            _hao.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{worst['id']}",
                                body=json.dumps({"daily_budget": max(worst["budget"] - move, 2000)}),
                                headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
                            actions_taken.append({"action": "redistribuir", "from": worst["name"], "to": best["name"], "amount": move, "reason": f"Mejor CPL: {best['name']} (${best['cpl']:,.0f}) vs {worst['name']} (${worst['cpl']:,.0f})"})
                        except Exception:
                            pass
        return response(200, {"actions": actions_taken, "alerts": alerts, "campaigns_checked": len(camps)})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error auto-optimize: {e}")
        return response(200, {"actions": [], "alerts": [], "error": str(e)})


# --- L18161-18293 (133 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_launch(client_id, body):
    """POST /ads/launch Гўв‚¬вЂќ Lanza campanas con funnel inteligente."""
    import urllib3 as _u3l
    _hl = _u3l.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(400, {"error": error})
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    brand = config.get("brand_name", "Negocio")
    currency = config.get("currency", "COP")
    # PRE-LAUNCH CHECK
    errors_list = []
    service_slug = body.get("service_slug", "")
    budget_daily = int(body.get("budget_daily", 0))
    variants = body.get("variants", [])
    country = body.get("country", "CO")
    city = body.get("city", "")
    radius = body.get("radius", "0")
    if not budget_daily or budget_daily < 3000:
        errors_list.append("Presupuesto diario minimo: $3,000")
    if not variants:
        errors_list.append("No hay variantes de anuncio")
    if not page_id:
        errors_list.append("No hay pagina de Facebook")
    if not ad_account:
        errors_list.append("No hay cuenta publicitaria")
    for i, v in enumerate(variants):
        if not v.get("headline") or not v.get("text"):
            errors_list.append(f"Variante {i+1} incompleta")
    if errors_list:
        return response(400, {"error": "Pre-launch check fallido", "checks_failed": errors_list})
    # DECIDIR ESTRUCTURA
    usd_rates = {"COP": 4200, "MXN": 17, "ARS": 900, "CLP": 950, "PEN": 3.7, "BRL": 5, "USD": 1, "EUR": 0.92}
    rate = usd_rates.get(currency, 1)
    budget_usd = budget_daily / rate if rate > 0 else budget_daily
    structure = "single" if budget_usd < 15 else ("double" if budget_usd < 50 else "full")
    # TARGETING
    targeting = {"age_min": int(body.get("age_min", 18)), "age_max": int(body.get("age_max", 65))}
    gender = body.get("gender", "all")
    if gender == "male":
        targeting["genders"] = [1]
    elif gender == "female":
        targeting["genders"] = [2]
    if city and radius != "0":
        try:
            cr = _hl.request("GET", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/search?type=adgeolocation&location_types=city&q={city}&access_token={token}", timeout=8.0)
            if cr.status == 200:
                cd = json.loads(cr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
                if cd:
                    targeting["geo_locations"] = {"cities": [{"key": cd[0]["key"], "radius": int(radius), "distance_unit": "kilometer"}]}
        except Exception:
            pass
    if "geo_locations" not in targeting:
        targeting["geo_locations"] = {"countries": [country]}
    interests = body.get("interests", [])
    if interests:
        targeting["flexible_spec"] = [{"interests": [{"id": i.get("id",""), "name": i.get("name","")} for i in interests]}]
    cities = body.get("cities", [])
    if cities and "cities" not in targeting.get("geo_locations", {}):
        targeting["geo_locations"]["cities"] = [{"key": c["key"]} for c in cities]
        targeting["geo_locations"].pop("countries", None)
    excluded = body.get("excluded_cities", [])
    if excluded:
        targeting["excluded_geo_locations"] = {"cities": [{"key": c["key"]} for c in excluded]}
    phone_wa = (config.get("phone_display", "") or "").replace("+", "").replace(" ", "")
    link = f"https://wa.me/{phone_wa}" if phone_wa else "https://wa.me/"
    svc_image = ""
    if service_slug:
        svcs = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "services_catalog"}).get("Item", {}).get("services", [])
        svc = next((s for s in svcs if s.get("slug") == service_slug), None)
        if svc:
            svc_image = svc.get("image_url", "")
    # HELPER: crear campana + adset + ads
    def _create_camp(name, objective, opt_goal, budget, tgt):
        cids = {"campaign_id": "", "adset_id": "", "ad_ids": []}
        cr = _hl.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/campaigns",
            body=json.dumps({"name": name, "objective": objective, "status": "PAUSED", "special_ad_categories": [], "is_adset_budget_sharing_enabled": False}),
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
        if cr.status >= 300:
            return None
        cids["campaign_id"] = json.loads(cr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("id", "")
        asr = _hl.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/adsets",
            body=json.dumps({"name": f"{name} - AdSet", "campaign_id": cids["campaign_id"], "daily_budget": budget, "billing_event": "IMPRESSIONS", "optimization_goal": opt_goal, "bid_strategy": "LOWEST_COST_WITHOUT_CAP", "status": "PAUSED", "targeting": tgt}),
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
        if asr.status >= 300:
            return None
        cids["adset_id"] = json.loads(asr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("id", "")
        for idx, v in enumerate(variants[:4]):
            ccr = _hl.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/adcreatives",
                body=json.dumps({"name": f"{name} - Creative {idx+1}", "object_story_spec": {"page_id": page_id, "link_data": {"message": v.get("text", ""), "link": link, "picture": v.get("image_url", svc_image), "name": v.get("headline", ""), "description": v.get("description", ""), "call_to_action": {"type": v.get("cta", "WHATSAPP_MESSAGE")}}}}),
                headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
            if ccr.status < 300:
                crid = json.loads(ccr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("id", "")
                adr = _hl.request("POST", f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/ads",
                    body=json.dumps({"name": f"{name} - Ad {idx+1}", "adset_id": cids["adset_id"], "creative": {"creative_id": crid}, "status": "PAUSED"}),
                    headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
                if adr.status < 300:
                    cids["ad_ids"].append(json.loads(adr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("id", ""))
        return cids
    # CREAR CAMPANAS
    created = []
    base_name = body.get("name", brand)
    try:
        if structure == "single":
            r = _create_camp(f"{base_name} - Leads", "OUTCOME_LEADS", "LEAD_GENERATION", budget_daily, targeting)
            if r:
                created.append({"type": "leads", **r, "budget": budget_daily})
        else:
            if structure == "double":
                splits = [("awareness", "OUTCOME_AWARENESS", "REACH", int(budget_daily * 0.35)), ("leads", "OUTCOME_LEADS", "LEAD_GENERATION", int(budget_daily * 0.65))]
            else:
                splits = [("awareness", "OUTCOME_AWARENESS", "REACH", int(budget_daily * 0.25)), ("consideration", "OUTCOME_TRAFFIC", "LINK_CLICKS", int(budget_daily * 0.30)), ("leads", "OUTCOME_LEADS", "LEAD_GENERATION", int(budget_daily * 0.45))]
            for stage, obj, opt, bgt in splits:
                if bgt < 2000:
                    continue
                r = _create_camp(f"{base_name} - {stage.capitalize()}", obj, opt, bgt, targeting)
                if r:
                    created.append({"type": stage, **r, "budget": bgt})
        # Guardar
        try:
            cfg = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
            camps = cfg.get("ads_campaigns", [])
            for cc in created:
                camps.append({**cc, "name": base_name, "status": "PAUSED", "created_at": int(time.time())})
            kb_table.update_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}, UpdateExpression="SET ads_campaigns = :c", ExpressionAttributeValues={":c": camps[-50:]})
        except Exception:
            pass
        total_ads = sum(len(c.get("ad_ids", [])) for c in created)
        return response(201, {"message": f"Funnel creado: {len(created)} campana(s), {total_ads} anuncios", "structure": structure, "campaigns": created, "note": "Campanas PAUSADAS. Activalas cuando estes listo."})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error ads launch: {e}")
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})



# --- L18294-18326 (33 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_init(client_id, period="last_30d", ad_account_id=""):
    """GET /ads/init Гўв‚¬вЂќ UN solo endpoint que devuelve TODO lo que la pagina de ads necesita.
    Reemplaza 7 fetches paralelos del frontend = 7x menos rate limit en Meta.
    Usa meta_cached_request() para no golpear Meta cada vez (TTL 15 min).
    """
    try:
        dashboard = handle_ads_dashboard(client_id, period)
        accounts = handle_ads_accounts(client_id)
        pages = handle_ads_pages(client_id)
        instagram = handle_ads_instagram(client_id)
        audiences = handle_ads_audiences_list(client_id)
        saved_audiences = handle_ads_saved_audiences_list(client_id)
        campaigns = handle_ads_campaigns_list(client_id)
        # Cada handler devuelve un dict con statusCode + body. Extraemos el body.
        def _body(resp):
            if isinstance(resp, dict) and "body" in resp:
                try:
                    return json.loads(resp["body"])
                except Exception:
                    return {}
            return resp or {}
        return response(200, {
            "dashboard": _body(dashboard),
            "accounts": _body(accounts),
            "pages": _body(pages),
            "instagram": _body(instagram),
            "audiences": _body(audiences),
            "saved_audiences": _body(saved_audiences),
            "campaigns": _body(campaigns),
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/init: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L18327-18486 (160 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_dashboard(client_id, period="last_30d"):
    """GET /ads/dashboard Гўв‚¬вЂќ Metricas globales + por campana + status correcto + rendimiento."""
    import urllib3 as _u3d
    _hd = _u3d.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    empty = {"global": {"spend": 0, "impressions": 0, "clicks": 0, "leads": 0, "ctr": 0, "cpl": 0}, "campaigns": [], "alerts": []}
    if error:
        return response(200, empty)
    # Periodos validos de Meta
    valid_periods = {"today": "today", "last_7d": "last_7d", "last_30d": "last_30d", "last_90d": "last_90d"}
    date_preset = valid_periods.get(period, "last_30d")
    try:
        # 1. Metricas globales
        _global_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/insights?fields=spend,impressions,clicks,ctr,cpc,actions,reach,frequency&date_preset={date_preset}"
        _global_cache_key = f"{client_id}_dash_global_{date_preset}"
        _global_data = meta_cached_request(_hd, _global_url, token, _global_cache_key, ttl=900)
        g = {}
        g_leads = 0
        gdata = _global_data.get("data", [])
        if True:
            if gdata:
                g = gdata[0]
                for a in g.get("actions", []):
                    if a.get("action_type") in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d", "onsite_conversion.lead_grouped"):
                        g_leads += int(a.get("value", 0))
        g_spend = float(g.get("spend", 0))
        global_metrics = {
            "spend": g_spend,
            "impressions": int(g.get("impressions", 0)),
            "reach": int(g.get("reach", 0)),
            "clicks": int(g.get("clicks", 0)),
            "ctr": round(float(g.get("ctr", 0)), 2),
            "frequency": round(float(g.get("frequency", 0)), 1),
            "leads": g_leads,
            "cpl": round(g_spend / g_leads, 0) if g_leads > 0 else 0,
        }
        # Cruzar con CRM para ventas reales
        try:
            pays = payments_table.query(IndexName="company_id-index", KeyConditionExpression=Key("company_id").eq(client_id))
            paid = [p for p in pays.get("Items", []) if p.get("status") == "PAGADO"]
            total_revenue = sum(int(p.get("amount", 0)) for p in paid)
            global_metrics["sales"] = len(paid)
            global_metrics["revenue"] = total_revenue
            global_metrics["roas"] = round(total_revenue / g_spend, 1) if g_spend > 0 else 0
        except Exception:
            global_metrics["sales"] = 0
            global_metrics["revenue"] = 0
            global_metrics["roas"] = 0
        # 2. Metricas por campana
        _camps_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/campaigns?fields=id,name,status,effective_status,daily_budget,lifetime_budget,objective,created_time&limit=25"
        _camps_cache_key = f"{client_id}_dash_campaigns"
        _camps_data = meta_cached_request(_hd, _camps_url, token, _camps_cache_key, ttl=900)
        campaigns = []
        alerts = []
        if True:
            camps_data = _camps_data.get("data", [])
            for c in camps_data:
                cid = c.get("id", "")
                eff_status = c.get("effective_status", c.get("status", "UNKNOWN"))
                # Metricas de esta campana
                c_spend = 0
                c_impressions = 0
                c_clicks = 0
                c_ctr = 0
                c_leads = 0
                c_frequency = 0
                c_reach = 0
                ad_count = 0
                try:
                    _ci_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{cid}/insights?fields=spend,impressions,clicks,ctr,actions,reach,frequency&date_preset={date_preset}"
                    _ci_cache_key = f"{client_id}_dash_camp_{cid}_{date_preset}"
                    _ci_raw = meta_cached_request(_hd, _ci_url, token, _ci_cache_key, ttl=900)
                    if True:
                        ci_data = _ci_raw.get("data", [])
                        if ci_data:
                            ci = ci_data[0]
                            c_spend = float(ci.get("spend", 0))
                            c_impressions = int(ci.get("impressions", 0))
                            c_clicks = int(ci.get("clicks", 0))
                            c_ctr = round(float(ci.get("ctr", 0)), 2)
                            c_reach = int(ci.get("reach", 0))
                            c_frequency = round(float(ci.get("frequency", 0)), 1)
                            for a in ci.get("actions", []):
                                if a.get("action_type") in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d", "onsite_conversion.lead_grouped"):
                                    c_leads += int(a.get("value", 0))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                # Contar ads
                try:
                    _ads_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{cid}/ads?fields=id&limit=50"
                    _ads_cache_key = f"{client_id}_dash_ads_{cid}"
                    _ads_raw = meta_cached_request(_hd, _ads_url, token, _ads_cache_key, ttl=900)
                    if True:
                        ad_count = len(_ads_raw.get("data", []))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                # Calcular rendimiento
                c_cpl = round(c_spend / c_leads, 0) if c_leads > 0 else 0
                if c_leads >= 3 and c_cpl < (global_metrics["cpl"] * 1.2 if global_metrics["cpl"] > 0 else 999999):
                    rendimiento = "alto"
                elif c_leads > 0:
                    rendimiento = "medio"
                elif c_spend > 0 and c_impressions > 500:
                    rendimiento = "bajo"
                else:
                    rendimiento = "sin_datos"
                # Status humano
                status_map = {
                    "ACTIVE": "activa", "PAUSED": "pausada", "DELETED": "eliminada",
                    "ARCHIVED": "archivada", "WITH_ISSUES": "con_problemas",
                    "CAMPAIGN_PAUSED": "pausada", "ADSET_PAUSED": "pausada",
                    "IN_PROCESS": "procesando", "DISAPPROVED": "rechazada"
                }
                status_human = status_map.get(eff_status, eff_status.lower() if eff_status else "desconocido")
                # Si esta ACTIVE pero sin spend en el periodo, marcar como "sin actividad"
                if eff_status == "ACTIVE" and c_spend == 0 and c_impressions == 0:
                    status_human = "sin actividad"
                raw_budget = int(c.get("daily_budget", 0)) if c.get("daily_budget") else 0
                campaigns.append({
                    "campaign_id": cid,
                    "name": c.get("name", ""),
                    "status": eff_status,
                    "status_human": status_human,
                    "rendimiento": rendimiento,
                    "budget_daily": raw_budget,
                    "objective": c.get("objective", ""),
                    "ad_count": ad_count,
                    "metrics": {
                        "spend": c_spend,
                        "impressions": c_impressions,
                        "reach": c_reach,
                        "clicks": c_clicks,
                        "ctr": c_ctr,
                        "leads": c_leads,
                        "cpl": c_cpl,
                        "frequency": c_frequency,
                    },
                    "created_at": int(time.mktime(time.strptime(c["created_time"][:19], "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S"))) if c.get("created_time") else 0,
                })
                # Alertas
                if eff_status == "ACTIVE":
                    if c_frequency > 2.5 and c_ctr > 0:
                        alerts.append({"campaign": c.get("name", ""), "type": "saturacion", "message": f"Frequency {c_frequency} - tus anuncios se estan saturando. Renueva creativos.", "severity": "warning"})
                    if c_spend > 15 and c_leads == 0 and c_impressions > 1000:
                        alerts.append({"campaign": c.get("name", ""), "type": "sin_resultados", "message": f"${c_spend:,.0f} gastados sin leads. Revisa el creativo o la oferta.", "severity": "danger"})
                    if c_ctr < 0.5 and c_leads == 0 and c_impressions > 1000:
                        alerts.append({"campaign": c.get("name", ""), "type": "ctr_bajo", "message": "CTR muy bajo y sin leads. El creativo no esta funcionando.", "severity": "danger"})
                    if c_leads >= 3 and c_cpl < (global_metrics["cpl"] * 0.7 if global_metrics["cpl"] > 0 else 0):
                        alerts.append({"campaign": c.get("name", ""), "type": "oportunidad", "message": f"Esta campana tiene CPL bajo (${c_cpl:,.0f}). Considera escalar.", "severity": "success"})
        # Ordenar: activas primero, luego por spend
        campaigns.sort(key=lambda x: (0 if x["status"] in ("ACTIVE",) else 1, -x["metrics"]["spend"]))
        return response(200, {
            "global": global_metrics,
            "campaigns": campaigns,
            "alerts": alerts,
            "period": date_preset,
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error ads dashboard: {e}")
        return response(200, empty)


# --- L18487-18510 (24 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_campaign_toggle(client_id, body):
    """PUT /ads/campaigns/toggle Гўв‚¬вЂќ Pausar o activar una campana en Meta."""
    import urllib3 as _u3t
    _ht = _u3t.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(400, {"error": error})
    campaign_id = body.get("campaign_id", "").strip()
    new_status = body.get("status", "").strip()
    if not campaign_id:
        return response(400, {"error": "campaign_id es requerido"})
    if new_status not in ("ACTIVE", "PAUSED"):
        return response(400, {"error": "status debe ser ACTIVE o PAUSED"})
    try:
        res = _ht.request("POST",
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{campaign_id}",
            body=json.dumps({"status": new_status}),
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"})
        if res.status < 300:
            return response(200, {"message": f"Campana {'activada' if new_status == 'ACTIVE' else 'pausada'}", "campaign_id": campaign_id, "status": new_status})
        err = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("error", {}).get("message", "Error")
        return response(400, {"error": err})
    except Exception as e:
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L18511-18592 (82 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_campaigns_list(client_id):
    """GET /ads/campaigns Гўв‚¬вЂќ Lista campanas con effective_status (estado REAL de Meta).
    Usa campos anidados para eliminar N+1 queries (ad count viene en el mismo request).
    Cache 5 min via meta_cached_request.
    """
    import urllib3 as _u3cl
    _hcl = _u3cl.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    local_camps = config.get("ads_campaigns", [])
    if error or not ad_account:
        return response(200, {"campaigns": local_camps})
    try:
        # effective_status = estado REAL actual (ACTIVE, PAUSED, ARCHIVED, etc)
        # ads.limit(0).summary(total_count) = count de ads sin cargarlos (N+1 eliminado)
        fields = "id,name,status,effective_status,daily_budget,created_time,objective,ads.limit(0).summary(total_count){id}"
        data = meta_cached_request(
            _hcl,
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/campaigns?fields={fields}&limit=50",
            token,
            f"camps_list_{ad_account}",
            ttl=300,
        )
        # Obtener phone_number_id del tenant para detectar campanas conectadas al bot
        bot_phone_id = config.get("phone_number_id", "")

        meta_camps = []
        for c in data.get("data", []):
            cid = c.get("id", "")
            ad_count = c.get("ads", {}).get("summary", {}).get("total_count", 0) if isinstance(c.get("ads"), dict) else 0
            raw_budget = int(c.get("daily_budget", 0)) if c.get("daily_budget") else 0
            real_status = c.get("effective_status") or c.get("status", "UNKNOWN")

            # Detectar si la campana esta conectada al bot via adsets
            connected_to_bot = False
            whatsapp_number = ""
            try:
                adsets_url = (
                    f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{cid}/adsets"
                    f"?fields=destination_type,promoted_object&limit=5&access_token={token}"
                )
                adsets_res = _hcl.request("GET", adsets_url, timeout=8.0)
                if adsets_res.status == 200:
                    adsets_data = json.loads(adsets_res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [])
                    for adset in adsets_data:
                        dest = adset.get("destination_type", "")
                        promoted = adset.get("promoted_object", {}) or {}
                        wa_phone = str(promoted.get("whatsapp_phone_number_id", ""))
                        if dest in ("WHATSAPP", "MESSENGER_WHATSAPP") or wa_phone:
                            whatsapp_number = wa_phone
                            if bot_phone_id and wa_phone == str(bot_phone_id):
                                connected_to_bot = True
                            elif wa_phone:
                                connected_to_bot = False  # WA pero otro numero
                            break
            except Exception as _ce:
                logger.warning(f"No se pudo verificar adsets de campana {cid}: {_ce}")

            meta_camps.append({
                "campaign_id": cid,
                "name": c.get("name", ""),
                "status": real_status,
                "configured_status": c.get("status", "UNKNOWN"),
                "budget_daily": raw_budget,
                "ad_count": ad_count,
                "ad_ids": ["x"] * ad_count,
                "objective": c.get("objective", ""),
                "created_at": int(time.mktime(time.strptime(c["created_time"][:19], "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S"))) if c.get("created_time") else 0,
                "source": "meta",
                "connected_to_bot": connected_to_bot,
                "whatsapp_number_id": whatsapp_number,
                "attribution_note": (
                    "ГўЕ“вЂ¦ Conectada al bot Гўв‚¬вЂќ ROAS medible" if connected_to_bot
                    else "ГўЕЎ ГЇВёВЏ Apunta a otro canal Гўв‚¬вЂќ ROAS no medible" if whatsapp_number
                    else "ГўВќвЂњ Canal desconocido Гўв‚¬вЂќ verifica configuraciГѓВіn"
                ),
            })
        if meta_camps:
            return response(200, {"campaigns": meta_camps})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error listando campanas de Meta: {e}", exc_info=True)
    return response(200, {"campaigns": local_camps})


# --- L18593-18620 (28 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_metrics(client_id):
    import urllib3 as _u3m
    _hm = _u3m.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(200, {"spend": 0, "impressions": 0, "clicks": 0, "ctr": 0, "cpc": 0, "leads": 0, "campaigns": []})
    try:
        res = _hm.request("GET",
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_account}/insights?fields=spend,impressions,clicks,ctr,cpc,actions&date_preset=last_30d&access_token={token}",
            timeout=10.0)
        if res.status == 200:
            data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [{}])[0] if json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data") else {}
            leads_count = 0
            for a in data.get("actions", []):
                if a.get("action_type") in ("lead", "onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d"):
                    leads_count += int(a.get("value", 0))
            return response(200, {
                "spend": float(data.get("spend", 0)),
                "impressions": int(data.get("impressions", 0)),
                "clicks": int(data.get("clicks", 0)),
                "ctr": float(data.get("ctr", 0)),
                "cpc": float(data.get("cpc", 0)),
                "leads": leads_count,
                "date_preset": "last_30d"
            })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error ads metrics: {e}")
    return response(200, {"spend": 0, "impressions": 0, "clicks": 0, "ctr": 0, "cpc": 0, "leads": 0})


# --- L18621-18683 (63 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_optimize(client_id):
    """POST /ads/optimize Гўв‚¬вЂќ IA analiza campanas y sugiere acciones."""
    import urllib3 as _u3o
    _ho = _u3o.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(400, {"error": error})
    config = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
    brand = config.get("brand_name", "Negocio")
    currency = config.get("currency", "COP")
    campaigns = config.get("ads_campaigns", [])
    if not campaigns:
        return response(200, {"recommendations": [], "message": "No hay campanas para analizar"})
    # Obtener metricas por campana
    campaign_data = []
    for camp in campaigns[-10:]:
        cid = camp.get("campaign_id", "")
        if not cid:
            continue
        try:
            res = _ho.request("GET",
                f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{cid}/insights?fields=spend,impressions,clicks,ctr,cpc,actions&date_preset=last_7d&access_token={token}",
                timeout=8.0)
            if res.status == 200:
                data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8")).get("data", [{}])
                metrics = data[0] if data else {}
                campaign_data.append({
                    "name": camp.get("name", ""),
                    "campaign_id": cid,
                    "status": camp.get("status", "PAUSED"),
                    "budget_daily": camp.get("budget_daily", 0),
                    "spend": float(metrics.get("spend", 0)),
                    "impressions": int(metrics.get("impressions", 0)),
                    "clicks": int(metrics.get("clicks", 0)),
                    "ctr": float(metrics.get("ctr", 0)),
                    "cpc": float(metrics.get("cpc", 0)),
                })
        except Exception:
            pass
    if not campaign_data:
        return response(200, {"recommendations": [], "message": "Sin datos de metricas aun"})
    # Gemini analiza y sugiere
    gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
    if not gemini_key:
        return response(200, {"recommendations": [], "message": "IA no disponible"})
    try:
        prompt = f"Analiza estas campanas de Facebook Ads de {brand} ({currency}) y da recomendaciones. Datos: {json.dumps(campaign_data)}. Responde JSON: {{\"recommendations\": [{{\"campaign_name\": \"\", \"action\": \"pause|scale|optimize|create_variation\", \"reason\": \"explicacion breve\", \"priority\": \"high|medium|low\"}}]}}"
        url = f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:generateContent?key={gemini_key}"
        res = _ho.request("POST", url,
            body=json.dumps({"contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": prompt}]}], "generationConfig": {"temperature": 0.3, "maxOutputTokens": 800, "responseMimeType": "application/json"}}),
            headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"}, timeout=10.0)
        if res.status == 200:
            data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
            result = json.loads(data["candidates"][0]["content"]["parts"][0]["text"])
            return response(200, {**result, "campaign_data": campaign_data})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error ads optimize: {e}")
    return response(200, {"recommendations": [], "campaign_data": campaign_data})

# BRAND DNA Гўв‚¬вЂќ Scraping multi-source + Gemini analysis

_BRAND_DNA_TTL_DAYS = int(os.environ.get("BRAND_DNA_TTL_DAYS", "90"))
_BRAND_DNA_COOLDOWN_DAYS = int(os.environ.get("BRAND_DNA_REGENERATE_COOLDOWN_DAYS", "15"))


# --- L18838-18968 (131 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def _analyze_brand_with_gemini(scraped_data: list, brand_name: str,
                                business_vertical: str = "") -> dict:
    """Llama a Gemini Flash Lite para analizar todo el contenido scrapeado
    y devolver el Brand DNA estructurado.
    """
    import urllib3 as _u3_bd
    import unicodedata
    
    gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
    if not gemini_key:
        return {"error": "GEMINI_API_KEY no configurada"}
    
    # Construir contexto de todas las fuentes
    own_content = []
    competitor_content = []
    for src in scraped_data:
        if not src.get("ok"):
            continue
        source = src.get("source", "")
        if source == "competitor":
            competitor_content.append(
                f"[Competidor {src.get('url', '')}]:\n"
                f"Title: {src.get('title', '')}\n"
                f"Text: {src.get('text', '')[:1500]}"
            )
        elif source == "website":
            own_content.append(
                f"[Website propio {src.get('url', '')}]:\n"
                f"Title: {src.get('title', '')}\n"
                f"Text: {src.get('text', '')[:2000]}"
            )
        elif source == "instagram":
            own_content.append(
                f"[Instagram {src.get('post_count', 0)} posts, "
                f"avg_likes={src.get('avg_likes', 0)}]:\n"
                f"{src.get('captions_concat', '')[:1500]}"
            )
        elif source == "facebook":
            own_content.append(
                f"[Facebook {src.get('post_count', 0)} posts, "
                f"avg_reactions={src.get('avg_reactions', 0)}]:\n"
                f"{src.get('messages_concat', '')[:1500]}"
            )
    
    own_text = "\n\n".join(own_content)
    competitor_text = "\n\n".join(competitor_content) if competitor_content else "No se proporciono."
    
    # Normalizar acentos (Leccion 18 Гўв‚¬вЂќ Gemini bug con UTF-8)
    own_text_norm = "".join(
        c for c in unicodedata.normalize("NFD", own_text)
        if unicodedata.category(c) != "Mn"
    )[:8000]
    comp_text_norm = "".join(
        c for c in unicodedata.normalize("NFD", competitor_text)
        if unicodedata.category(c) != "Mn"
    )[:5000]
    
    vertical_hint = f" (vertical: {business_vertical})" if business_vertical else ""
    
    prompt = (
        f"Eres un experto en branding y marketing digital. Analiza el contenido "
        f"de la marca '{brand_name}'{vertical_hint} y genera un ADN de marca "
        f"estructurado para usar en generacion de anuncios con IA.\n\n"
        f"=== CONTENIDO PROPIO DE LA MARCA ===\n{own_text_norm}\n\n"
        f"=== CONTENIDO DE COMPETIDORES (para diferenciacion) ===\n{comp_text_norm}\n\n"
        "Genera un ADN de marca con estos campos. Responde SOLO en JSON valido:\n"
        "{\n"
        '  "voice": "descripcion de la voz (ej: profesional, calida, autoritaria)",\n'
        '  "tone": "tono comunicativo (directo, formal, casual, etc)",\n'
        '  "target_audience": {\n'
        '    "demographics": "edad, genero, ubicacion, nivel socioeconomico",\n'
        '    "psychographics": "valores, intereses, estilo de vida",\n'
        '    "pain_points": ["dolor 1", "dolor 2", "dolor 3"]\n'
        "  },\n"
        '  "value_propositions": ["propuesta 1", "propuesta 2", "propuesta 3"],\n'
        '  "legal_social_proof": [\n'
        '    "Frase 1 con vague specificity (numeros grandes referenciando MERCADO no cliente)",\n'
        '    "Frase 2",\n'
        '    "Frase 3",\n'
        '    "Frase 4",\n'
        '    "Frase 5"\n'
        "  ],\n"
        '  "competitor_insights": ["insight 1 sobre que hace la competencia", "insight 2"],\n'
        '  "key_differentiators": ["en que somos UNICOS vs competencia"]\n'
        "}\n\n"
        "REGLA CRITICA del legal_social_proof: NUNCA inventar numeros sobre el cliente.\n"
        "MAL: 'He capacitado 500 alumnos' (mentira)\n"
        "BIEN: '+500 personas que aman su seguridad eligen capacitarse'\n"
        "BIEN: 'El 80% de quienes se forman en defensa personal recomendarian el curso'\n"
        "Usa numeros del MERCADO o tendencia, no del cliente individual."
    )
    
    payload = {
        "contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": prompt}]}],
        "generationConfig": {
            "temperature": 0.7,
            "maxOutputTokens": 1500,
            "responseMimeType": "application/json",
        },
    }
    
    # Cascada de modelos (Leccion 19)
    models = ["gemini-2.5-flash-lite", "gemini-flash-lite-latest"]
    last_err = ""
    for model in models:
        try:
            _hbd = _u3_bd.PoolManager()
            url = (
                f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/"
                f"models/{model}:generateContent?key={gemini_key}"
            )
            res = _hbd.request("POST", url,
                               body=json.dumps(payload),
                               headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"},
                               timeout=30.0)
            if res.status != 200:
                last_err = f"{model} status={res.status}"
                continue
            data = json.loads(res.data.decode("utf-8"))
            text = (data.get("candidates", [{}])[0]
                    .get("content", {}).get("parts", [{}])[0]
                    .get("text", "")).strip()
            if text.startswith("```"):
                text = text.split("\n", 1)[-1].rsplit("```", 1)[0].strip()
            parsed = json.loads(text)
            return {"ok": True, "dna": parsed, "model": model}
        except Exception as e:
            last_err = f"{model}: {str(e)[:200]}"
            continue
    
    return {"ok": False, "error": f"Gemini fallo: {last_err}"}


# --- L19298-19334 (37 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_video_upload_url(event, client_id):
    """GET /ads/video/upload-url?file_name=video.mp4
    Genera presigned URL S3 para que frontend suba video directo (Lambda no toca).
    Soporta MP4 y MOV (acepta hasta 500MB para Meta).
    """
    import time as _t
    import re as _re
    try:
        qs = event.get("queryStringParameters") or {}
        file_name = (qs.get("file_name") or "").strip()
        if not file_name:
            return response(400, {"error": "file_name requerido"})
        safe_name = _re.sub(r"[^a-zA-Z0-9_.-]", "_", file_name)[:120]
        ext = safe_name.rsplit(".", 1)[-1].lower() if "." in safe_name else "mp4"
        if ext not in ("mp4", "mov", "m4v"):
            return response(400, {"error": "Formato no soportado. Solo MP4 o MOV."})
        content_type = "video/mp4" if ext in ("mp4", "m4v") else "video/quicktime"
        key = f"brand-assets/{client_id}/video/{int(_t.time())}_{safe_name}"
        bucket = os.environ.get("S3_MEDIA_BUCKET", "clientes-bot-media")
        upload_url = s3_client.generate_presigned_url(
            "put_object",
            Params={"Bucket": bucket, "Key": key, "ContentType": content_type},
            ExpiresIn=3600,
        )
        region = os.environ.get("AWS_REGION", "us-east-1")
        public_url = f"https://{bucket}.s3.{region}.amazonaws.com/{key}"
        return response(200, {
            "upload_url": upload_url,
            "public_url": public_url,
            "key": key,
            "content_type": content_type,
            "expires_in": 3600,
            "max_size_mb": 500,
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/video/upload-url: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)[:200]})


# --- L19335-19414 (80 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_video_register(event, client_id):
    """POST /ads/video/register Гўв‚¬вЂќ Registra video subido en AdsCreativeGenerations.
    Frontend llama este endpoint despues de hacer PUT exitoso a la presigned URL.
    Persiste en la biblioteca multi-tenant + permite reutilizar el video en
    futuras campanas.
    Body: {
        "public_url": "https://.../brand-assets/{cid}/video/{ts}_{name}.mp4",
        "file_name": "mi-video.mp4",        # opcional, para mostrar en UI
        "duration_seconds": 30,             # opcional
        "size_bytes": 5242880,              # opcional
        "service_slug": "...",              # opcional, contexto
        "language": "es",
        "country": "CO"
    }
    """
    try:
        body = json.loads(event.get("body", "{}") or "{}")
        public_url = (body.get("public_url") or "").strip()
        if not public_url:
            return response(400, {"error": "public_url requerido"})
        # Validacion basica: la URL debe pertenecer al bucket del tenant
        bucket = os.environ.get("S3_MEDIA_BUCKET", "clientes-bot-media")
        expected_prefix = f"brand-assets/{client_id}/video/"
        if bucket not in public_url or expected_prefix not in public_url:
            return response(400, {"error": "URL no pertenece a tu cuenta"})
        file_name = (body.get("file_name") or "").strip()[:120]
        duration_seconds = int(body.get("duration_seconds") or 0)
        size_bytes = int(body.get("size_bytes") or 0)
        service_slug = (body.get("service_slug") or "").strip()
        language = (body.get("language") or "es").strip().lower()
        country = (body.get("country") or "").strip().upper()
        # business_vertical desde config_pro (multi-tenant)
        business_vertical = ""
        try:
            cfg_item = kb_table.get_item(
                Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"},
                ProjectionExpression="business_vertical",
            ).get("Item") or {}
            business_vertical = cfg_item.get("business_vertical", "")
        except Exception:
            pass
        prompt_used = (
            f"manual_upload | file={file_name} | "
            f"duration={duration_seconds}s | size={size_bytes}B"
        )[:5000]
        generation_id = persist_generation(
            client_id=client_id,
            asset_type="video",
            asset_subtype="manual_upload",
            prompt_used=prompt_used,
            refs_used=[],
            model="manual-upload",
            service_slug=service_slug,
            business_vertical=business_vertical,
            pattern_target="",
            language=language,
            country=country,
            s3_url=public_url,
        )
        if generation_id == "library_full":
            return response(200, {
                "ok": True,
                "registered": False,
                "library_full": True,
                "message": "Biblioteca llena Гўв‚¬вЂќ el video NO se guardo, pero puedes usarlo en tu campana",
                "public_url": public_url,
            })
        if not generation_id:
            return response(500, {"error": "No se pudo registrar el video"})
        logger.info(f"video_register OK: client={client_id} gen_id={generation_id} url={public_url[:80]}")
        return response(200, {
            "ok": True,
            "registered": True,
            "generation_id": generation_id,
            "public_url": public_url,
            "asset_type": "video",
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"handle_ads_video_register error: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)[:200]})
