# --- L20977-21006 (30 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_saved_audience_create(client_id, body):
    """POST /ads/saved-audiences - Guarda un publico."""
    name = body.get("name", "").strip()
    if not name:
        return response(400, {"error": "name es requerido"})
    try:
        cfg = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
        saved = cfg.get("saved_audiences", [])
        new_aud = {
            "id": f"AUD_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:10].upper()}",
            "name": name,
            "country": body.get("country", "CO"),
            "cities": body.get("cities", []),
            "interests": body.get("interests", []),
            "age_min": int(body.get("age_min", 18)),
            "age_max": int(body.get("age_max", 65)),
            "gender": body.get("gender", "all"),
            "created_at": int(time.time()),
        }
        saved.append(new_aud)
        saved = saved[:30]  # max 30 publicos guardados
        kb_table.update_item(
            Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"},
            UpdateExpression="SET saved_audiences = :s",
            ExpressionAttributeValues={":s": saved}
        )
        return response(201, {"message": "Publico guardado", "audience": new_aud})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error save audience: {e}")
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L21007-21022 (16 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_saved_audience_delete(client_id, audience_id):
    """DELETE /ads/saved-audiences - Elimina un publico guardado."""
    if not audience_id:
        return response(400, {"error": "id es requerido"})
    try:
        cfg = kb_table.get_item(Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}).get("Item", {})
        saved = [a for a in cfg.get("saved_audiences", []) if a.get("id") != audience_id]
        kb_table.update_item(
            Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"},
            UpdateExpression="SET saved_audiences = :s",
            ExpressionAttributeValues={":s": saved}
        )
        return response(200, {"message": "Publico eliminado"})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error delete audience: {e}")
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L21023-21060 (38 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_ad_preview(client_id, ad_id):
    """GET /ads/ad-preview?ad_id=X - Obtiene datos actuales del creative de un anuncio."""
    import urllib3 as _u3ap
    _hap = _u3ap.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(400, {"error": error})
    if not ad_id:
        return response(400, {"error": "ad_id requerido"})
    try:
        # Obtener creative del anuncio
        ar = _hap.request("GET",
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{ad_id}?fields=creative&access_token={token}",
            timeout=10.0)
        if ar.status != 200:
            return response(400, {"error": "No se pudo obtener el anuncio"})
        creative_id = json.loads(ar.data.decode("utf-8")).get("creative", {}).get("id", "")
        if not creative_id:
            return response(400, {"error": "Anuncio sin creative"})
        # Obtener datos del creative
        cr = _hap.request("GET",
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{creative_id}?fields=object_story_spec&access_token={token}",
            timeout=10.0)
        if cr.status != 200:
            return response(400, {"error": "No se pudo leer el creative"})
        oss = json.loads(cr.data.decode("utf-8")).get("object_story_spec", {})
        ld = oss.get("link_data", {})
        return response(200, {
            "headline": ld.get("name", ""),
            "text": ld.get("message", ""),
            "description": ld.get("description", ""),
            "image_url": ld.get("picture", ""),
            "link": ld.get("link", ""),
            "cta": (ld.get("call_to_action") or {}).get("type", ""),
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error ad preview: {e}")
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L21061-21322 (262 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_overlay_and_resize(event, client_id):
    """POST /ads/overlay-and-resize - Bug #71 v3: 3 formatos sin texto + Pillow overlay.
    Pipeline limpio:
      1. Gemini genera 3 formatos (1:1, 9:16, 16:9) SIN texto (mejor calidad imagen)
      2. Si include_overlay=true, Pillow incrusta texto profesional encima
         (auto-wrap, smart gradient, AI placement, fuente Inter Bold)
      3. Persiste cada formato en AdsCreativeGenerations con asset_subtype correcto
    Body: {
        "image_url": "https://...",
        "overlay_text": "Texto a incrustar (ilimitado)",
        "include_overlay": true,
        "text_position": "auto|top|bottom",       # default: auto (AI Placement)
        "text_bg_mode": "smart_gradient|black_gradient|brand_mode",
        "brand_color_hex": "",
        "service_slug": "",                        # contexto persistencia
        "language": "es",
        "country": "CO",
        "pattern_target": ""
    }
    """
    import urllib3 as _u3_ov
    import base64 as _b64_ov
    import uuid as _uuid_ov
    from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed
    try:
        body = json.loads(event.get("body", "{}") or "{}")
        image_url = (body.get("image_url") or "").strip()
        overlay_text = (body.get("overlay_text") or "").strip()
        include_overlay = body.get("include_overlay", True)
        text_position = (body.get("text_position") or "auto").strip().lower()
        text_bg_mode = (body.get("text_bg_mode") or "smart_gradient").strip().lower()
        brand_color_hex = (body.get("brand_color_hex") or "").strip()
        service_slug = (body.get("service_slug") or "").strip()
        language = (body.get("language") or "es").strip().lower()
        country = (body.get("country") or "CO").strip().upper()
        pattern_target = (body.get("pattern_target") or "").strip().lower()
        # Rich Overlay v2 Гўв‚¬вЂќ campos opcionales con auto-extraccion desde tenant
        price_chip = (body.get("price_chip") or "").strip()
        location_chip = (body.get("location_chip") or "").strip()
        urgency_sticker = (body.get("urgency_sticker") or "").strip()
        # Logo watermark OFF default (Gemini ya genera logos desde refs del uniforme)
        # Logo watermark ON por default Гўв‚¬вЂќ los helpers ya existen.
        # Gemini NO pinta logo en la imagen (rule en prompt), Pillow lo agrega aqui.
        show_logo_watermark = body.get("show_logo_watermark", True)
        if not image_url:
            return response(400, {"error": "image_url requerido"})
        gemini_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
        if not gemini_key:
            return response(400, {"error": "GEMINI_API_KEY no configurada"})
        # Cargar config del tenant + business_profile + servicio (auto-fill chips)
        cfg = {}
        try:
            cfg = kb_table.get_item(
                Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "config_pro"}
            ).get("Item", {}) or {}
        except Exception:
            pass
        business_vertical = cfg.get("business_vertical", "")
        bp = cfg.get("business_profile", {}) or {}
        # Toggles desde business_profile (default true)
        bp_show_price = bool(bp.get("ads_overlay_show_price", True))
        bp_show_location = bool(bp.get("ads_overlay_show_location", True))
        bp_show_urgency = bool(bp.get("ads_overlay_show_urgency", True))
        bp_show_logo = bool(bp.get("ads_overlay_show_logo_watermark", True))
        # Si toggle false ГўвЂ вЂ™ vaciar el chip aunque venga en body
        if not bp_show_price:
            price_chip = ""
        if not bp_show_location:
            location_chip = ""
        if not bp_show_urgency:
            urgency_sticker = ""
        if not bp_show_logo:
            show_logo_watermark = False
        # Auto-fill price_chip desde servicio si no llega del body
        if bp_show_price and not price_chip and service_slug:
            try:
                cat = kb_table.get_item(
                    Key={"company_id": client_id, "kb_key": "services_catalog"}
                ).get("Item", {}) or {}
                for s in (cat.get("services", []) or []):
                    if s.get("slug") == service_slug:
                        pricing = s.get("pricing", {}) or {}
                        reg = pricing.get("regular_price", 0)
                        cur = pricing.get("currency", cfg.get("currency", "COP"))
                        if reg:
                            reg_int = int(reg)
                            if reg_int >= 1000:
                                # Formato $280K para precios >= 1000
                                price_chip = f"${reg_int // 1000}K"
                            else:
                                price_chip = f"${reg_int} {cur}"
                        break
            except Exception:
                pass
        # Auto-fill location_chip desde address si no llega del body
        if bp_show_location and not location_chip:
            addr = cfg.get("address", "") or ""
            if addr:
                # Tomar solo la primera coma (ciudad) Гўв‚¬вЂќ "Guarne, Antioquia (a minutos...)" ГўвЂ вЂ™ "Guarne, Antioquia"
                parts = addr.split("(")[0].strip()
                location_chip = parts[:40]
        # Auto-fill urgency_sticker desde business_profile (random del pool)
        if bp_show_urgency and not urgency_sticker:
            pool = bp.get("urgency_phrases", []) or []
            if pool:
                import random as _rand
                urgency_sticker = str(_rand.choice(pool))[:30]
        # Pre-descargar logo una sola vez (no en cada formato)
        logo_bytes = b""
        if show_logo_watermark:
            logo_url = _select_best_logo_url(client_id)
            if logo_url:
                try:
                    import urllib3 as _u3_pre
                    _hpre = _u3_pre.PoolManager(timeout=8.0)
                    lr = _hpre.request("GET", logo_url, timeout=8.0)
                    if lr.status == 200:
                        logo_bytes = lr.data
                except Exception:
                    pass
        # Descargar imagen original
        _hov = _u3_ov.PoolManager(timeout=15.0)
        dl = _hov.request("GET", image_url, timeout=15.0)
        if dl.status != 200:
            return response(400, {"error": "No se pudo descargar la imagen"})
        img_b64 = _b64_ov.b64encode(dl.data).decode("utf-8")
        ct = dl.headers.get("Content-Type", "image/jpeg")
        formats = {
            "square": {"ratio": "1:1", "size": "1K"},
            "vertical": {"ratio": "9:16", "size": "1K"},
            "horizontal": {"ratio": "16:9", "size": "1K"},
        }
        bucket = os.environ.get("S3_MEDIA_BUCKET", "clientes-bot-media")
        region = os.environ.get("AWS_REGION", "us-east-1")
        model = os.environ.get("IMAGE_MODEL_FINAL", "gemini-3.1-flash-image-preview")
        def _gen_format(fmt_name, fmt_config):
            """Pillow crop centro + resize HD Гўв‚¬вЂќ sin IA, sin alucinaciones, $0 extra.
            Filosofia "es mas facil cortar que agregar": Gemini genera 1 imagen
            wide-angle 1024x1024 con sujeto centrado al 50%, luego recortamos:
              square (1:1)     -> 1024x1024 nativo (sin tocar)
              vertical (9:16)  -> crop centro 576x1024 -> resize 720x1280 HD
              horizontal (16:9) -> crop centro 1024x576 -> resize 1280x720 HD
            Scale 1.25x con LANCZOS es invisible al ojo en mobile.
            """
            try:
                from PIL import Image as _Img
                import io as _io_g
                master = _Img.open(_io_g.BytesIO(dl.data)).convert("RGB")
                if master.size != (1024, 1024):
                    s = min(master.size)
                    master = master.crop(((master.size[0]-s)//2, (master.size[1]-s)//2,
                                          (master.size[0]+s)//2, (master.size[1]+s)//2))
                    master = master.resize((1024, 1024), _Img.LANCZOS)
                # Dimensiones Meta MAX recomendadas (calidad maxima en mobile)
                if fmt_name == "square":
                    # 1024 -> 1080 (resize leve x1.055)
                    resized = master.resize((1080, 1080), _Img.LANCZOS)
                    buf = _io_g.BytesIO()
                    resized.save(buf, format="JPEG", quality=94)
                    raw_bytes = buf.getvalue()
                elif fmt_name == "vertical":
                    # Crop centro 576x1024 -> resize 1080x1920 (HD Stories/Reels)
                    left = (1024 - 576) // 2
                    cropped = master.crop((left, 0, left + 576, 1024))
                    resized = cropped.resize((1080, 1920), _Img.LANCZOS)
                    buf = _io_g.BytesIO()
                    resized.save(buf, format="JPEG", quality=94)
                    raw_bytes = buf.getvalue()
                elif fmt_name == "horizontal":
                    # Crop centro 1024x576 -> resize 1920x1080 (HD Feed/Landscape)
                    top = (1024 - 576) // 2
                    cropped = master.crop((0, top, 1024, top + 576))
                    resized = cropped.resize((1920, 1080), _Img.LANCZOS)
                    buf = _io_g.BytesIO()
                    resized.save(buf, format="JPEG", quality=94)
                    raw_bytes = buf.getvalue()
                else:
                    raw_bytes = dl.data
                # Aplicar overlay Pillow (texto + watermark logo)
                if include_overlay and overlay_text:
                    final_bytes = apply_text_overlay_pillow(
                        image_bytes=raw_bytes,
                        text=overlay_text,
                        position=text_position,
                        bg_mode=text_bg_mode,
                        brand_color_hex=brand_color_hex,
                        target_format=fmt_name,
                        gemini_key=gemini_key,
                        client_id=client_id,
                        price_chip=price_chip,
                        location_chip=location_chip,
                        urgency_sticker=urgency_sticker,
                        show_logo_watermark=show_logo_watermark,
                        logo_bytes=logo_bytes,
                    )
                else:
                    final_bytes = raw_bytes
                key = f"brand-assets/{client_id}/wizard-final/{_uuid_ov.uuid4().hex[:8]}_{fmt_name}.jpg"
                s3_client.put_object(
                    Bucket=bucket, Key=key,
                    Body=final_bytes,
                    ContentType="image/jpeg",
                    CacheControl="public, max-age=86400",
                )
                pub_url = f"https://{bucket}.s3.{region}.amazonaws.com/{key}"
                generation_id = persist_generation(
                    client_id=client_id,
                    asset_type="image",
                    asset_subtype=fmt_name,
                    prompt_used=("pillow_crop_resize_" + fmt_name +
                                " | text=" + (overlay_text or "")[:200]),
                    refs_used=[{"asset_id": "", "type": "source", "s3_url": image_url}],
                    model="pillow-crop-hd",
                    service_slug=service_slug,
                    business_vertical=business_vertical,
                    pattern_target=pattern_target,
                    language=language,
                    country=country,
                    s3_url=pub_url,
                )
                return fmt_name, pub_url, None
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error("_gen_format pillow-hd error: " + str(e), exc_info=True)
                return fmt_name, None, str(e)[:200]

        # Generar 3 formatos en paralelo
        results = {}
        errors = {}
        with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=3) as executor:
            futures = {
                executor.submit(_gen_format, fn, fc): fn
                for fn, fc in formats.items()
            }
            for future in as_completed(futures):
                fn, pub_url, err = future.result()
                if pub_url:
                    results[fn] = pub_url
                else:
                    errors[fn] = err
        logger.info(f"Overlay+resize v3: company={client_id} ok={len(results)} "
                    f"errors={len(errors)} overlay={include_overlay} "
                    f"text_len={len(overlay_text)} position={text_position}")
        return response(200, {
            "ok": len(results) > 0,
            "images": results,
            "square": results.get("square", ""),
            "vertical": results.get("vertical", ""),
            "horizontal": results.get("horizontal", ""),
            "overlay_applied": bool(include_overlay and overlay_text),
            "overlay_text": overlay_text if include_overlay else None,
            "text_position": text_position,
            "text_bg_mode": text_bg_mode,
            "price_chip": price_chip,
            "location_chip": location_chip,
            "urgency_sticker": urgency_sticker,
            "logo_watermark_applied": bool(show_logo_watermark and logo_bytes),
            "errors": errors if errors else None,
        })
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error /ads/overlay-and-resize: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)[:200]})



# --- L21323-21388 (66 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_resize_image(client_id, body):
    """POST /ads/resize-image - Recibe URL de imagen y genera 3 formatos (1:1, 9:16, 16:9)."""
    import urllib3 as _u3ri
    _hri = _u3ri.PoolManager()
    image_url = body.get("image_url", "").strip()
    if not image_url:
        return response(400, {"error": "image_url es requerido"})
    try:
        from PIL import Image
        import io
        import boto3 as _boto3
        # Descargar imagen original
        img_res = _hri.request("GET", image_url, timeout=15.0)
        if img_res.status != 200:
            return response(400, {"error": "No se pudo descargar la imagen"})
        img = Image.open(io.BytesIO(img_res.data))
        if img.mode != "RGB":
            img = img.convert("RGB")
        # Detectar color de fondo dominante (esquina superior izquierda)
        bg_color = img.getpixel((5, 5))
        formats = {
            "square": (1080, 1080),    # 1:1 Feed
            "vertical": (1080, 1920),  # 9:16 Stories/Reels
            "horizontal": (1200, 628), # 16:9 Landscape
        }
        s3 = _boto3.client("s3")
        bucket = "clientes-bot-media"
        results = {}
        for fmt_name, (tw, th) in formats.items():
            # Calcular escala para que la imagen quepa sin distorsion
            ow, oh = img.size
            scale = min(tw / ow, th / oh)
            nw, nh = int(ow * scale), int(oh * scale)
            resized = img.resize((nw, nh), Image.LANCZOS)
            # Crear canvas con color de fondo y pegar imagen centrada
            canvas = Image.new("RGB", (tw, th), bg_color)
            x = (tw - nw) // 2
            y = (th - nh) // 2
            canvas.paste(resized, (x, y))
            # Guardar en buffer
            buf = io.BytesIO()
            canvas.save(buf, format="JPEG", quality=90)
            buf.seek(0)
            # Subir a S3
            key = f"{client_id}/ads/{int(time.time())}_{fmt_name}.jpg"
            s3.put_object(
                Bucket=bucket,
                Key=key,
                Body=buf.getvalue(),
                ContentType="image/jpeg",
            )
            results[fmt_name] = f"https://{bucket}.s3.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/{key}"
        logger.info(f"Imagenes redimensionadas: {list(results.keys())}")
        return response(200, {
            "message": "Imagenes generadas en 3 formatos",
            "images": results,
            "square": results.get("square", ""),
            "vertical": results.get("vertical", ""),
            "horizontal": results.get("horizontal", ""),
        })
    except ImportError:
        logger.error("Pillow no disponible")
        return response(500, {"error": "Procesamiento de imagenes no disponible"})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error resize image: {e}")
        return response(500, {"error": str(e)})


# --- L21389-21594 (206 lГѓВ­neas) ---
def handle_ads_campaign_ads(client_id, campaign_id):
    """GET /ads/campaign-ads?campaign_id=X - Lista ads enriquecida con creative + metricas + razon rechazo.
    Vista enriquecida v2: incluye image_url, headline, text, description, metrics, disapproval_reason.
    Usa cache 15 min para no golpear Meta cada expansion.
    """
    import urllib3 as _u3ca
    _hca = _u3ca.PoolManager()
    ad_account, token, pixel, page_id, error = _get_ads_config(client_id)
    if error:
        return response(200, {"ads": [], "rejected_count": 0})
    if not campaign_id:
        return response(400, {"error": "campaign_id requerido"})
    try:
        # 1. Lista de ads con campos basicos + creative + issues + insights
        fields = (
            "id,name,effective_status,issues_info,"
            "creative{id,image_url,thumbnail_url,object_story_spec,asset_feed_spec,body,title},"
            "insights.date_preset(maximum){spend,impressions,clicks,ctr,actions,reach,frequency}"
        )
        ads_data = meta_cached_request(
            _hca,
            f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{campaign_id}/ads?fields={fields}&limit=100",
            token,
            f"camp_ads_v2_{campaign_id}",
            ttl=900
        )
        ads_raw = ads_data.get("data", [])
        rejected = 0
        ads_list = []
        for ad in ads_raw:
            st = ad.get("effective_status", "")
            if st in ("DISAPPROVED", "WITH_ISSUES"):
                rejected += 1
            # Razon del rechazo si aplica
            disapproval_reason = ""
            issues = ad.get("issues_info", []) or []
            if issues:
                disapproval_reason = issues[0].get("error_summary", "") or issues[0].get("error_message", "")
            # Creative: extraer imagen, titulo, texto
            creative = ad.get("creative", {}) or {}
            image_url = creative.get("image_url", "") or creative.get("thumbnail_url", "")
            headline = creative.get("title", "") or ""
            text = creative.get("body", "") or ""
            description = ""
            # Si viene en object_story_spec (caso normal de ads link/post)
            oss = creative.get("object_story_spec", {}) or {}
            link_data = oss.get("link_data", {}) or oss.get("video_data", {}) or {}
            if link_data:
                if not headline:
                    headline = link_data.get("name", "") or link_data.get("message", "")[:60]
                if not text:
                    text = link_data.get("message", "")
                if not description:
                    description = link_data.get("description", "")
                if not image_url:
                    image_url = link_data.get("picture", "") or link_data.get("image_url", "")
            # Si viene en asset_feed_spec (caso Advantage+ creative)
            afs = creative.get("asset_feed_spec", {}) or {}
            if afs:
                titles = afs.get("titles", []) or []
                bodies = afs.get("bodies", []) or []
                descs = afs.get("descriptions", []) or []
                images = afs.get("images", []) or []
                if not headline and titles:
                    headline = titles[0].get("text", "")
                if not text and bodies:
                    text = bodies[0].get("text", "")
                if not description and descs:
                    description = descs[0].get("text", "")
                if not image_url and images:
                    image_url = images[0].get("url", "") or images[0].get("permalink_url", "")
            # Metricas
            insights_arr = ad.get("insights", {}).get("data", []) if isinstance(ad.get("insights"), dict) else []
            ins = insights_arr[0] if insights_arr else {}
            spend = float(ins.get("spend", 0) or 0)
            impressions = int(ins.get("impressions", 0) or 0)
            clicks = int(ins.get("clicks", 0) or 0)
            ctr = round(float(ins.get("ctr", 0) or 0), 2)
            reach = int(ins.get("reach", 0) or 0)
            frequency = round(float(ins.get("frequency", 0) or 0), 2)
            # Leads desde acciones (onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d para CTW)
            leads = 0
            for action in (ins.get("actions", []) or []):
                at = action.get("action_type", "")
                if at in ("onsite_conversion.messaging_conversation_started_7d", "onsite_conversion.lead_grouped", "lead"):
                    leads += int(float(action.get("value", 0) or 0))
            cpl = round(spend / leads, 0) if leads else 0
            ads_list.append({
                "id": ad.get("id", ""),
                "name": ad.get("name", ""),
                "status": st,
                "image_url": image_url,
                "headline": headline[:100],
                "text": text[:300],
                "description": description[:100],
                "disapproval_reason": disapproval_reason,
                "metrics": {
                    "spend": spend,
                    "impressions": impressions,
                    "reach": reach,
                    "clicks": clicks,
                    "ctr": ctr,
                    "frequency": frequency,
                    "leads": leads,
                    "cpl": cpl,
                }
            })
        return response(200, {"ads": ads_list, "rejected_count": rejected, "total": len(ads_list)})
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error campaign ads enriched: {e}", exc_info=True)
        return response(200, {"ads": [], "rejected_count": 0})
